### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Análise Arquitetural

## 1. Análise da Arquitetura V12

### 1.1. Pontos Únicos de Falha (SPOF) Identificados

```javascript
// Arquivo: analysis/v12-spof-analysis.js
/**
 * Análise de Pontos Únicos de Falha da V12
 * Data: 2024-01-15
 * Status: Aceito
 */

const V12_SPOF_ANALYSIS = {
  // SPOF 1: Banco de Dados Centralizado
  database: {
    issue: "PostgreSQL single instance sem replicação",
    impact: "Falha do banco = sistema inoperante",
    detection: "Monitoramento ausente de health check do DB",
    mitigation: "Implementar replicação master-slave"
  },
  
  // SPOF 2: Serviço de Autenticação
  authService: {
    issue: "Serviço JWT central sem fallback",
    impact: "Usuários não conseguem autenticar",
    detection: "Latência > 2s ou status !== 200",
    mitigation: "Cache local de tokens válidos + auth service secundário"
  },
  
  // SPOF 3: Message Broker (RabbitMQ)
  messageBroker: {
    issue: "Cluster RabbitMQ não configurado",
    impact: "Comunicação entre serviços interrompida",
    detection: "Queue depth > 10k ou consumers offline",
    mitigation: "Cluster RabbitMQ + dead letter queues"
  },
  
  // SPOF 4: Serviço de Upload de Arquivos
  fileService: {
    issue: "Storage único (S3 bucket em uma região)",
    impact: "Upload/download de arquivos indisponível",
    detection: "Error rate > 5% ou latency > 5s",
    mitigation: "Multi-region storage + CDN"
  }
};

module.exports = V12_SPOF_ANALYSIS;
```

### 1.2. Gargalos de Performance

```javascript
// Arquivo: analysis/v12-performance-bottlenecks.js
/**
 * Identificação de Gargalos de Performance
 * Data: 2024-01-15
 */

const PERFORMANCE_BOTTLENECKS = {
  // Gargalo 1: API Gateway sem cache
  apiGateway: {
    metric: "95th percentile latency > 800ms",
    rootCause: "Validação JWT em cada request sem cache",
    solution: "Implementar cache de tokens válidos (Redis)"
  },
  
  // Gargalo 2: Queries N+1 no ORM
  databaseQueries: {
    metric: "Database connections > 80% pool",
    rootCause: "ORM gerando queries N+1 em relacionamentos",
    solution: "Eager loading otimizado + query monitoring"
  },
  
  // Gargalo 3: Serialização JSON pesada
  responseSerialization: {
    metric: "CPU > 70% durante picos",
    rootCause: "Serialização de objetos grandes sem paginação",
    solution: "Response pagination + selective field loading"
  },
  
  // Gargalo 4: Processamento síncrono de filas
  queueProcessing: {
    metric: "Queue backlog > 1000 mensagens",
    rootCause: "Processadores single-threaded",
    solution: "Worker pools + parallel processing"
  }
};

// Monitor de Performance em tempo real
class PerformanceMonitor {
  constructor() {
    this.metrics = new Map();
    this.thresholds = {
      latency: 500, // ms
      errorRate: 0.01, // 1%
      queueDepth: 1000,
      cpuUsage: 0.7 // 70%
    };
  }

  checkBottlenecks() {
    const bottlenecks = [];
    
    // Simulação de checagem
    const currentMetrics = {
      latency: 650,
      errorRate: 0.02,
      queueDepth: 1500,
      cpuUsage: 0.85
    };

    if (currentMetrics.latency > this.thresholds.latency) {
      bottlenecks.push({
        component: 'API Gateway',
        metric: 'latency',
        value: currentMetrics.latency,
        threshold: this.thresholds.latency
      });
    }

    return bottlenecks;
  }
}

module.exports = { PERFORMANCE_BOTTLENECKS, PerformanceMonitor };
```

## 2. ADR: Padrões de Resiliência para V13

```markdown
# Arquivo: adrs/ADR-001-resilience-patterns-v13.md

# ADR-001: Padrões de Resiliência para V13
Data: 2024-01-15
Status: Aceito
Autores: Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

## CONTEXTO:
A arquitetura V12 apresenta múltiplos pontos únicos de falha e falta de
padrões consistentes de resiliência. Incidentes recentes mostraram que
falhas em componentes individuais causam downtime total do sistema.
Necessitamos definir padrões arquiteturais que garantam 99.95% de disponibilidade.

## DECISÃO:
Implementar os seguintes padrões de resiliência em todos os serviços da V13:

1. **Circuit Breaker Pattern**: Para todas as chamadas entre serviços
2. **Retry com Backoff Exponencial**: Para falhas transitórias
3. **Fallback Strategies**: Respostas degradadas quando possível
4. **Bulkhead Pattern**: Isolamento de recursos por domínio
5. **Health Checks distribuídos**: Com auto-recovery

## OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:

### Opção A: Biblioteca específica (Resilience4j)
- **Prós**: 
  - Biblioteca madura e amplamente adotada
  - Integração nativa com Spring Boot
  - Métricas detalhadas out-of-the-box
- **Contras**:
  - Lock-in com ecossistema Java
  - Curva de aprendizado para times não-Java
  - Overhead em serviços leves

### Opção B: Implementação customizada com Polly (.NET Core)
- **Prós**:
  - Controle total sobre comportamento
  - Otimizado para nossa stack específica
  - Sem dependências externas
- **Contras**:
  - Custo de desenvolvimento e manutenção
  - Risco de bugs na implementação
  - Necessidade de documentação extensiva

### Opção C: Service Mesh (Istio com Linkerd)
- **Prós**:
  - Resiliência transparente no nível de rede
  - Sem mudanças no código dos serviços
  - Observabilidade unificada
- **Contras**:
  - Complexidade operacional aumentada
  - Custo computacional adicional
  - Curva de aprendizado íngreme

### Opção escolhida: A + Extensões Customizadas
**Justificativa**: Resilience4j oferece a base sólida que precisamos com
a maturidade de produção comprovada. Vamos estender com adaptadores para
nossos casos específicos e wrappers para serviços não-Java.

## CONSEQUÊNCIAS:

### Positivas:
1. Redução de 90% em cascading failures
2. Tempo de recuperação automática < 30s
3. Degradação graciosa em vez de falha total
4. Métricas padronizadas para SLOs

### Negativas:
1. Aumento de 15-20% na latência inicial
2. Complexidade aumentada no debugging
3. Necessidade de monitoramento adicional

### Riscos:
1. **Configuração incorreta**: Pode causar mais problemas que soluções
   - Mitigação: Templates pré-configurados + validação em CI/CD
2. **Overhead excessivo**: Impacto na performance
   - Mitigação: Feature flags + rollout gradual
3. **Dependência da biblioteca**: Breaking changes
   - Mitigação: Wrapper abstraction layer + version pinning

## REVISÃO:
Reavaliar em 6 meses (2024-07-15) com base em:
- Número de incidentes prevenidos
- Impacto na latência do sistema
- Complexidade operacional real
```

## 3. Implementação do Circuit Breaker

```javascript
// Arquivo: src/resilience/CircuitBreaker.js
/**
 * Implementação do Circuit Breaker Pattern
 * Baseado em Resilience4j com adaptações para Node.js
 */

class CircuitBreaker {
  constructor(config = {}) {
    this.config = {
      failureThreshold: config.failureThreshold || 5,
      resetTimeout: config.resetTimeout || 30000, // 30 segundos
      halfOpenMaxCalls: config.halfOpenMaxCalls || 2,
      ...config
    };
    
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.lastFailureTime = null;
    this.halfOpenSuccessCount = 0;
    
    // Métricas
    this.metrics = {
      totalCalls: 0,
      failedCalls: 0,
      successfulCalls: 0,
      circuitOpened: 0,
      stateChanges: []
    };
  }

  async execute(operation, fallback = null) {
    this.metrics.totalCalls++;
    
    // Estado OPEN: rejeita imediatamente
    if (this.state === 'OPEN') {
      if (this.shouldTryReset()) {
        this.transitionTo('HALF_OPEN');
      } else {
        this.metrics.failedCalls++;
        return this.executeFallback(fallback, 'Circuit breaker OPEN');
      }
    }
    
    try {
      const result = await operation();
      
      // Sucesso em HALF_OPEN
      if (this.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
        this.halfOpenSuccessCount++;
        if (this.halfOpenSuccessCount >= this.config.halfOpenMaxCalls) {
          this.transitionTo('CLOSED');
        }
      }
      
      // Sucesso em CLOSED - reset contador
      if (this.state === 'CLOSED') {
        this.failureCount = 0;
      }
      
      this.metrics.successfulCalls++;
      return result;
      
    } catch (error) {
      this.metrics.failedCalls++;
      
      // Incrementa falhas
      if (this.state === 'CLOSED' || this.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
        this.failureCount++;
        this.lastFailureTime = Date.now();
        
        // Transição para OPEN se threshold excedido
        if (this.failureCount >= this.config.failureThreshold) {
          this.transitionTo('OPEN');
        }
        
        // HALF_OPEN falhou - volta para OPEN
        if (this.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
          this.transitionTo('OPEN');
        }
      }
      
      return this.executeFallback(fallback, error);
    }
  }

  transitionTo(newState) {
    const oldState = this.state;
    this.state = newState;
    
    // Reset contadores
    if (newState === 'CLOSED') {
      this.failureCount = 0;
      this.halfOpenSuccessCount = 0;
    } else if (newState === 'OPEN') {
      this.metrics.circuitOpened++;
    }
    
    this.metrics.stateChanges.push({
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      from: oldState,
      to: newState
    });
    
    // Log da transição
    console.log(`CircuitBreaker: ${oldState} → ${newState}`);
  }

  shouldTryReset() {
    if (!this.lastFailureTime) return false;
    const timeSinceFailure = Date.now() - this.lastFailureTime;
    return timeSinceFailure >= this.config.resetTimeout;
  }

  executeFallback(fallback, error) {
    if (typeof fallback === 'function') {
      try {
        return fallback(error);
      } catch (fallbackError) {
        console.error('Fallback also failed:', fallbackError);
        throw new Error(`Original: ${error.message}, Fallback: ${fallbackError.message}`);
      }
    }
    
    // Fallback padrão
    return {
      status: 'degraded',
      data: null,
      error: 'Service temporarily unavailable',
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      circuitState: this.state
    };
  }

  getMetrics() {
    return {
      ...this.metrics,
      currentState: this.state,
      failureCount: this.failureCount,
      health: this.getHealthStatus()
    };
  }

  getHealthStatus() {
    const successRate = this.metrics.totalCalls > 0 
      ? this.metrics.successfulCalls / this.metrics.totalCalls 
      : 1;
    
    if (successRate > 0.95) return 'HEALTHY';
    if (successRate > 0.80) return 'DEGRADED';
    return 'UNHEALTHY';
  }
}

// Factory para circuit breakers por serviço
class CircuitBreakerRegistry {
  constructor() {
    this.breakers = new Map();
    this.defaultConfig = {
      failureThreshold: 5,
      resetTimeout: 30000,
      halfOpenMaxCalls: 2
    };
  }

  getOrCreate(serviceName, config = {}) {
    if (!this.breakers.has(serviceName)) {
      const breakerConfig = { ...this.defaultConfig, ...config };
      this.breakers.set(serviceName, new CircuitBreaker(breakerConfig));
    }
    return this.breakers.get(serviceName);
  }

  getGlobalMetrics() {
    const metrics = {
      totalBreakers: this.breakers.size,
      openBreakers: 0,
      healthyServices: 0,
      services: []
    };

    for (const [name, breaker] of this.breakers) {
      const breakerMetrics = breaker.getMetrics();
      metrics.services.push({
        name,
        ...breakerMetrics
      });

      if (breaker.state === 'OPEN') metrics.openBreakers++;
      if (breaker.getHealthStatus() === 'HEALTHY') metrics.healthyServices++;
    }

    return metrics;
  }
}

module.exports = { CircuitBreaker, CircuitBreakerRegistry };
```

## 4. Implementação de Retry com Backoff Exponencial

```javascript
// Arquivo: src/resilience/RetryStrategy.js
/**
 * Estratégia de Retry com Backoff Exponencial e Jitter
 */

class RetryStrategy {
  constructor(config = {}) {
    this.config = {
      maxAttempts: config.maxAttempts || 3,
      baseDelay: config.baseDelay || 100, // ms
      maxDelay: config.maxDelay || 10000, // ms
      jitter: config.jitter !== false, // default true
      retryableErrors: config.retryableErrors || [
        'ECONNRESET', 'ETIMEDOUT', 'ENOTFOUND'
      ],
      ...config
    };
    
    this.metrics = {
      totalRetries: 0,
      successfulRetries: 0,
      failedRetries: 0,
      totalDelayApplied: 0
    };
  }

  async execute(operation, shouldRetry = null) {
    let lastError;
    const startTime = Date.now();
    
    for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= this.config.maxAttempts; attempt++) {
      try {
        const result = await operation();
        
        if (attempt > 1) {
          this.metrics.successfulRetries++;
        }
        
        return {
          result,
          attempts: attempt,
          success: true,
          duration: Date.now() - startTime
        };
        
      } catch (error) {
        lastError = error;
        
        // Verifica se deve retry
        const canRetry = this.shouldRetry(error, attempt, shouldRetry);
        
        if (!canRetry || attempt === this.config.maxAttempts) {
          if (attempt > 1) {
            this.metrics.failedRetries++;
          }
          
          throw {
            error,
            attempts: attempt,
            success: false,
            duration: Date.now() - startTime,
            finalAttempt: true
          };
        }
        
        // Calcula delay com backoff exponencial
        const delay = this.calculateDelay(attempt);
        this.metrics.totalDelayApplied += delay;
        this.metrics.totalRetries++;
        
        // Aguarda antes do próximo retry
        await this.delay(delay);
        
        console.log(`Retry attempt ${attempt + 1}/${this.config.maxAttempts} after ${delay}ms`);
      }
    }
  }

  shouldRetry(error, attempt, customShouldRetry) {
    // Custom logic tem prioridade
    if (typeof customShouldRetry === 'function') {
      return customShouldRetry(error, attempt);
    }
    
    // Verifica se é erro retryable
    const isRetryableError = this.config.retryableErrors.some(
      errorCode => error.code === errorCode || error.message.includes(errorCode)
    );
    
    // Não retry para 4xx (exceto 429 - Too Many Requests)
    const isClientError = error.statusCode >= 400 && error.statusCode < 500;
    const isRateLimit = error.statusCode === 429;
    
    return isRetryableError || (isClientError && isRateLimit);
  }

  calculateDelay(attempt) {
    // Backoff exponencial: baseDelay * 2^(attempt-1)
    let delay = this.config.baseDelay * Math.pow(2, attempt - 1);
    
    // Adiciona jitter (variação aleatória)
    if (this.config.jitter) {
      const jitter = delay * 0.1; // 10% de jitter
      delay += Math.random() * jitter;
    }
    
    // Limita ao máximo configurado
    return Math.min(delay, this.config.maxDelay);
  }

  delay(ms) {
    return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
  }

  getMetrics() {
    const successRate = this.metrics.totalRetries > 0
      ? this.metrics.successfulRetries / this.metrics.totalRetries
      : 0;
    
    return {
      ...this.metrics,
      successRate: Math.round(successRate * 100) / 100,
      averageDelay: this.metrics.totalRetries > 0
        ? this.metrics.totalDelayApplied /

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# src/services/__init__.py
"""
Serviços da aplicação DIYAPP Evolution V13 Core
Implementa padrões de resiliência: circuit breakers, retry, timeout, fallback
"""

import json
import time
import logging
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Callable
from functools import wraps
import uuid

# Para circuit breaker
from circuitbreaker import circuit

# Para métricas
from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram, Gauge, generate_latest

# Para health checks
import psutil
import requests

# Configuração de logging estruturado
class StructuredLogger:
    """Logger estruturado em JSON com correlation ID"""
    
    def __init__(self, name: str = "diyapp"):
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(name)
        self.logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
        
        # Handler para console (em produção seria para ELK/CloudWatch)
        handler = logging.StreamHandler()
        handler.setFormatter(JsonFormatter())
        self.logger.addHandler(handler)
        
    def info(self, message: str, **kwargs):
        """Log info com dados estruturados"""
        self.logger.info(message, extra=kwargs)
    
    def error(self, message: str, **kwargs):
        """Log error com dados estruturados"""
        self.logger.error(message, extra=kwargs)
    
    def warning(self, message: str, **kwargs):
        """Log warning com dados estruturados"""
        self.logger.warning(message, extra=kwargs)
    
    def debug(self, message: str, **kwargs):
        """Log debug com dados estruturados"""
        self.logger.debug(message, extra=kwargs)

class JsonFormatter(logging.Formatter):
    """Formatter para logs em JSON"""
    
    def format(self, record):
        log_data = {
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
            "level": record.levelname,
            "logger": record.name,
            "message": record.getMessage(),
            "correlation_id": getattr(record, 'correlation_id', 'N/A'),
            "user_id": getattr(record, 'user_id', 'N/A'),
            "endpoint": getattr(record, 'endpoint', 'N/A'),
            "duration_ms": getattr(record, 'duration_ms', 0),
            "status": getattr(record, 'status', 'N/A'),
            "service": "diyapp-backend",
            "environment": "production"
        }
        
        # Adiciona campos extras
        for key, value in record.__dict__.items():
            if key not in ['args', 'asctime', 'created', 'exc_info', 'exc_text', 
                          'filename', 'funcName', 'levelname', 'levelno', 'lineno', 
                          'module', 'msecs', 'message', 'msg', 'name', 'pathname', 
                          'process', 'processName', 'relativeCreated', 'stack_info', 
                          'thread', 'threadName'] and not key.startswith('_'):
                if key not in log_data:
                    log_data[key] = value
        
        # Mascara dados sensíveis
        self._mask_sensitive_data(log_data)
        
        return json.dumps(log_data)
    
    def _mask_sensitive_data(self, log_data: Dict):
        """Mascara dados sensíveis nos logs"""
        sensitive_fields = ['email', 'cpf', 'password', 'token', 'credit_card', 'api_key']
        
        for field in sensitive_fields:
            if field in log_data and log_data[field]:
                log_data[field] = '***MASKED***'

# Instância global do logger
logger = StructuredLogger()

# Métricas Prometheus
REQUEST_LATENCY = Histogram(
    'http_request_duration_seconds',
    'HTTP request latency in seconds',
    ['method', 'endpoint', 'status']
)

REQUEST_COUNT = Counter(
    'http_requests_total',
    'Total HTTP requests',
    ['method', 'endpoint', 'status']
)

BUSINESS_TRANSACTIONS = Counter(
    'business_transactions_completed',
    'Business transactions completed',
    ['transaction_type', 'status']
)

EXTERNAL_CALLS = Counter(
    'external_service_calls_total',
    'Total external service calls',
    ['service', 'status']
)

EXTERNAL_CALL_LATENCY = Histogram(
    'external_service_call_duration_seconds',
    'External service call latency',
    ['service']
)

CIRCUIT_BREAKER_STATE = Gauge(
    'circuit_breaker_state',
    'Circuit breaker state (0=closed, 1=open, 2=half-open)',
    ['service']
)

SYSTEM_HEALTH = Gauge(
    'system_health_status',
    'System health status (1=healthy, 0=unhealthy)',
    ['component']
)

# Decorator para instrumentação de endpoints
def instrument_endpoint(method: str, endpoint: str):
    """Decorator para instrumentar endpoints com métricas e logging"""
    def decorator(func):
        @wraps(func)
        def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            correlation_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
            start_time = time.time()
            status = '200'
            
            try:
                # Extrai user_id se disponível
                user_id = kwargs.get('user_id') or (args[0].user_id if hasattr(args[0], 'user_id') else 'N/A')
                
                # Executa a função
                result = func(*args, **kwargs)
                
                # Calcula duração
                duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                
                # Log de sucesso
                logger.info(
                    f"Endpoint {method} {endpoint} completed",
                    correlation_id=correlation_id,
                    user_id=user_id,
                    endpoint=f"{method} {endpoint}",
                    duration_ms=duration_ms,
                    status=status
                )
                
                # Atualiza métricas
                REQUEST_COUNT.labels(method=method, endpoint=endpoint, status=status).inc()
                REQUEST_LATENCY.labels(method=method, endpoint=endpoint, status=status).observe(
                    duration_ms / 1000
                )
                
                return result
                
            except Exception as e:
                duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                status = '500' if not hasattr(e, 'status_code') else str(e.status_code)
                
                # Log de erro (sem stack trace no log estruturado)
                logger.error(
                    f"Endpoint {method} {endpoint} failed: {str(e)}",
                    correlation_id=correlation_id,
                    user_id=kwargs.get('user_id', 'N/A'),
                    endpoint=f"{method} {endpoint}",
                    duration_ms=duration_ms,
                    status=status,
                    error_type=type(e).__name__
                )
                
                # Atualiza métricas
                REQUEST_COUNT.labels(method=method, endpoint=endpoint, status=status).inc()
                REQUEST_LATENCY.labels(method=method, endpoint=endpoint, status=status).observe(
                    duration_ms / 1000
                )
                
                # Re-lança a exceção (será tratada no handler global)
                raise
        
        return wrapper
    return decorator

# Service base com resiliência
class ResilientService:
    """Classe base para serviços com resiliência embutida"""
    
    def __init__(self, service_name: str):
        self.service_name = service_name
        self.circuit_breaker_failure_threshold = 5
        self.circuit_breaker_recovery_timeout = 30
        self.expected_exceptions = (requests.exceptions.Timeout, 
                                   requests.exceptions.ConnectionError)
    
    def _external_call(self, func: Callable, *args, **kwargs) -> Any:
        """Wrapper para chamadas externas com resiliência"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        try:
            # Configura timeout explícito
            timeout = kwargs.pop('timeout', 10)
            if hasattr(func, '__self__') and hasattr(func.__self__, 'timeout'):
                func.__self__.timeout = timeout
            
            # Executa com circuit breaker
            @circuit(
                failure_threshold=self.circuit_breaker_failure_threshold,
                recovery_timeout=self.circuit_breaker_recovery_timeout,
                expected_exception=self.expected_exceptions
            )
            def protected_call():
                return func(*args, **kwargs)
            
            result = protected_call()
            duration = time.time() - start_time
            
            # Atualiza métricas
            EXTERNAL_CALLS.labels(service=self.service_name, status='success').inc()
            EXTERNAL_CALL_LATENCY.labels(service=self.service_name).observe(duration)
            CIRCUIT_BREAKER_STATE.labels(service=self.service_name).set(0)  # Closed
            
            return result
            
        except Exception as e:
            duration = time.time() - start_time
            
            # Atualiza métricas
            EXTERNAL_CALLS.labels(service=self.service_name, status='error').inc()
            EXTERNAL_CALL_LATENCY.labels(service=self.service_name).observe(duration)
            
            # Log do erro
            logger.error(
                f"External service {self.service_name} call failed",
                service=self.service_name,
                error=str(e),
                error_type=type(e).__name__,
                duration_seconds=duration
            )
            
            # Circuit breaker aberto?
            if isinstance(e, self.expected_exceptions):
                CIRCUIT_BREAKER_STATE.labels(service=self.service_name).set(1)  # Open
            
            # Fallback gracioso
            return self._fallback(e, *args, **kwargs)
    
    def _fallback(self, error: Exception, *args, **kwargs) -> Any:
        """Implementação de fallback - deve ser sobrescrita por serviços específicos"""
        raise error  # Por padrão, propaga o erro
    
    def _retry_with_backoff(self, func: Callable, max_retries: int = 3, 
                           base_delay: float = 1.0, *args, **kwargs) -> Any:
        """Retry com backoff exponencial e jitter"""
        import random
        
        last_exception = None
        
        for attempt in range(max_retries + 1):
            try:
                if attempt > 0:
                    # Backoff exponencial com jitter
                    delay = base_delay * (2 ** (attempt - 1))
                    jitter = random.uniform(0, delay * 0.1)
                    time.sleep(delay + jitter)
                    
                    logger.info(
                        f"Retry attempt {attempt} for {self.service_name}",
                        attempt=attempt,
                        delay=delay + jitter
                    )
                
                return func(*args, **kwargs)
                
            except self.expected_exceptions as e:
                last_exception = e
                if attempt == max_retries:
                    break
        
        # Se todas as tentativas falharem
        if last_exception:
            raise last_exception

# Health Check Service
class HealthCheckService(ResilientService):
    """Serviço de health checks detalhados"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__("health_check")
        self.checks = []
        self._register_default_checks()
    
    def _register_default_checks(self):
        """Registra checks padrão do sistema"""
        self.register_check("database", self._check_database)
        self.register_check("redis", self._check_redis)
        self.register_check("external_api", self._check_external_api)
        self.register_check("disk_space", self._check_disk_space)
        self.register_check("memory", self._check_memory)
    
    def register_check(self, name: str, check_func: Callable):
        """Registra um novo health check"""
        self.checks.append({
            "name": name,
            "check": check_func
        })
    
    @instrument_endpoint("GET", "/health")
    def get_health_status(self, detailed: bool = False) -> Dict:
        """Retorna status de saúde do sistema"""
        overall_healthy = True
        checks_results = []
        
        for check in self.checks:
            start_time = time.time()
            try:
                result = check["check"]()
                duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                
                checks_results.append({
                    "name": check["name"],
                    "status": "healthy",
                    "duration_ms": round(duration_ms, 2),
                    "details": result if detailed else None
                })
                
                # Atualiza métrica
                SYSTEM_HEALTH.labels(component=check["name"]).set(1)
                
            except Exception as e:
                duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                overall_healthy = False
                
                checks_results.append({
                    "name": check["name"],
                    "status": "unhealthy",
                    "duration_ms": round(duration_ms, 2),
                    "error": str(e),
                    "details": {"error": str(e)} if detailed else None
                })
                
                # Atualiza métrica
                SYSTEM_HEALTH.labels(component=check["name"]).set(0)
                
                logger.error(
                    f"Health check failed for {check['name']}",
                    check_name=check["name"],
                    error=str(e)
                )
        
        response = {
            "status": "healthy" if overall_healthy else "unhealthy",
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
            "service": "diyapp-backend",
            "version": "v13",
            "checks": checks_results
        }
        
        if not overall_healthy:
            response["unhealthy_components"] = [
                check["name"] for check in checks_results 
                if check["status"] == "unhealthy"
            ]
        
        return response
    
    def _check_database(self) -> Dict:
        """Check de conexão com banco de dados"""
        # Implementação real dependeria do ORM/Driver
        # Esta é uma implementação de exemplo
        import sqlite3
        
        try:
            # Para exemplo, usamos SQLite em memória
            conn = sqlite3.connect(':memory:')
            cursor = conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute('SELECT 1')
            result = cursor.fetchone()
            conn.close()
            
            return {
                "connected": True,
                "latency_ms": 1,  # Simulado
                "active_connections": 5  # Simulado
            }
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"Database connection failed: {str(e)}")
    
    def _check_redis(self) -> Dict:
        """Check de conexão com Redis"""
        # Implementação de exemplo
        try:
            # Simula check do Redis
            time.sleep(0.01)  # Simula latência
            
            return {
                "connected": True,
                "memory_used_mb": 128,  # Simulado
                "keys_count": 1000  # Simulado
            }
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"Redis connection failed: {str(e)}")
    
    def _check_external_api(self) -> Dict:
        """Check de conexão com API externa"""
        try:
            # Exemplo: check de uma API externa
            response = requests.get(
                'https://httpbin.org/status/200',
                timeout=5
            )
            response.raise_for_status()
            
            return {
                "reachable": True,
                "status_code": response.status_code,
                "response_time_ms": response.elapsed.total_seconds() * 1000
            }
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"External API unreachable: {str(e)}")
    
    def _check_disk_space(self) -> Dict:
        """Check de espaço em disco"""
        try:
            disk_usage = psutil.disk_usage('/')
            
            return {
                "total_gb": round(disk_usage.total / (1024**3), 2),
                "used_gb": round(disk_usage.used / (1024**3), 2),
                "free_gb": round(disk_usage.free / (1024**3), 2),
                "percent_used": disk_usage.percent
            }
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"Disk space check failed: {str(e)}")
    
    def _check_memory(self) -> Dict:
        """Check de uso de memória"""
        try:
            memory = psutil.virtual_memory()
            
            return {
                "total_gb": round(memory.total / (1024**3), 2),
                "available_gb": round(memory.available / (1024**3), 2),
                "percent_used": memory.percent,
                "swap_used_percent": psutil.swap_memory().percent
            }
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"Memory check failed: {str(e)}")

# Business Service com métricas de transações
class TransactionService(ResilientService):
    """Serviço de transações de negócio com métricas"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__("transaction_service")
    
    @instrument_endpoint("POST", "/transactions")
    def create_transaction(self, transaction_data: Dict, user_id: str) -> Dict:
        """Cria uma nova transação com métricas de negócio"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        try:
            # Validação de input (simplificada)
            if not transaction_data.get('amount') or transaction_data['amount'] <= 0:
                raise ValueError("Invalid transaction amount")
            
            if not transaction_data.get('type'):
                raise ValueError("Transaction type is required")
            
            # Simula processamento
            time.sleep(0.05)  # 50ms de processamento
            
            # Gera ID da transação
            transaction_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
            
            # Registra métrica de negócio
            BUSINESS_TRANSACTIONS.labels(
                transaction_type=transaction_data['type'],
                status='completed'
            ).inc()
            
            duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
            
            logger.info(
                "Transaction completed successfully",
                transaction_id=transaction_id,
                user_id=user_id,
                transaction_type=transaction_data['type'],
                amount=transaction_data['amount

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Sistema de Design

Vou implementar o novo sistema de design V13 com componentes React, focando em performance, acessibilidade e fidelidade ao design. Vou criar um sistema completo com tokens de design, componentes reutilizáveis, skeleton screens, transições suaves e tratamento de erros granulares.

```typescript
// ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO:
/*

├── design-system/
│   ├── tokens/

│   │   ├── spacing.ts

│   │   ├── shadows.ts
│   │   └── index.ts

│   │   └── index.ts

│       ├── performance-monitor.ts
│       └── index.ts

// 1. TOKENS DO DESIGN SYSTEM (src/design-system/tokens/)
// colors.ts
export const colors = {
  // Primary
  primary: {
    50: '#f0f9ff',
    100: '#e0f2fe',
    200: '#bae6fd',
    300: '#7dd3fc',
    400: '#38bdf8',
    500: '#0ea5e9',
    600: '#0284c7',
    700: '#0369a1',
    800: '#075985',
    900: '#0c4a6e',
  },
  
  // Neutral
  neutral: {
    50: '#fafafa',
    100: '#f5f5f5',
    200: '#e5e5e5',
    300: '#d4d4d4',
    400: '#a3a3a3',
    500: '#737373',
    600: '#525252',
    700: '#404040',
    800: '#262626',
    900: '#171717',
  },
  
  // Semantic
  success: {
    50: '#f0fdf4',
    500: '#10b981',
    700: '#047857',
  },
  warning: {
    50: '#fffbeb',
    500: '#f59e0b',
    700: '#b45309',
  },
  error: {
    50: '#fef2f2',
    500: '#ef4444',
    700: '#b91c1c',
  },
  
  // Background
  background: {
    light: '#ffffff',
    dark: '#0f172a',
  },
  
  // Text
  text: {
    primary: '#1e293b',
    secondary: '#64748b',
    disabled: '#94a3b8',
    inverse: '#ffffff',
  },
} as const;

// 2. COMPONENTES REACT (src/design-system/components/)

// Button.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { colors, spacing, typography, shadows } from '../tokens';

interface ButtonProps extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost';
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
}

export const Button: React.FC<ButtonProps> = ({
  children,
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  isLoading = false,
  leftIcon,
  rightIcon,
  disabled,
  className = '',
  ...props
}) => {
  const baseStyles = `
    inline-flex items-center justify-center
    font-medium rounded-lg
    transition-all duration-200 ease-in-out
    focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2
    disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed
    ${className}
  `;

  const variants = {
    primary: `
      bg-${colors.primary[600]}
      text-white
      hover:bg-${colors.primary[700]}
      focus:ring-${colors.primary[500]}
      active:bg-${colors.primary[800]}
    `,
    secondary: `
      bg-${colors.neutral[200]}
      text-${colors.neutral[800]}
      hover:bg-${colors.neutral[300]}
      focus:ring-${colors.neutral[400]}
      active:bg-${colors.neutral[400]}
    `,
    outline: `
      border border-${colors.neutral[300]}
      bg-transparent
      text-${colors.neutral[700]}
      hover:bg-${colors.neutral[50]}
      focus:ring-${colors.neutral[400]}
      active:bg-${colors.neutral[100]}
    `,
    ghost: `
      bg-transparent
      text-${colors.neutral[700]}
      hover:bg-${colors.neutral[100]}
      focus:ring-${colors.neutral[400]}
      active:bg-${colors.neutral[200]}
    `,
  };

  const sizes = {
    sm: `h-8 px-3 text-sm`,
    md: `h-10 px-4 text-base`,
    lg: `h-12 px-6 text-lg`,
  };

  return (
    <button
      className={`
        ${baseStyles}
        ${variants[variant]}
        ${sizes[size]}
        ${isLoading ? 'cursor-wait' : ''}
      `}
      disabled={disabled || isLoading}
      aria-busy={isLoading}
      {...props}
    >
      {isLoading && (
        <svg
          className="animate-spin -ml-1 mr-2 h-4 w-4"
          xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
          fill="none"
          viewBox="0 0 24 24"
        >
          <circle
            className="opacity-25"
            cx="12"
            cy="12"
            r="10"
            stroke="currentColor"
            strokeWidth="4"
          />
          <path
            className="opacity-75"
            fill="currentColor"
            d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
          />
        </svg>
      )}
      {!isLoading && leftIcon && <span className="mr-2">{leftIcon}</span>}
      {children}
      {!isLoading && rightIcon && <span className="ml-2">{rightIcon}</span>}
    </button>
  );
};

// Skeleton.tsx - Componente para skeleton screens
interface SkeletonProps {
  width?: string;
  height?: string;
  borderRadius?: string;
  className?: string;
}

export const Skeleton: React.FC<SkeletonProps> = ({
  width = '100%',
  height = '1rem',
  borderRadius = '0.375rem',
  className = '',
}) => {
  return (
    <div
      className={`animate-pulse bg-${colors.neutral[200]} ${className}`}
      style={{
        width,
        height,
        borderRadius,
      }}
      aria-label="Loading content"
      role="status"
    />
  );
};

// SkeletonCard.tsx - Skeleton composto para cards
export const SkeletonCard: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <div className="p-4 border border-neutral-200 rounded-lg">
      <div className="flex items-start space-x-4">
        <Skeleton width="3rem" height="3rem" borderRadius="9999px" />
        <div className="flex-1 space-y-3">
          <Skeleton width="60%" height="1.25rem" />
          <Skeleton width="40%" height="1rem" />
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <Skeleton width="100%" height="0.75rem" />
            <Skeleton width="90%" height="0.75rem" />
            <Skeleton width="80%" height="0.75rem" />
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// Alert.tsx - Componente de alerta com tratamento de erros granular
type AlertVariant = 'success' | 'warning' | 'error' | 'info';

interface AlertProps {
  variant: AlertVariant;
  title?: string;
  message: string;
  onClose?: () => void;
  showIcon?: boolean;
  className?: string;
}

export const Alert: React.FC<AlertProps> = ({
  variant,
  title,
  message,
  onClose,
  showIcon = true,
  className = '',
}) => {
  const variantStyles = {
    success: `bg-${colors.success[50]} border-${colors.success[500]} text-${colors.success[700]}`,
    warning: `bg-${colors.warning[50]} border-${colors.warning[500]} text-${colors.warning[700]}`,
    error: `bg-${colors.error[50]} border-${colors.error[500]} text-${colors.error[700]}`,
    info: `bg-${colors.primary[50]} border-${colors.primary[500]} text-${colors.primary[700]}`,
  };

  const icons = {
    success: (
      <svg className="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
        <path fillRule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.707-9.293a1 1 0 00-1.414-1.414L9 10.586 7.707 9.293a1 1 0 00-1.414 1.414l2 2a1 1 0 001.414 0l4-4z" clipRule="evenodd" />
      </svg>
    ),
    warning: (
      <svg className="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
        <path fillRule="evenodd" d="M8.257 3.099c.765-1.36 2.722-1.36 3.486 0l5.58 9.92c.75 1.334-.213 2.98-1.742 2.98H4.42c-1.53 0-2.493-1.646-1.743-2.98l5.58-9.92zM11 13a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zm-1-8a1 1 0 00-1 1v3a1 1 0 002 0V6a1 1 0 00-1-1z" clipRule="evenodd" />
      </svg>
    ),
    error: (
      <svg className="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
        <path fillRule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zM8.707 7.293a1 1 0 00-1.414 1.414L8.586 10l-1.293 1.293a1 1 0 101.414 1.414L10 11.414l1.293 1.293a1 1 0 001.414-1.414L11.414 10l1.293-1.293a1 1 0 00-1.414-1.414L10 8.586 8.707 7.293z" clipRule="evenodd" />
      </svg>
    ),
    info: (
      <svg className="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
        <path fillRule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-7-4a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zM9 9a1 1 0 000 2v3a1 1 0 001 1h1a1 1 0 100-2v-3a1 1 0 00-1-1H9z" clipRule="evenodd" />
      </svg>
    ),
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={`
        relative p-4 border-l-4 rounded-r-lg
        ${variantStyles[variant]}
        ${className}
      `}
      role="alert"
      aria-live="polite"
    >
      <div className="flex items-start">
        {showIcon && (
          <div className="flex-shrink-0 mr-3">
            {icons[variant]}
          </div>
        )}
        <div className="flex-1">
          {title && (
            <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold mb-1">
              {title}
            </h3>
          )}
          <p className="text-sm">{message}</p>
        </div>
        {onClose && (
          <button
            onClick={onClose}
            className="flex-shrink-0 ml-4 text-current opacity-50 hover:opacity-75 focus:outline-none"
            aria-label="Close alert"
          >
            <svg className="w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
              <path fillRule="evenodd" d="M4.293 4.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 8.586l4.293-4.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414L11.414 10l4.293 4.293a1 1 0 01-1.414 1.414L10 11.414l-4.293 4.293a1 1 0 01-1.414-1.414L8.586 10 4.293 5.707a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clipRule="evenodd" />
            </svg>
          </button>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

## 1. Configuração Principal do Datadog

```yaml
# Datadog Agent Configuration for DIYAPP V13
api_key: ${DD_API_KEY}
site: datadoghq.com

logs_enabled: true
apm_config:
  enabled: true
  env: production
  receiver_port: 8126
  max_traces_per_second: 100
  extra_sample_rate: 1.0
  max_events_per_second: 200

process_config:
  enabled: true
  intervals:
    container: 10
    process: 10

dogstatsd:
  port: 8125
  non_local_traffic: true

tags:
  - env:production
  - version:v13
  - service:diyapp
  - squad:autonomous
  - region:${REGION}

log_level: INFO

use_dogstatsd: true
hostname: ${HOSTNAME}
```

### `src/monitoring/datadog/config/apm-config.yaml`

```yaml
# APM Configuration
apm_config:
  enabled: true
  log_level: INFO
  
  # Service-specific configurations
  services:
    diyapp-api:
      env: production
      extra_services:
        - "diyapp-auth"
        - "diyapp-llm-gateway"
        - "diyapp-database"
    
  # Sampling rates
  sampling_rules:
    - sample_rate: 1.0
      name: health-check
      service: diyapp-api
      resource: GET /health
    - sample_rate: 0.1
      name: high-volume-endpoints
      service: diyapp-api
      resource: "GET /api/*"
    
  # Ignore specific endpoints
  ignore_resources:
    - "GET /robots.txt"
    - "OPTIONS *"
    
  # Custom tags for business metrics
  extra_tags:
    - "user_id"
    - "plan_type"
    - "llm_provider"
```

## 2. Definições de SLOs/SLIs

### `src/monitoring/slo/slo-definitions.yaml`

```yaml
# DIYAPP V13 SLO Definitions
version: "1.0"
last_updated: "2024-01-15"
service: "diyapp-v13"

slo_definitions:
  # API Availability SLO
  - name: "api-availability"
    description: "API HTTP availability"
    sli_type: "availability"
    target: 0.9995  # 99.95%
    time_window: "30d"
    burn_rate_thresholds:
      - rate: 1.0
        duration: "1h"
        severity: "warning"
      - rate: 5.0
        duration: "1h"
        severity: "critical"
    
    # SLI Configuration
    sli_config:
      query_type: "datadog"
      numerator: "sum:http.requests{status_code:2xx,status_code:3xx,service:diyapp-api}.as_count()"
      denominator: "sum:http.requests{service:diyapp-api}.as_count()"
      rollup: "1h"
      
  # API Latency SLO
  - name: "api-latency-p95"
    description: "95th percentile API response time"
    sli_type: "latency"
    target: 0.200  # 200ms
    time_window: "30d"
    
    sli_config:
      query_type: "datadog"
      query: "p95:trace.http.request.duration{service:diyapp-api,resource_name:GET /api/*}"
      threshold: 0.200
      rollup: "5m"
      
  # Error Rate SLO
  - name: "api-error-rate"
    description: "API 5xx error rate"
    sli_type: "error_rate"
    target: 0.001  # 0.1%
    time_window: "30d"
    
    sli_config:
      query_type: "datadog"
      numerator: "sum:http.requests{status_code:5xx,service:diyapp-api}.as_count()"
      denominator: "sum:http.requests{service:diyapp-api}.as_count()"
      rollup: "1h"
      
  # LLM Latency SLO
  - name: "llm-latency-p95"
    description: "95th percentile LLM response time"
    sli_type: "latency"
    target: 8.0  # 8 seconds
    time_window: "30d"
    
    sli_config:
      query_type: "datadog"
      query: "p95:diyapp.llm.response_time{service:diyapp-llm-gateway}"
      threshold: 8.0
      rollup: "5m"
      
  # LLM Availability SLO
  - name: "llm-availability"
    description: "LLM Gateway availability"
    sli_type: "availability"
    target: 0.999  # 99.9%
    time_window: "30d"
    
    sli_config:
      query_type: "datadog"
      numerator: "sum:diyapp.llm.requests{status:success}.as_count()"
      denominator: "sum:diyapp.llm.requests.as_count()"
      rollup: "1h"

# Error Budget Policy
error_budget_policy:
  burn_rate_thresholds:
    - rate: 1.0
      duration: "1h"
      action: "warning"
    - rate: 5.0
      duration: "1h"
      action: "critical"
    - rate: 10.0
      duration: "1h"
      action: "page"
      
  consumption_actions:
    - threshold: 0.5  # 50% budget remaining
      action: "normal_operations"
    - threshold: 0.2  # 20% budget remaining
      action: "increased_caution"
      notify: ["squad_leader", "product_manager"]
    - threshold: 0.0  # 0% budget remaining
      action: "feature_freeze"
      notify: ["squad_leader", "product_manager", "cto"]
```

### `src/monitoring/slo/error-budget-calculator.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Error Budget Calculator for DIYAPP V13
Calculates SLO compliance and error budget consumption
"""

import json
import yaml
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
import requests
import os

@dataclass
class SLOStatus:
    """SLO Status and Error Budget"""
    name: str
    target: float
    actual: float
    compliance: float
    error_budget_remaining: float
    error_budget_consumed: float
    burn_rate: float
    status: str  # healthy, warning, critical
    
class ErrorBudgetCalculator:
    def __init__(self, datadog_api_key: str, datadog_app_key: str):
        self.datadog_api_key = datadog_api_key
        self.datadog_app_key = datadog_app_key
        self.base_url = "https://api.datadoghq.com/api/v1"
        
    def calculate_slo_status(self, slo_id: str, timeframe: str = "30d") -> SLOStatus:
        """Calculate SLO status from Datadog"""
        headers = {
            "DD-API-KEY": self.datadog_api_key,
            "DD-APPLICATION-KEY": self.datadog_app_key,
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        
        # Get SLO data from Datadog
        url = f"{self.base_url}/slo/{slo_id}/history"
        params = {
            "from_ts": int((datetime.now() - timedelta(days=30)).timestamp()),
            "to_ts": int(datetime.now().timestamp()),
            "interval": 3600  # 1 hour intervals
        }
        
        response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params)
        response.raise_for_status()
        data = response.json()
        
        # Calculate metrics
        total_requests = sum(interval['numerator'] for interval in data['data'])
        total_success = sum(interval['denominator'] for interval in data['data'])
        
        actual_availability = total_success / total_requests if total_requests > 0 else 1.0
        target_availability = data['data'][0]['target'] if data['data'] else 0.999
        
        # Calculate error budget
        error_budget_minutes = 30 * 24 * 60 * (1 - target_availability)  # 30 days in minutes
        downtime_minutes = 30 * 24 * 60 * (1 - actual_availability)
        error_budget_consumed = downtime_minutes / error_budget_minutes if error_budget_minutes > 0 else 0
        error_budget_remaining = 1 - error_budget_consumed
        
        # Calculate burn rate (downtime in last hour / allowed downtime per hour)
        last_hour = data['data'][-1] if data['data'] else None
        if last_hour:
            hour_downtime = last_hour['denominator'] - last_hour['numerator']
            hour_allowed_downtime = (1 - target_availability) * last_hour['denominator']
            burn_rate = hour_downtime / hour_allowed_downtime if hour_allowed_downtime > 0 else 0
        else:
            burn_rate = 0
            
        # Determine status
        if error_budget_remaining > 0.5:
            status = "healthy"
        elif error_budget_remaining > 0.2:
            status = "warning"
        else:
            status = "critical"
            
        return SLOStatus(
            name=data.get('name', slo_id),
            target=target_availability,
            actual=actual_availability,
            compliance=actual_availability / target_availability if target_availability > 0 else 1.0,
            error_budget_remaining=error_budget_remaining,
            error_budget_consumed=error_budget_consumed,
            burn_rate=burn_rate,
            status=status
        )
    
    def generate_error_budget_report(self, slo_definitions_path: str) -> Dict:
        """Generate comprehensive error budget report"""
        with open(slo_definitions_path, 'r') as f:
            slo_defs = yaml.safe_load(f)
            
        report = {
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "overall_status": "healthy",
            "slo_status": [],
            "recommendations": []
        }
        
        critical_slos = []
        
        for slo in slo_defs['slo_definitions']:
            # In production, this would use actual SLO IDs from Datadog
            # For now, simulate with mock data
            status = self._mock_slo_status(slo)
            report['slo_status'].append(status.__dict__)
            
            if status.status == "critical":
                critical_slos.append(status.name)
                
        # Determine overall status
        if any(s['status'] == 'critical' for s in report['slo_status']):
            report['overall_status'] = "critical"
            report['recommendations'].append({
                "action": "feature_freeze",
                "reason": f"Critical SLOs: {', '.join(critical_slos)}",
                "urgency": "immediate"
            })
        elif any(s['status'] == 'warning' for s in report['slo_status']):
            report['overall_status'] = "warning"
            report['recommendations'].append({
                "action": "increased_caution",
                "reason": "Warning thresholds exceeded",
                "urgency": "high"
            })
            
        return report
    
    def _mock_slo_status(self, slo_def: Dict) -> SLOStatus:
        """Mock SLO status for demonstration"""
        # In production, replace with actual Datadog API calls
        import random
        
        target = slo_def['target']
        actual = target * random.uniform(0.98, 1.02)  # ±2% variation
        actual = min(actual, 1.0)  # Cap at 100%
        
        error_budget_consumed = random.uniform(0.0, 0.6)
        error_budget_remaining = 1 - error_budget_consumed
        
        if error_budget_remaining > 0.5:
            status = "healthy"
        elif error_budget_remaining > 0.2:
            status = "warning"
        else:
            status = "critical"
            
        return SLOStatus(
            name=slo_def['name'],
            target=target,
            actual=actual,
            compliance=actual / target if target > 0 else 1.0,
            error_budget_remaining=error_budget_remaining,
            error_budget_consumed=error_budget_consumed,
            burn_rate=random.uniform(0.5, 2.0),
            status=status
        )

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Load configuration
    api_key = os.getenv('DD_API_KEY')
    app_key = os.getenv('DD_APP_KEY')
    
    if not api_key or not app_key:
        print("Error: DD_API_KEY and DD_APP_KEY must be set")
        exit(1)
        
    calculator = ErrorBudgetCalculator(api_key, app_key)
    
    # Generate report
    report = calculator.generate_error_budget_report('src/monitoring/slo/slo-definitions.yaml')
    
    # Output report
    print(json.dumps(report, indent=2))
    
    # Save to file
    with open('error_budget_report.json', 'w') as f:
        json.dump(report, f, indent=2)
        
    print(f"\nReport saved to error_budget_report.json")
    print(f"Overall Status: {report['overall_status']}")
```

/**
 * API Instrumentation for DIYAPP V13

class APIInstrumentation {
  constructor() {
    this.metrics = metrics;
    this.logger = logger;
  }

  /**
   * Instrument Express.js middleware
   */
  instrumentExpress(app) {
    // Request timing middleware
    app.use((req, res, next) => {
      const startTime = Date.now();
      const path = req.path;
      const method = req.method;

      // Add trace headers
      const span = tracer.scope().active();
      if (span) {
        span.setTag('http.method', method);
        span.setTag('http.url', req.originalUrl);
        span.setTag('http.route', path);
      }

      // Capture response time
      res.on('finish', () => {

## 2. PADRÕES DE RESILIÊNCIA PARA V13

### 2.1. Circuit Breaker Pattern Implementation

```javascript
// Arquivo: src/v13/resilience/CircuitBreaker.js
class CircuitBreaker {
  constructor(service, options = {}) {
    this.service = service;
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.successCount = 0;
    this.nextAttempt = Date.now();
    
    this.threshold = options.threshold || 5;
    this.timeout = options.timeout || 10000;
    this.resetTimeout = options.resetTimeout || 60000;
    
    this.metrics = {
      totalRequests: 0,
      failedRequests: 0,
      successfulRequests: 0,
      stateChanges: []
    };
  }

  async call(...args) {
    this.metrics.totalRequests++;
    
    if (this.state === 'OPEN') {
      if (this.nextAttempt <= Date.now()) {
        this.state = 'HALF_OPEN';
        this.logStateChange('OPEN → HALF_OPEN');
      } else {
        throw new Error('Circuit breaker is OPEN');
      }
    }
    
    try {
      const result = await this.service(...args);
      this.onSuccess();
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      this.onFailure();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  onSuccess() {
    this.successCount++;
    this.failureCount = 0;
    
    if (this.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
      if (this.successCount >= this.threshold) {
        this.state = 'CLOSED';
        this.logStateChange('HALF_OPEN → CLOSED');
      }
    }
  }

  onFailure() {
    this.failureCount++;
    this.successCount = 0;
    this.metrics.failedRequests++;
    
    if (this.failureCount >= this.threshold && this.state !== 'OPEN') {
      this.state = 'OPEN';
      this.nextAttempt = Date.now() + this.timeout;
      this.logStateChange(`${this.state} → OPEN`);
      
      // Schedule automatic reset
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (this.state === 'OPEN') {
          this.state = 'HALF_OPEN';
          this.logStateChange('OPEN → HALF_OPEN (auto-reset)');
        }
      }, this.resetTimeout);
    }
  }

  logStateChange(transition) {
    this.metrics.stateChanges.push({
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      transition,
      metrics: { ...this.metrics }
    });
    
    // Emit event for monitoring
    this.emit('stateChange', {
      state: this.state,
      transition,
      metrics: this.metrics
    });
  }

  getStatus() {
    return {
      state: this.state,
      metrics: this.metrics,
      nextAttempt: this.state === 'OPEN' ? this.nextAttempt : null,
      health: this.calculateHealth()
    };
  }

  calculateHealth() {
    const total = this.metrics.totalRequests;
    if (total === 0) return 1.0;
    return this.metrics.successfulRequests / total;
  }
}

module.exports = CircuitBreaker;
```

### 2.2. Retry Strategy with Exponential Backoff

```javascript
// Arquivo: src/v13/resilience/RetryStrategy.js
class RetryStrategy {
  constructor(options = {}) {
    this.maxRetries = options.maxRetries || 3;
    this.baseDelay = options.baseDelay || 100;
    this.maxDelay = options.maxDelay || 10000;
    this.retryableErrors = options.retryableErrors || [
      'ECONNRESET', 'ETIMEDOUT', 'ECONNREFUSED'
    ];
    this.jitter = options.jitter || 0.1;
  }

  async execute(operation, context = {}) {
    let lastError;
    
    for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= this.maxRetries; attempt++) {
      try {
        if (attempt > 0) {
          const delay = this.calculateDelay(attempt);
          await this.sleep(delay);
          
          console.log(`Retry attempt ${attempt}/${this.maxRetries} after ${delay}ms`, {
            operation: context.operation,
            attempt
          });
        }
        
        return await operation();
        
      } catch (error) {
        lastError = error;
        
        if (!this.shouldRetry(error) || attempt === this.maxRetries) {
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    
    throw this.enhanceError(lastError, context);
  }

  calculateDelay(attempt) {
    // Exponential backoff with jitter
    const exponentialDelay = this.baseDelay * Math.pow(2, attempt);
    const delay = Math.min(exponentialDelay, this.maxDelay);
    
    // Add jitter to prevent thundering herd
    const jitterAmount = delay * this.jitter;
    const jitter = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * jitterAmount;
    
    return Math.max(0, delay + jitter);
  }

  shouldRetry(error) {
    // Check error code
    if (error.code && this.retryableErrors.includes(error.code)) {
      return true;
    }
    
    // Check HTTP status codes
    if (error.statusCode) {
      return [408, 429, 500, 502, 503, 504].includes(error.statusCode);
    }
    
    // Check error message patterns
    const retryablePatterns = [
      /timeout/i,
      /connection reset/i,
      /service unavailable/i,
      /too many requests/i
    ];
    
    return retryablePatterns.some(pattern => 
      pattern.test(error.message)
    );
  }

  sleep(ms) {
    return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
  }

  enhanceError(error, context) {
    error.retryContext = {
      ...context,
      retriesAttempted: this.maxRetries,
      timestamp: Date.now()
    };
    
    error.message = `Operation failed after ${this.maxRetries} retries: ${error.message}`;
    
    return error;
  }
}

module.exports = RetryStrategy;
```

### 2.3. Fallback Strategy Implementation

```javascript
// Arquivo: src/v13/resilience/FallbackStrategy.js
class FallbackStrategy {
  constructor(options = {}) {
    this.fallbackHandlers = new Map();
    this.cache = options.cache || null;
    this.defaultTtl = options.defaultTtl || 300000; // 5 minutes
    this.metrics = {
      fallbackTriggers: 0,
      fallbackSuccesses: 0,
      fallbackFailures: 0,
      cacheHits: 0,
      cacheMisses: 0
    };
  }

  register(operationName, fallbackHandler, options = {}) {
    this.fallbackHandlers.set(operationName, {
      handler: fallbackHandler,
      cacheKey: options.cacheKey || operationName,
      ttl: options.ttl || this.defaultTtl,
      staleWhileRevalidate: options.staleWhileRevalidate || false
    });
  }

  async execute(operationName, primaryOperation, ...args) {
    try {
      return await primaryOperation(...args);
    } catch (primaryError) {
      this.metrics.fallbackTriggers++;
      
      // Check cache first
      const cachedResult = await this.getFromCache(operationName);
      if (cachedResult) {
        this.metrics.cacheHits++;
        
        // Async revalidation if enabled
        if (this.shouldRevalidate(operationName)) {
          this.revalidateInBackground(operationName, primaryOperation, args);
        }
        
        return cachedResult;
      }
      
      this.metrics.cacheMisses++;
      
      // Execute fallback
      const fallbackConfig = this.fallbackHandlers.get(operationName);
      if (!fallbackConfig) {
        throw this.createFallbackError(primaryError, 'NO_FALLBACK_CONFIGURED');
      }
      
      try {
        const fallbackResult = await fallbackConfig.handler(...args);
        this.metrics.fallbackSuccesses++;
        
        // Cache the fallback result
        await this.cacheResult(operationName, fallbackResult, fallbackConfig.ttl);
        
        return fallbackResult;
      } catch (fallbackError) {
        this.metrics.fallbackFailures++;
        throw this.createFallbackError(primaryError, 'FALLBACK_FAILED', fallbackError);
      }
    }
  }

  async getFromCache(operationName) {
    if (!this.cache) return null;
    
    const config = this.fallbackHandlers.get(operationName);
    if (!config) return null;
    
    return this.cache.get(config.cacheKey);
  }

  async cacheResult(operationName, result, ttl) {
    if (!this.cache) return;
    
    const config = this.fallbackHandlers.get(operationName);
    await this.cache.set(config.cacheKey, result, ttl);
  }

  shouldRevalidate(operationName) {
    const config = this.fallbackHandlers.get(operationName);
    return config && config.staleWhileRevalidate;
  }

  async revalidateInBackground(operationName, primaryOperation, args) {
    setTimeout(async () => {
      try {
        const freshResult = await primaryOperation(...args);
        await this.cacheResult(operationName, freshResult);
      } catch (error) {
        console.warn(`Background revalidation failed for ${operationName}:`, error);
      }
    }, 0);
  }

  createFallbackError(primaryError, reason, fallbackError = null) {
    const error = new Error(`Fallback strategy triggered: ${reason}`);
    error.originalError = primaryError;
    error.fallbackError = fallbackError;
    error.reason = reason;
    error.timestamp = Date.now();
    error.metrics = { ...this.metrics };
    
    return error;
  }

  getMetrics() {
    return {
      ...this.metrics,
      successRate: this.metrics.fallbackTriggers > 0 
        ? this.metrics.fallbackSuccesses / this.metrics.fallbackTriggers 
        : 1
    };
  }
}

module.exports = FallbackStrategy;
```

## 3. Espaçamento (tokens/spacing.css)

```css
:root {
  /* Espaçamento baseado em 4px */
  --spacing-0: 0;
  --spacing-1: 0.25rem;   /* 4px */
  --spacing-2: 0.5rem;    /* 8px */
  --spacing-3: 0.75rem;   /* 12px */
  --spacing-4: 1rem;      /* 16px */
  --spacing-5: 1.25rem;   /* 20px */
  --spacing-6: 1.5rem;    /* 24px */
  --spacing-8: 2rem;      /* 32px */
  --spacing-10: 2.5rem;   /* 40px */
  --spacing-12: 3rem;     /* 48px */
  --spacing-16: 4rem;     /* 64px */
  --spacing-20: 5rem;     /* 80px */
  
  /* Border radius */
  --radius-sm: 0.25rem;   /* 4px */
  --radius-md: 0.375rem;  /* 6px */
  --radius-lg: 0.5rem;    /* 8px */
  --radius-xl: 0.75rem;   /* 12px */
  --radius-2xl: 1rem;     /* 16px */
  --radius-full: 9999px;
  
  /* Shadows - Elevação */
  --shadow-sm: 0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05);
  --shadow-md: 0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 2px 4px -2px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1);
  --shadow-lg: 0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 4px 6px -4px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1);
  --shadow-xl: 0 20px 25px -5px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 8px 10px -6px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1);
  
  /* Transições */
  --transition-fast: 150ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
  --transition-normal: 250ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
  --transition-slow: 350ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
}
```

## 1. Configurações de Resiliência

**src/config/resilienceConfig.js**
```javascript
/**
 * Configurações de resiliência para serviços externos
 * Timeouts em milissegundos
 */
const resilienceConfig = {
  // Timeouts por tipo de serviço
  timeouts: {
    database: {
      query: 2000,
      transaction: 5000,
      connection: 10000
    },
    externalApi: {
      fast: 1000,
      normal: 3000,
      slow: 10000
    },
    cache: {
      get: 100,
      set: 200,
      delete: 100
    },
    llm: {
      completion: 30000,  // 30 segundos para LLMs
      embedding: 10000
    }
  },

  // Circuit Breaker
  circuitBreaker: {
    failureThreshold: 5,      // 5 falhas consecutivas
    resetTimeout: 30000,      // 30 segundos para resetar
    halfOpenMaxAttempts: 3    // 3 tentativas em half-open
  },

  // Retry Strategy
  retry: {
    maxAttempts: 3,
    initialDelay: 100,
    maxDelay: 5000,
    jitter: true,
    retryableErrors: ['ECONNRESET', 'ETIMEDOUT', 'ECONNREFUSED', 503, 504]
  },

  // Bulkhead Pattern
  bulkhead: {
    maxConcurrent: 10,
    maxQueue: 100
  },

  // Rate Limiting
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: 60000,  // 1 minuto
    max: 100          // 100 requisições por minuto
  }
};

module.exports = resilienceConfig;
```

## 2. Logger Estruturado em JSON

**src/services/core/monitoring/structuredLogger.js**
```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

class StructuredLogger {
  constructor(serviceName = 'diyapp-v13') {
    this.serviceName = serviceName;
    this.correlationId = null;
    
    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.json()
      ),
      defaultMeta: { service: this.serviceName },
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.Console(),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: 'logs/error.log', 
          level: 'error' 
        }),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: 'logs/combined.log' 
        })
      ]
    });
  }

  setCorrelationId(correlationId) {
    this.correlationId = correlationId;
  }

  generateCorrelationId() {
    return uuidv4();
  }

  // Métodos de logging com dados estruturados
  info(message, meta = {}) {
    this.logger.info(message, this._enrichMeta(meta));
  }

  error(message, error = null, meta = {}) {
    const enrichedMeta = this._enrichMeta(meta);
    
    if (error) {
      enrichedMeta.error = {
        message: error.message,
        stack: error.stack,
        code: error.code,
        name: error.name
      };
    }
    
    this.logger.error(message, enrichedMeta);
  }

  warn(message, meta = {}) {
    this.logger.warn(message, this._enrichMeta(meta));
  }

  debug(message, meta = {}) {
    this.logger.debug(message, this._enrichMeta(meta));
  }

  // Método para log de requisições HTTP
  httpRequest(req, res, durationMs) {
    const meta = {
      correlation_id: this.correlationId || req.correlationId,
      user_id: req.user?.id || 'anonymous',
      endpoint: `${req.method} ${req.originalUrl}`,
      duration_ms: durationMs,
      status: res.statusCode,
      user_agent: req.get('User-Agent'),
      ip: req.ip,
      query_params: this._maskSensitiveData(req.query),
      body: this._maskSensitiveData(req.body)
    };

    if (res.statusCode >= 400) {
      this.error(`HTTP ${req.method} ${req.originalUrl}`, null, meta);
    } else {
      this.info(`HTTP ${req.method} ${req.originalUrl}`, meta);
    }
  }

  // Método para log de chamadas externas
  externalCall(service, operation, durationMs, success, error = null, meta = {}) {
    const logMeta = {
      ...meta,
      correlation_id: this.correlationId,
      service,
      operation,
      duration_ms: durationMs,
      success
    };

    if (error) {
      this.error(`External call failed: ${service}.${operation}`, error, logMeta);
    } else {
      this.info(`External call: ${service}.${operation}`, logMeta);
    }
  }

  // Método para log de métricas de negócio
  businessMetric(metricName, value, tags = {}) {
    this.info(`Business metric: ${metricName}`, {
      correlation_id: this.correlationId,
      metric_name: metricName,
      metric_value: value,
      metric_type: 'business',
      tags
    });
  }

  // Métodos privados
  _enrichMeta(meta) {
    return {
      ...meta,
      correlation_id: this.correlationId,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      environment: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development'
    };
  }

  _maskSensitiveData(data) {
    if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') return data;
    
    const masked = { ...data };
    const sensitiveFields = [
      'password', 'token', 'secret', 'key', 
      'credit_card', 'cvv', 'cpf', 'ssn',
      'email', 'phone'
    ];

    sensitiveFields.forEach(field => {
      if (masked[field]) {
        masked[field] = '***MASKED***';
      }
    });

    return masked;
  }
}

// Singleton instance
const logger = new StructuredLogger();
module.exports = logger;
```

## 3. Circuit Breaker Pattern

**src/services/core/resilience/circuitBreaker.js**
```javascript
const logger = require('../monitoring/structuredLogger');

class CircuitBreaker {
  constructor(name, options = {}) {
    this.name = name;
    this.state = 'CLOSED'; // CLOSED, OPEN, HALF_OPEN
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.successCount = 0;
    this.lastFailureTime = null;
    
    // Configurações
    this.failureThreshold = options.failureThreshold || 5;
    this.resetTimeout = options.resetTimeout || 30000; // 30 segundos
    this.halfOpenMaxAttempts = options.halfOpenMaxAttempts || 3;
    this.halfOpenAttempts = 0;
    
    // Métricas
    this.metrics = {
      totalCalls: 0,
      successfulCalls: 0,
      failedCalls: 0,
      circuitOpened: 0,
      circuitClosed: 0
    };
  }

  async execute(operation, fallback = null) {
    this.metrics.totalCalls++;
    
    // Verifica se o circuito está aberto
    if (this.state === 'OPEN') {
      const timeSinceFailure = Date.now() - this.lastFailureTime;
      
      if (timeSinceFailure > this.resetTimeout) {
        this._transitionToHalfOpen();
      } else {
        this.metrics.failedCalls++;
        logger.warn(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} is OPEN - using fallback`, {
          circuit_state: this.state,
          time_since_failure_ms: timeSinceFailure
        });
        
        return this._executeFallback(fallback, new Error(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} is OPEN`));
      }
    }
    
    try {
      // Executa a operação
      const result = await operation();
      
      // Registra sucesso
      this._recordSuccess();
      this.metrics.successfulCalls++;
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      // Registra falha
      this._recordFailure(error);
      this.metrics.failedCalls++;
      
      logger.error(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} operation failed`, error, {
        circuit_state: this.state,
        failure_count: this.failureCount
      });
      
      // Executa fallback se disponível
      return this._executeFallback(fallback, error);
    }
  }

  _recordSuccess() {
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.halfOpenAttempts = 0;
    
    if (this.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
      this.halfOpenAttempts++;
      
      if (this.halfOpenAttempts >= this.halfOpenMaxAttempts) {
        this._transitionToClosed();
      }
    }
    
    this.successCount++;
  }

  _recordFailure(error) {
    this.failureCount++;
    this.lastFailureTime = Date.now();
    
    if (this.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
      this._transitionToOpen();
    } else if (this.state === 'CLOSED' && this.failureCount >= this.failureThreshold) {
      this._transitionToOpen();
    }
  }

  _transitionToOpen() {
    this.state = 'OPEN';
    this.metrics.circuitOpened++;
    
    logger.error(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} transitioned to OPEN`, null, {
      failure_count: this.failureCount,
      last_failure_time: new Date(this.lastFailureTime).toISOString()
    });
  }

  _transitionToHalfOpen() {
    this.state = 'HALF_OPEN';
    this.halfOpenAttempts = 0;
    
    logger.warn(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} transitioned to HALF_OPEN`);
  }

  _transitionToClosed() {
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.metrics.circuitClosed++;
    
    logger.info(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} transitioned to CLOSED`);
  }

  async _executeFallback(fallback, error) {
    if (fallback && typeof fallback === 'function') {
      try {
        logger.info(`Executing fallback for circuit breaker ${this.name}`);
        return await fallback(error);
      } catch (fallbackError) {
        logger.error(`Fallback for circuit breaker ${this.name} also failed`, fallbackError);
        throw new Error(`Primary operation and fallback failed: ${error.message}`);
      }
    }
    
    throw error;
  }

  getMetrics() {
    return {
      ...this.metrics,
      name: this.name,
      state: this.state,
      failureCount: this.failureCount,
      successCount: this.successCount,
      lastFailureTime: this.lastFailureTime,
      health: this.getHealth()
    };
  }

  getHealth() {
    const successRate = this.metrics.totalCalls > 0 
      ? (this.metrics.successfulCalls / this.metrics.totalCalls) * 100 
      : 100;
    
    return {
      status: this.state === 'CLOSED' ? 'healthy' : 'degraded',
      successRate: successRate.toFixed(2),
      isCircuitOpen: this.state === 'OPEN'
    };
  }

  reset() {
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.successCount = 0;
    this.lastFailureTime = null;
    this.halfOpenAttempts = 0;
    
    logger.info(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} manually reset`);
  }
}

// Registry para gerenciar múltiplos circuit breakers
class CircuitBreakerRegistry {
  constructor() {
    this.breakers = new Map();
  }

  getOrCreate(name, options = {}) {
    if (!this.breakers.has(name)) {
      this.breakers.set(name, new CircuitBreaker(name, options));
    }
    
    return this.breakers.get(name);
  }

  getMetrics() {
    const metrics = {};
    
    for (const [name, breaker] of this.breakers) {
      metrics[name] = breaker.getMetrics();
    }
    
    return metrics;
  }

  getHealth() {
    const health = {
      overall: 'healthy',
      breakers: {}
    };
    
    let hasOpenCircuit = false;
    
    for (const [name, breaker] of this.breakers) {
      const breakerHealth = breaker.getHealth();
      health.breakers[name] = breakerHealth;
      
      if (breakerHealth.isCircuitOpen) {
        hasOpenCircuit = true;
      }
    }
    
    health.overall = hasOpenCircuit ? 'degraded' : 'healthy';
    
    return health;
  }

  resetAll() {
    for (const breaker of this.breakers.values()) {
      breaker.reset();
    }
  }
}

// Singleton instance
const registry = new CircuitBreakerRegistry();
module.exports = { CircuitBreaker, CircuitBreakerRegistry, registry };
```

## 4. Retry Strategy com Backoff Exponencial

**src/services/core/resilience/retryStrategy.js**
```javascript
const logger = require('../monitoring/structuredLogger');

class RetryStrategy {
  constructor(options = {}) {
    this.maxAttempts = options.maxAttempts || 3;
    this.initialDelay = options.initialDelay || 100;
    this.maxDelay = options.maxDelay || 5000;
    this.jitter = options.jitter !== false;
    this.retryableErrors = options.retryableErrors || [
      'ECONNRESET', 'ETIMEDOUT', 'ECONNREFUSED',
      503, 504, 'ENOTFOUND'
    ];
  }

  async execute(operation, context = {}) {
    let lastError;
    let attempt = 1;
    
    while (attempt <= this.maxAttempts) {
      try {
        const startTime = Date.now();
        const result = await operation();
        const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
        
        if (attempt > 1) {
          logger.info(`Operation succeeded on retry attempt ${attempt}`, {
            ...context,
            attempt,
            total_attempts: attempt,
            duration_ms: duration
          });
        }
        
        return result;
      } catch (error) {
        lastError = error;
        
        // Verifica se o erro é retryable
        if (!this._isRetryableError(error)) {
          logger.error('Non-retryable error encountered', error, {
            ...context,
            attempt
          });
          throw error;
        }
        
        // Log do erro de retry
        logger.warn(`Retry attempt ${attempt} failed`, error, {
          ...context,
          attempt,
          error_code: error.code,
          error_message: error.message
        });
        
        // Se for a última tentativa, lança o erro
        if (attempt === this.maxAttempts) {
          logger.error(`Max retry attempts (${this.maxAttempts}) exceeded`, error, {
            ...context,
            total_attempts: attempt
          });
          throw new Error(`Operation failed after ${attempt} attempts: ${error.message}`);
        }
        
        // Calcula delay com backoff exponencial
        const delay = this._calculateDelay(attempt);
        
        // Aguarda antes da próxima tentativa
        await this._sleep(delay);
        
        attempt++;
      }
    }
    
    throw lastError;
  }

  _isRetryableError(error) {
    // Verifica por código de erro
    if (error.code && this.retryableErrors.includes(error.code)) {
      return true;
    }
    
    // Verifica por status HTTP
    if (error.statusCode && this.retryableErrors.includes(error.statusCode)) {
      return true;
    }
    
    // Verifica por tipo de erro
    if (error.name && this.retryableErrors.includes(error.name)) {
      return true;
    }
    
    return false;
  }

  _calculateDelay(attempt) {
    // Backoff exponencial: initialDelay * 2^(attempt-1)
    let delay = this.initialDelay * Math.pow(2, attempt - 1);
    
    // Aplica limite máximo
    delay = Math.min(delay, this.maxDelay);
    
    // Adiciona jitter para evitar thundering herd
    if (this.jitter) {
      const jitter = delay * 0.1; // 10% de jitter
      delay += Math.random() * jitter;
    }
    
    return Math.floor(delay);
  }

  _sleep(ms) {
    return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
  }

  // Método estático para uso rápido
  static async retry(operation, options = {}, context = {}) {
    const strategy = new RetryStrategy(options);
   

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
