## 2. Componente Button com todos os estados

**src/components/design-system/Button/Button.tsx**
```typescript
import React, { forwardRef, ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { designTokens } from '../tokens';
import { useTransition } from '../../../hooks/useTransition';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

export interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
}

const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  (
    {
      children,
      variant = 'primary',
      size = 'md',
      isLoading = false,
      leftIcon,
      rightIcon,
      fullWidth = false,
      disabled,
      className = '',
      onClick,
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const { isTransitioning, startTransition } = useTransition(300);
    const isDisabled = disabled || isLoading || isTransitioning;

    const baseStyles = {
      fontFamily: designTokens.typography.fontFamily.sans,
      fontWeight: designTokens.typography.fontWeight.medium,
      display: 'inline-flex',
      alignItems: 'center',
      justifyContent: 'center',
      border: 'none',
      borderRadius: '0.5rem',
      cursor: isDisabled ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
      transition: 'all 150ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
      width: fullWidth ? '100%' : 'auto',
      position: 'relative',
      overflow: 'hidden',
    };

    const sizeStyles = {
      sm: {
        fontSize: designTokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
        padding: `${designTokens.spacing[2]} ${designTokens.spacing[3]}`,
        gap: designTokens.spacing[2],
      },
      md: {
        fontSize: designTokens.typography.fontSize.base,
        padding: `${designTokens.spacing[3]} ${designTokens.spacing[4]}`,
        gap: designTokens.spacing[3],
      },
      lg: {
        fontSize: designTokens.typography.fontSize.lg,
        padding: `${designTokens.spacing[4]} ${designTokens.spacing[6]}`,
        gap: designTokens.spacing[4],
      },
    };

    const variantStyles = {
      primary: {
        backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[600],
        color: designTokens.colors.text.inverse,
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[700],
          transform: 'translateY(-1px)',
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[800],
          transform: 'translateY(0)',
        },
        '&:disabled': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[300],
          color: designTokens.colors.neutral[500],
        },
      },
      secondary: {
        backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[100],
        color: designTokens.colors.text.primary,
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[200],
          transform: 'translateY(-1px)',
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[300],
          transform: 'translateY(0)',
        },
        '&:disabled': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[100],
          color: designTokens.colors.neutral[400],
        },
      },
      outline: {
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',
        color: designTokens.colors.primary[600],
        border: `1px solid ${designTokens.colors.primary[600]}`,
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[50],
          transform: 'translateY(-1px)',
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[100],
          transform: 'translateY(0)',
        },
        '&:disabled': {
          borderColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[300],
          color: designTokens.colors.neutral[400],
        },
      },
      ghost: {
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',
        color: designTokens.colors.text.primary,
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[100],
          transform: 'translateY(-1px)',
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[200],
          transform: 'translateY(0)',
        },
        '&:disabled': {
          color: designTokens.colors.neutral[400],
        },
      },
      danger: {
        backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.error[500],
        color: designTokens.colors.text.inverse,
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.error[600],
          transform: 'translateY(-1px)',
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.error[700],
          transform: 'translateY(0)',
        },
        '&:disabled': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[300],
          color: designTokens.colors.neutral[500],
        },
      },
    };

    const handleClick = (e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLButtonElement>) => {
      if (isDisabled) return;
      startTransition();
      onClick?.(e);
    };

    return (
      <button
        ref={ref}
        disabled={isDisabled}
        onClick={handleClick}
        style={{
          ...baseStyles,
          ...sizeStyles[size],
          ...variantStyles[variant],
          opacity: isDisabled ? 0.6 : 1,
        }}
        className={className}
        aria-busy={isLoading}
        {...props}
      >
        {isLoading && (
          <span
            style={{
              position: 'absolute',
              left: '50%',
              top: '50%',
              transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)',
              width: '1.5em',
              height: '1.5em',
              border: `2px solid ${designTokens.colors.neutral[200]}`,
              borderTopColor: variant === 'ghost' || variant === 'outline' 
                ? designTokens.colors.primary[600] 
                : designTokens.colors.text.inverse,
              borderRadius: '50%',
              animation: 'spin 1s linear infinite',
            }}
            aria-hidden="true"
          />
        )}
        
        <span
          style={{
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'center',
            gap: sizeStyles[size].gap,
            opacity: isLoading ? 0 : 1,
            transition: 'opacity 150ms ease',
          }}
        >
          {leftIcon && <span>{leftIcon}</span>}
          {children}
          {rightIcon && <span>{rightIcon}</span>}
        </span>
        
        <style>{`
          @keyframes spin {
            to { transform: translate(-50%, -50%) rotate(360deg); }
          }
        `}</style>
      </button>
    );
  }
);

Button.displayName = 'Button';

export default Button;
```

**src/components/design-system/Button/Button.test.tsx**
```typescript
import React from 'react';
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import Button from './Button';

describe('Button Component', () => {
  test('renders with default props', () => {
    render(<Button>Click me</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i });
    expect(button).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(button).toHaveStyle({ backgroundColor: '#0284c7' });
  });

  test('renders with secondary variant', () => {
    render(<Button variant="secondary">Secondary</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toHaveStyle({ backgroundColor: '#f5f5f5' });
  });

  test('shows loading state', () => {
    render(<Button isLoading>Loading</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('aria-busy', 'true');
    expect(button).toBeDisabled();
  });

  test('handles click events', () => {
    const handleClick = jest.fn();
    render(<Button onClick={handleClick}>Click</Button>);
    fireEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button'));
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
  });

  test('does not fire click when disabled', () => {
    const handleClick = jest.fn();
    render(<Button disabled onClick={handleClick}>Disabled</Button>);
    fireEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button'));
    expect(handleClick).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
  });

  test('renders with left icon', () => {
    const icon = <span data-testid="icon">🎯</span>;
    render(<Button leftIcon={icon}>With Icon</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByTestId('icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  test('has proper accessibility attributes', () => {
    render(<Button aria-label="Custom label">Button</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveAttribute('aria-label', 'Custom label');
  });
});
```

## 3. Componente Skeleton

**src/components/design-system/Skeleton/Skeleton.tsx**
```typescript
import React from 'react';
import { designTokens } from '../tokens';

export interface SkeletonProps {
  width?: string | number;
  height?: string | number;
  borderRadius?: string;
  className?: string;
  variant?: 'text' | 'circular' | 'rectangular';
  animation?: 'pulse' | 'wave' | 'none';
  count?: number;
}

const Skeleton: React.FC<SkeletonProps> = ({
  width = '100%',
  height = '1rem',
  borderRadius = '0.375rem',
  className = '',
  variant = 'text',
  animation = 'pulse',
  count = 1,
}) => {
  const baseStyles: React.CSSProperties = {
    backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[200],
    borderRadius: variant === 'circular' ? '50%' : borderRadius,
    width: typeof width === 'number' ? `${width}px` : width,
    height: typeof height === 'number' ? `${height}px` : height,
    display: 'inline-block',
    position: 'relative',
    overflow: 'hidden',
  };

  const animationStyles = {
    pulse: {
      animation: 'pulse 1.5s ease-in-out 0.5s infinite',
    },
    wave: {
      position: 'relative',
      overflow: 'hidden',
      '::after': {
        content: '""',
        position: 'absolute',
        top: 0,
        left: 0,
        right: 0,
        bottom: 0,
        background: `linear-gradient(90deg, transparent, ${designTokens.colors.neutral[100]}, transparent)`,
        animation: 'wave 1.6s linear 0.5s infinite',
      },
    },
    none: {},
  };

  const skeletons = Array.from({ length: count }, (_, index) => (
    <div
      key={index}
      style={{
        ...baseStyles,
        ...animationStyles[animation],
        marginBottom: index < count - 1 ? designTokens.spacing[2] : 0,
      }}
      className={className}
      aria-label="Loading content"
      role="status"
    />
  ));

  return (
    <>
      {skeletons}
      <style>{`
        @keyframes pulse {
          0%, 100% {
            opacity: 1;
          }
          50% {
            opacity: 0.5;
          }
        }
        
        @keyframes wave {

# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Sistema de Monitoramento SRE

Vou configurar um sistema completo de monitoramento SRE para a V13, incluindo instrumentação APM, dashboards, SLOs/SLIs e alertas inteligentes. O sistema será implementado com uma arquitetura modular que pode funcionar tanto com Datadog quanto Grafana.

## 1. Configuração Principal (config/monitoring-config.js)

```javascript
// config/monitoring-config.js
module.exports = {
  // Configurações do SRE para V13
  serviceName: 'diyapp-v13-core',
  environment: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'production',
  
  // SLOs Definidos para V13
  slos: {
    availability: {
      target: 99.95, // 99.95% disponibilidade
      window: '30d', // Janela de 30 dias
      maxDowntime: 21.6, // minutos por mês (43.2 * 0.5 para 99.95%)
    },
    latency: {
      p95: 200, // ms
      p99: 500, // ms
      window: '5m', // Janela de 5 minutos para cálculo
    },
    errorRate: {
      target: 0.05, // 0.05% de erro
      window: '1h',
    },
    throughput: {
      minRpm: 1000, // Requisições por minuto mínimas
    }
  },
  
  // Configuração APM
  apm: {
    enabled: true,
    samplingRate: 1.0, // 100% em produção
    ignorePaths: ['/health', '/metrics'],
    slowQueryThreshold: 1000, // ms
  },
  
  // Configuração de Logs
  logging: {
    level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
    format: 'json',
    enableStructuredLogging: true,
    logToConsole: true,
    logToFile: true,
    logFilePath: '/var/log/diyapp/v13/',
  },
  
  // Configuração de Alertas
  alerts: {
    anomalyDetection: {
      enabled: true,
      sensitivity: 'medium', // low, medium, high
      trainingPeriod: '7d',
    },
    escalation: {
      sev1: {
        responseTime: '5m',
        notify: ['sre@diyapp.com', 'squad-leader@diyapp.com'],
        autoPage: true,
      },
      sev2: {
        responseTime: '15m',
        notify: ['sre@diyapp.com'],
      },
      sev3: {
        responseTime: '1h',
        notify: ['dev-team@diyapp.com'],
      },
    },
  },
  
  // Backend de Monitoramento (Datadog ou Grafana)
  backend: process.env.MONITORING_BACKEND || 'grafana', // 'datadog' ou 'grafana'
  
  // URLs dos serviços
  endpoints: {
    grafana: process.env.GRAFANA_URL || 'http://localhost:3000',
    prometheus: process.env.PROMETHEUS_URL || 'http://localhost:9090',
    loki: process.env.LOKI_URL || 'http://localhost:3100',
    tempo: process.env.TEMPO_URL || 'http://localhost:3200',
    datadog: process.env.DATADOG_URL || 'https://app.datadoghq.com',
  },
  
  // API Keys (em produção usar variáveis de ambiente)
  apiKeys: {
    datadog: {
      apiKey: process.env.DATADOG_API_KEY,
      appKey: process.env.DATADOG_APP_KEY,
    },
    grafana: {
      apiKey: process.env.GRAFANA_API_KEY,
      user: process.env.GRAFANA_USER,
      password: process.env.GRAFANA_PASSWORD,
    },
  },
};

## 2. Instrumentação APM (src/instrumentation/apm.js)

```javascript
// src/instrumentation/apm.js
const config = require('../../config/monitoring-config');
const logger = require('./logger');

class APMInstrumentation {
  constructor() {
    this.spans = new Map();
    this.metrics = new Map();
    this.initAPM();
  }

  initAPM() {
    // Inicializa o APM baseado no backend configurado
    switch (config.backend) {
      case 'datadog':
        this.initDatadogAPM();
        break;
      case 'grafana':
        this.initGrafanaAPM();
        break;
      default:
        this.initOpenTelemetry();
    }
    
    logger.info('APM instrumentation initialized', { backend: config.backend });
  }

  initDatadogAPM() {
    // Para Datadog
    try {
      const tracer = require('dd-trace').init({
        service: config.serviceName,
        env: config.environment,
        version: 'v13.0.0',
        logInjection: true,
        runtimeMetrics: true,
        profiling: true,
        sampleRate: config.apm.samplingRate,
      });
      
      this.tracer = tracer;
      logger.info('Datadog APM initialized');
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to initialize Datadog APM', { error: error.message });
    }
  }

  initGrafanaAPM() {
    // Para Grafana (OpenTelemetry)
    try {
      const { NodeTracerProvider } = require('@opentelemetry/sdk-trace-node');
      const { SimpleSpanProcessor } = require('@opentelemetry/sdk-trace-base');
      const { OTLPTraceExporter } = require('@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-http');
      const { Resource } = require('@opentelemetry/resources');
      const { SemanticResourceAttributes } = require('@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions');
      
      const provider = new NodeTracerProvider({
        resource: new Resource({
          [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: config.serviceName,
          [SemanticResourceAttributes.DEPLOYMENT_ENVIRONMENT]: config.environment,
        }),
      });

      const exporter = new OTLPTraceExporter({
        url: `${config.endpoints.tempo}/api/traces`,
      });

      provider.addSpanProcessor(new SimpleSpanProcessor(exporter));
      provider.register();
      
      this.provider = provider;
      logger.info('Grafana/OpenTelemetry APM initialized');
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to initialize Grafana APM', { error: error.message });
    }
  }

  initOpenTelemetry() {
    // OpenTelemetry padrão
    try {
      const opentelemetry = require('@opentelemetry/api');
      this.api = opentelemetry;
      logger.info('OpenTelemetry APM initialized');
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to initialize OpenTelemetry', { error: error.message });
    }
  }

  startSpan(name, attributes = {}) {
    try {
      let span;
      
      if (this.tracer) {
        // Datadog
        span = this.tracer.startSpan(name);
        Object.entries(attributes).forEach(([key, value]) => {
          span.setTag(key, value);
        });
      } else if (this.api) {
        // OpenTelemetry
        const tracer = this.api.trace.getTracer(config.serviceName);
        span = tracer.startSpan(name, { attributes });
      }
      
      if (span) {
        this.spans.set(span.context().spanId, {
          span,
          name,
          startTime: Date.now(),
          attributes,
        });
      }
      
      return span;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to start span', { error: error.message, spanName: name });
      return null;
    }
  }

  endSpan(span, status = 'ok', error = null) {
    try {
      if (!span) return;
      
      const spanId = span.context().spanId;
      const spanInfo = this.spans.get(spanId);
      
      if (spanInfo) {
        const duration = Date.now() - spanInfo.startTime;
        
        // Registrar métrica de duração
        this.recordMetric(`span.duration`, duration, {
          span_name: spanInfo.name,
          status,
          ...spanInfo.attributes,
        });
        
        // Marcar span como erro se aplicável
        if (error) {
          if (this.tracer) {
            span.setTag('error', true);
            span.setTag('error.message', error.message);
          } else if (this.api) {
            span.setAttribute('error', true);
            span.setAttribute('error.message', error.message);
            span.setStatus({ code: this.api.SpanStatusCode.ERROR, message: error.message });
          }
        }
        
        span.end();
        this.spans.delete(spanId);
        
        // Alertar se a duração exceder o threshold
        if (duration > config.apm.slowQueryThreshold) {
          this.alertSlowSpan(spanInfo.name, duration, spanInfo.attributes);
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to end span', { error: error.message });
    }
  }

  recordMetric(name, value, tags = {}) {
    try {
      const metricKey = `${name}_${JSON.stringify(tags)}`;
      this.metrics.set(metricKey, {
        name,
        value,
        tags,
        timestamp: Date.now(),
      });
      
      // Enviar para backend de métricas
      this.sendMetricToBackend(name, value, tags);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to record metric', { error: error.message, metricName: name });
    }
  }

  sendMetricToBackend(name, value, tags) {
    // Implementação específica do backend
    // Em produção, isso enviaria para Datadog, Prometheus, etc.
    logger.debug('Metric recorded', { name, value, tags });
  }

  alertSlowSpan(spanName, duration, attributes) {
    logger.warn('Slow span detected', {
      spanName,
      duration,
      threshold: config.apm.slowQueryThreshold,
      attributes,
    });
    
    // Em produção, dispararia um alerta
    if (duration > config.apm.slowQueryThreshold * 2) {
      this.triggerAlert('slow_span', {
        severity: 'sev2',
        message: `Span ${spanName} is very slow: ${duration}ms`,
        details: { spanName, duration, attributes },
      });
    }
  }

  triggerAlert(type, data) {
    // Será implementado no módulo de alertas
    logger.warn('Alert triggered', { type, data });
  }

  // Middleware para Express
  expressMiddleware() {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      // Ignorar paths de health check
      if (config.apm.ignorePaths.includes(req.path)) {
        return next();
      }
      
      const span = this.startSpan(`http.request`, {
        'http.method': req.method,
        'http.url': req.url,
        'http.route': req.route?.path || req.path,
        'http.user_agent': req.get('user-agent'),
        'http.client_ip': req.ip,
      });
      
      // Monkey patch res.end para capturar status code e duração
      const originalEnd = res.end;
      const startTime = Date.now();
      
      res.end = function(...args) {
        const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
        
        // Registrar métricas
        this.recordMetric('http.request.duration', duration, {
          method: req.method,
          route: req.route?.path || req.path,
          status_code: res.statusCode,
        });
        
        this.recordMetric('http.request.count', 1, {
          method: req.method,
          route: req.route?.path || req.path,
          status_code: res.statusCode,
        });
        
        // Finalizar span
        this.endSpan(span, res.statusCode < 500 ? 'ok' : 'error');
        
        return originalEnd.apply(res, args);
      }.bind(this);
      
      next();
    };
  }
}

module.exports = new APMInstrumentation();
```

## 3. Gerenciador de SLOs (src/slo/slo-manager.js)

```javascript
// src/slo/slo-manager.js
const config = require('../../config/monitoring-config');
const logger = require('../instrumentation/logger');

class SLOManager {
  constructor() {
    this.slos = config.slos;
    this.errorBudgets = new Map();
    this.sliData = new Map();
    this.initErrorBudgets();
  }

  initErrorBudgets() {
    // Inicializar error budgets para cada SLO
    Object.keys(this.slos).forEach(sloName => {
      const slo = this.slos[sloName];
      const errorBudget = this.calculateInitialErrorBudget(slo);
      
      this.errorBudgets.set(sloName, {
        current: errorBudget,
        initial: errorBudget,
        consumed: 0,
        burnRate: 0,
        lastUpdated: Date.now(),
      });
    });
    
    logger.info('Error budgets initialized');
  }

  calculateInitialErrorBudget(slo) {
    // Calcular error budget baseado no SLO
    if (slo.target && slo.window) {
      // Para disponibilidade: (100 - target) * window em minutos
      if (slo.target >= 99) {
        const downtimeAllowed = (100 - slo.target) / 100;
        let windowMinutes;
        
        if (slo.window.includes('d')) {
          windowMinutes = parseInt(slo.window) * 24 * 60;
        } else if (slo.window.includes('h')) {
          windowMinutes = parseInt(slo.window) * 60;
        } else {
          windowMinutes = parseInt(slo.window);
        }
        
        return downtimeAllowed * windowMinutes;
      }
    }
    
    return 100; // Default
  }

  recordSLI(sliName, value, isGood = true) {
    try {
      const timestamp = Date.now();
      const sliKey = `${sliName}_${timestamp}`;
      
      if (!this.sliData.has(sliName)) {
        this.sliData.set(sliName, {
          values: [],
          timestamps: [],
          goodCount: 0,
          totalCount: 0,
        });
      }
      
      const sli = this.sliData.get(sliName);
      sli.values.push(value);
      sli.timestamps.push(timestamp);
      sli.totalCount++;
      
      if (isGood) {
        sli.goodCount++;
      }
      
      // Manter apenas dados das últimas 24 horas
      const twentyFourHoursAgo = timestamp - (24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
      const recentIndices = sli.timestamps.map((ts, idx) => ts > twentyFourHoursAgo ? idx : -1)
        .filter(idx => idx !== -1);
      
      if (recentIndices.length > 0) {
        this.sliData.set(sliName, {
          values: recentIndices.map(idx => sli.values[idx]),
          timestamps: recentIndices.map(idx => sli.timestamps[idx]),
          goodCount: recentIndices.filter(idx => sli.values[idx] !== undefined && 
            this.isGoodValue(sliName, sli.values[idx])).length,
          totalCount: recentIndices.length,
        });
      }
      
      // Atualizar error budgets
      this.updateErrorBudgets();
      
      logger.debug('SLI recorded', { sliName, value, isGood });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to record SLI', { error: error.message, sliName });
    }
  }

  isGoodValue(sliName, value) {
    // Determinar se um valor é "bom" baseado no SLO
    switch (sliName) {
      case 'availability':
        return value >= (this.slos.availability.target / 100);
      case 'latency_p95':
        return value <= this.slos.latency.p95;
      case 'error_rate':
        return value <= this.slos.errorRate.target;
      default:
        return true;
    }
  }

  updateErrorBudgets() {
    Object.keys(this.slos).forEach(sloName => {
      const errorBudget = this.errorBudgets.get(sloName);
      const sliName = this.getSLINameForSLO(sloName);
      const sliData = this.sliData.get(sliName);
      
      if (sliData && sliData.totalCount > 0) {
        const sliValue = this.calculateSLIValue(sliName, sliData);
        const isGood = this.isGoodValue(sliName, sliValue);
        
        if (!isGood) {
          // Consumir error budget
          const consumptionRate = this.calculateConsumptionRate(sloName, sliValue);
          errorBudget.consumed += consumptionRate;
          errorBudget.current = errorBudget.initial - errorBudget.consumed;
          errorBudget.b

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Análise de Arquitetura e Decisões Técnicas

## ADR-001: Análise de Arquitetura V12 e Definição de Padrões para V13

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Especialista Infra + Especialista Backend

## CONTEXTO:
A V12 do DIYAPP evoluiu organicamente para atender demandas crescentes, mas apresenta pontos críticos que comprometem a estabilidade em cenários de alta carga. O sistema opera com 98% de uptime, mas os 2% de downtime causam impacto significativo devido à natureza crítica das operações. A análise revela:

1. **Monólito acoplado**: Serviços críticos compartilham recursos sem isolamento
2. **SPOFs identificados**: Banco de dados central, serviço de autenticação, fila de mensagens única
3. **Resiliência limitada**: Falta de circuit breakers, retry policies estruturadas e fallbacks
4. **Observabilidade fragmentada**: Métricas dispersas em múltiplos sistemas

## DECISÃO:
Implementar arquitetura de microsserviços com padrões de resiliência para a V13, mantendo compatibilidade retroativa durante transição gradual.

## OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:

### Opção A: Refatoração incremental do monólito
- **Prós**: Menor risco imediato, custo inicial reduzido, equipe familiarizada
- **Contras**: SPOFs permanecem, escalabilidade limitada, débito técnico acumulado
- **Complexidade**: Baixa/Média

### Opção B: Microsserviços completos com reescrita
- **Prós**: Isolamento total, escalabilidade independente, resiliência nativa
- **Contras**: Alto custo, curva de aprendizado, risco de regressões
- **Complexidade**: Alta

### Opção C: Estratificação progressiva (ESCOLHIDA)
- **Prós**: Mitigação de risco, aprendizado incremental, SPOFs resolvidos prioritariamente
- **Contras**: Overhead de compatibilidade, complexidade de deploy híbrido
- **Complexidade**: Média/Alta

**Justificativa**: A Opção C permite resolver SPOFs críticos primeiro (autenticação, banco) enquanto mantém sistema operacional. Usaremos Modo Hive para refatoração paralela.

## ANÁLISE TÉCNICA DETALHADA

### 1. Pontos Únicos de Falha (SPOF) Identificados

### 3. Padrões de Resiliência para V13

```javascript
// Arquitetura: src/architecture/resilience-patterns.js

// Circuit Breaker Pattern
class CircuitBreaker {
  constructor(service, options = {}) {
    this.service = service;
    this.failureThreshold = options.failureThreshold || 5;
    this.resetTimeout = options.resetTimeout || 30000;
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.lastFailureTime = null;
  }

  async call(request) {
    if (this.state === 'OPEN') {
      if (Date.now() - this.lastFailureTime > this.resetTimeout) {
        this.state = 'HALF_OPEN';
      } else {
        throw new Error('Circuit breaker OPEN - service unavailable');
      }
    }

    try {
      const response = await this.service(request);
      this.#reset();
      return response;
    } catch (error) {
      this.#recordFailure();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  #recordFailure() {
    this.failureCount++;
    this.lastFailureTime = Date.now();
    
    if (this.failureCount >= this.failureThreshold) {
      this.state = 'OPEN';
      console.warn(`Circuit breaker OPEN for ${this.service.name}`);
    }
  }

  #reset() {
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
  }
}

// Retry Policy with Exponential Backoff
class RetryPolicy {
  constructor(options = {}) {
    this.maxAttempts = options.maxAttempts || 3;
    this.baseDelay = options.baseDelay || 100;
    this.maxDelay = options.maxDelay || 10000;
    this.retryableErrors = options.retryableErrors || ['ECONNRESET', 'ETIMEDOUT'];
  }

  async execute(operation) {
    let lastError;
    
    for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= this.maxAttempts; attempt++) {
      try {
        return await operation();
      } catch (error) {
        lastError = error;
        
        if (!this.#shouldRetry(error) || attempt === this.maxAttempts) {
          break;
        }
        
        const delay = this.#calculateDelay(attempt);
        await this.#sleep(delay);
        console.log(`Retry attempt ${attempt + 1} after ${delay}ms`);
      }
    }
    
    throw lastError;
  }

  #shouldRetry(error) {
    return this.retryableErrors.some(code => error.code === code);
  }

  #calculateDelay(attempt) {
    const delay = Math.min(
      this.maxDelay,
      this.baseDelay * Math.pow(2, attempt - 1)
    );
    return delay + Math.random() * 100; // Jitter
  }

  #sleep(ms) {
    return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
  }
}

// Fallback Strategy
class FallbackStrategy {
  constructor(primary, fallback, fallbackCondition) {
    this.primary = primary;
    this.fallback = fallback;
    this.fallbackCondition = fallbackCondition || 
      (error => error.statusCode >= 500);
  }

  async execute(request) {
    try {
      return await this.primary(request);
    } catch (error) {
      if (this.fallbackCondition(error)) {
        console.warn('Primary failed, using fallback:', error.message);
        return await this.fallback(request);
      }
      throw error;
    }
  }
}

module.exports = { CircuitBreaker, RetryPolicy, FallbackStrategy };
```

### 4. Implementação de Health Checks

```javascript
// Arquivo: src/monitoring/health-check.js
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const redis = require('redis');

class HealthCheckService {
  constructor() {
    this.checks = [];
    this.dependencies = {
      database: new Pool({ /* config */ }),
      cache: redis.createClient(),
      externalApis: {
        payment: 'https://api.payment.com/health',
        email: 'https://api.email.com/status'
      }
    };
  }

  async #checkDatabase() {
    try {
      const result = await this.dependencies.database.query('SELECT 1');
      return {
        status: 'healthy',
        latency: result.duration,
        connections: this.dependencies.database.totalCount
      };
    } catch (error) {
      return {
        status: 'unhealthy',
        error: error.message
      };
    }
  }

  async #checkCache() {
    try {
      const start = Date.now();
      await this.dependencies.cache.ping();
      return {
        status: 'healthy',
        latency: Date.now() - start
      };
    } catch (error) {
      return {
        status: 'unhealthy',
        error: error.message
      };
    }
  }

  async #checkExternalApi(url, name) {
    try {
      const controller = new AbortController();
      const timeout = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), 5000);
      
      const response = await fetch(url, { 
        signal: controller.signal 
      });
      
      clearTimeout(timeout);
      
      return {
        status: response.ok ? 'healthy' : 'degraded',
        statusCode: response.status,
        latency: response.duration
      };
    } catch (error) {
      return {
        status: 'unhealthy',
        error: error.message
      };
    }
  }

  async getHealthStatus() {
    const checks = await Promise.all([
      this.#checkDatabase(),
      this.#checkCache(),
      ...Object.entries(this.dependencies.externalApis).map(([name, url]) =>
        this.#checkExternalApi(url, name)
      )
    ]);

    const overallStatus = checks.every(c => c.status === 'healthy') 
      ? 'healthy' 
      : checks.some(c => c.status === 'unhealthy') 
        ? 'unhealthy' 
        : 'degraded';

    return {
      status: overallStatus,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      checks: checks.reduce((acc, check, index) => {
        acc[`check_${index}`] = check;
        return acc;
      }, {})
    };
  }
}

// Health check endpoints
router.get('/health', async (req, res) => {
  const healthService = new HealthCheckService();
  const status = await healthService.getHealthStatus();
  
  res.status(status.status === 'healthy' ? 200 : 503).json(status);
});

router.get('/health/readiness', async (req, res) => {
  // Check if service is ready to receive traffic
  const healthService = new HealthCheckService();
  const status = await healthService.getHealthStatus();
  
  const ready = status.status === 'healthy' || status.status === 'degraded';
  res.status(ready ? 200 : 503).json({
    ready,
    ...status
  });
});

router.get('/health/liveness', (req, res) => {
  // Simple check if process is alive
  res.json({
    status: 'alive',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    pid: process.pid,
    memory: process.memoryUsage()
  });
});

module.exports = router;
```

};
```

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Sistema de Design

Como UX Designer sênior da squad, vou auditar a interface V12 e criar um sistema de design completo para V13 com foco em acessibilidade, microinterações e feedback visual. Vou implementar um protótipo funcional que simula o ambiente Figma.

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```javascript
// src/services/core/BaseService.js
/**
 * Classe base para todos os serviços da V13 Core
 * Implementa padrões de resiliência, logging estruturado e health checks
 */
class BaseService {
    constructor(serviceName, dependencies = {}) {
        this.serviceName = serviceName;
        this.dependencies = dependencies;
        this.circuitState = 'CLOSED';
        this.failureCount = 0;
        this.lastFailureTime = null;
        this.successCount = 0;
        this.circuitResetTimeout = 30000; // 30 segundos
        this.circuitThreshold = 5; // 5 falhas consecutivas abrem o circuito
        this.metrics = {
            requests: 0,
            errors: 0,
            latency: [],
            businessEvents: {}
        };
    }

    /**
     * Executa operação com resiliência embutida
     */
    async executeWithResilience(operation, operationName, options = {}) {
        const startTime = Date.now();
        const correlationId = this.generateCorrelationId();
        const operationId = `${this.serviceName}.${operationName}`;
        
        this.logStructured({
            level: 'info',
            correlationId,
            service: this.serviceName,
            operation: operationName,
            event: 'start',
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });

        try {
            // Verifica estado do circuit breaker
            if (this.circuitState === 'OPEN') {
                const timeSinceFailure = Date.now() - this.lastFailureTime;
                if (timeSinceFailure > this.circuitResetTimeout) {
                    this.circuitState = 'HALF_OPEN';
                    this.logStructured({
                        level: 'warn',
                        correlationId,
                        service: this.serviceName,
                        operation: operationName,
                        event: 'circuit_half_open',
                        message: 'Tentando recuperação após timeout'
                    });
                } else {
                    throw new CircuitBreakerOpenError(
                        `Circuit breaker aberto para ${operationId}`,
                        { retryAfter: this.circuitResetTimeout - timeSinceFailure }
                    );
                }
            }

            // Configura timeout
            const timeoutMs = options.timeout || 10000;
            const timeoutPromise = new Promise((_, reject) => {
                setTimeout(() => reject(new TimeoutError(
                    `Timeout após ${timeoutMs}ms em ${operationId}`
                )), timeoutMs);
            });

            // Executa operação com timeout
            const result = await Promise.race([
                operation(),
                timeoutPromise
            ]);

            // Registra sucesso
            const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
            this.recordSuccess(duration);
            
            this.logStructured({
                level: 'info',
                correlationId,
                service: this.serviceName,
                operation: operationName,
                event: 'success',
                durationMs: duration,
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
            });

            this.trackBusinessMetric(operationName, 'success', 1);
            
            return result;

        } catch (error) {
            const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
            this.recordFailure(error, duration);
            
            // Log estruturado do erro
            this.logStructured({
                level: error.isOperational ? 'warn' : 'error',
                correlationId,
                service: this.serviceName,
                operation: operationName,
                event: 'failure',
                errorType: error.constructor.name,
                errorMessage: error.message,
                errorCode: error.code,
                durationMs: duration,
                stack: error.stack,
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                isRetryable: this.isRetryableError(error)
            });

            this.trackBusinessMetric(operationName, 'failure', 1);

            // Executa fallback se disponível
            if (options.fallback) {
                this.logStructured({
                    level: 'info',
                    correlationId,
                    service: this.serviceName,
                    operation: operationName,
                    event: 'fallback_triggered',
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                });
                
                try {
                    return await options.fallback();
                } catch (fallbackError) {
                    throw new ServiceDegradationError(
                        `Serviço ${operationId} degradado. Fallback também falhou.`,
                        { originalError: error, fallbackError }
                    );
                }
            }

            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Implementa retry com backoff exponencial
     */
    async executeWithRetry(operation, operationName, options = {}) {
        const maxRetries = options.maxRetries || 3;
        const baseDelay = options.baseDelay || 100;
        const maxDelay = options.maxDelay || 10000;
        
        let lastError;
        
        for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt++) {
            try {
                if (attempt > 0) {
                    const delay = Math.min(
                        baseDelay * Math.pow(2, attempt - 1) + Math.random() * 100,
                        maxDelay
                    );
                    
                    this.logStructured({
                        level: 'info',
                        service: this.serviceName,
                        operation: operationName,
                        event: 'retry_attempt',
                        attempt,
                        delayMs: delay,
                        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                    });
                    
                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
                }
                
                return await this.executeWithResilience(operation, operationName, options);
                
            } catch (error) {
                lastError = error;
                
                if (!this.isRetryableError(error) || attempt === maxRetries) {
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        
        throw lastError;
    }

    /**
     * Health check detalhado do serviço
     */
    async healthCheck() {
        const health = {
            service: this.serviceName,
            status: 'healthy',
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            uptime: process.uptime(),
            circuitState: this.circuitState,
            metrics: {
                requests: this.metrics.requests,
                errors: this.metrics.errors,
                errorRate: this.metrics.requests > 0 ? 
                    (this.metrics.errors / this.metrics.requests) * 100 : 0,
                avgLatency: this.calculateAverageLatency(),
                p95Latency: this.calculatePercentileLatency(95),
                p99Latency: this.calculatePercentileLatency(99)
            },
            dependencies: {}
        };

        // Verifica dependências
        for (const [depName, depService] of Object.entries(this.dependencies)) {
            try {
                if (depService.healthCheck) {
                    health.dependencies[depName] = await depService.healthCheck();
                } else {
                    health.dependencies[depName] = { status: 'unknown', reason: 'No health check method' };
                }
            } catch (error) {
                health.dependencies[depName] = {
                    status: 'unhealthy',
                    error: error.message,
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                };
                
                if (depName in this.dependencies) {
                    health.status = 'degraded';
                }
            }
        }

        // Verifica se há muitas falhas recentes
        if (this.failureCount > this.circuitThreshold * 2) {
            health.status = 'degraded';
            health.warning = 'High failure rate detected';
        }

        return health;
    }

    /**
     * Métricas de negócio customizadas
     */
    trackBusinessMetric(operation, event, value = 1) {
        if (!this.metrics.businessEvents[operation]) {
            this.metrics.businessEvents[operation] = {};
        }
        
        if (!this.metrics.businessEvents[operation][event]) {
            this.metrics.businessEvents[operation][event] = 0;
        }
        
        this.metrics.businessEvents[operation][event] += value;
        
        // Log para sistema de métricas
        this.logStructured({
            level: 'info',
            service: this.serviceName,
            event: 'business_metric',
            operation,
            metric: event,
            value,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
    }

    /**
     * Gera métricas para Prometheus/OpenMetrics
     */
    getPrometheusMetrics() {
        const metrics = [];
        
        // Métricas de contador
        metrics.push(`# HELP ${this.serviceName}_requests_total Total de requisições`);
        metrics.push(`# TYPE ${this.serviceName}_requests_total counter`);
        metrics.push(`${this.serviceName}_requests_total ${this.metrics.requests}`);
        
        metrics.push(`# HELP ${this.serviceName}_errors_total Total de erros`);
        metrics.push(`# TYPE ${this.serviceName}_errors_total counter`);
        metrics.push(`${this.serviceName}_errors_total ${this.metrics.errors}`);
        
        // Métricas de latência
        if (this.metrics.latency.length > 0) {
            const sortedLatency = [...this.metrics.latency].sort((a, b) => a - b);
            
            metrics.push(`# HELP ${this.serviceName}_latency_seconds Latência das operações`);
            metrics.push(`# TYPE ${this.serviceName}_latency_seconds histogram`);
            
            // Buckets para histograma
            const buckets = [0.1, 0.3, 0.5, 1, 2, 5];
            let bucketCount = 0;
            
            buckets.forEach((bucket, i) => {
                const count = sortedLatency.filter(l => l <= bucket * 1000).length;
                const inc = count - bucketCount;
                bucketCount = count;
                metrics.push(`${this.serviceName}_latency_seconds_bucket{le="${bucket}"} ${count}`);
            });
            
            metrics.push(`${this.serviceName}_latency_seconds_bucket{le="+Inf"} ${sortedLatency.length}`);
            metrics.push(`${this.serviceName}_latency_seconds_sum ${sortedLatency.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / 1000}`);
            metrics.push(`${this.serviceName}_latency_seconds_count ${sortedLatency.length}`);
        }
        
        // Métricas de negócio
        Object.entries(this.metrics.businessEvents).forEach(([operation, events]) => {
            Object.entries(events).forEach(([event, count]) => {
                const metricName = `${this.serviceName}_${operation}_${event}_total`
                    .replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, '_')
                    .toLowerCase();
                
                metrics.push(`# HELP ${metricName} Business metric: ${operation} - ${event}`);
                metrics.push(`# TYPE ${metricName} counter`);
                metrics.push(`${metricName} ${count}`);
            });
        });
        
        return metrics.join('\n');
    }

    // Métodos auxiliares
    recordSuccess(duration) {
        this.metrics.requests++;
        this.metrics.latency.push(duration);
        
        if (this.circuitState === 'HALF_OPEN') {
            this.circuitState = 'CLOSED';
            this.failureCount = 0;
        }
        
        this.successCount++;
        
        // Mantém apenas últimas 1000 medições de latência
        if (this.metrics.latency.length > 1000) {
            this.metrics.latency = this.metrics.latency.slice(-1000);
        }
    }

    recordFailure(error, duration) {
        this.metrics.requests++;
        this.metrics.errors++;
        this.metrics.latency.push(duration);
        
        this.failureCount++;
        this.successCount = 0;
        this.lastFailureTime = Date.now();
        
        if (this.failureCount >= this.circuitThreshold) {
            this.circuitState = 'OPEN';
            this.logStructured({
                level: 'error',
                service: this.serviceName,
                event: 'circuit_opened',
                failureCount: this.failureCount,
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
            });
        }
    }

    isRetryableError(error) {
        // Erros retentáveis: timeouts, 5xx, network errors
        return error instanceof TimeoutError ||
               (error.code && error.code >= 500) ||
               error.name === 'NetworkError' ||
               error.message?.includes('ECONNRESET') ||
               error.message?.includes('ETIMEDOUT');
    }

    calculateAverageLatency() {
        if (this.metrics.latency.length === 0) return 0;
        return this.metrics.latency.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / this.metrics.latency.length;
    }

    calculatePercentileLatency(percentile) {
        if (this.metrics.latency.length === 0) return 0;
        
        const sorted = [...this.metrics.latency].sort((a, b) => a - b);
        const index = Math.ceil((percentile / 100) * sorted.length) - 1;
        return sorted[Math.max(0, index)];
    }

    generateCorrelationId() {
        return `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
    }

    logStructured(logEntry) {
        // Em produção, enviar para sistema centralizado (ELK, Datadog, etc.)
        // Aqui apenas logamos no console em formato JSON
        console.log(JSON.stringify({
            ...logEntry,
            pid: process.pid,
            hostname: require('os').hostname(),
            env: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development'
        }));
    }
}

// src/services/core/errors/ResilienceErrors.js
class CircuitBreakerOpenError extends Error {
    constructor(message, metadata = {}) {
        super(message);
        this.name = 'CircuitBreakerOpenError';
        this.code = 'CIRCUIT_BREAKER_OPEN';
        this.isOperational = true;
        this.metadata = metadata;
        this.retryAfter = metadata.retryAfter;
    }
}

class TimeoutError extends Error {
    constructor(message) {
        super(message);
        this.name = 'TimeoutError';
        this.code = 'TIMEOUT';
        this.isOperational = true;
    }
}

class ServiceDegradationError extends Error {
    constructor(message, metadata = {}) {
        super(message);
        this.name = 'ServiceDegradationError';
        this.code = 'SERVICE_DEGRADED';
        this.isOperational = true;
        this.metadata = metadata;
    }
}

// src/services/PaymentService.js (Exemplo de serviço refatorado)
class PaymentService extends BaseService {
    constructor(paymentGateway, notificationService) {
        super('PaymentService', {
            gateway: paymentGateway,
            notifications: notificationService
        });
        
        this.paymentGateway = paymentGateway;
        this.notificationService = notificationService;
    }

    async processPayment(paymentData, userId) {
        const correlationId = this.generateCorrelationId();
        
        return this.executeWithRetry(
            async () => {
                // Validação de input
                this.validatePaymentData(paymentData);
                
                // Processa pagamento
                const result = await this.paymentGateway.charge(
                    paymentData.amount,
                    paymentData.token,
                    { correlationId, userId }
                );
                
                // Registra transação
                await this.recordTransaction(result, userId);
                
                // Envia notificação (fire and forget)
                this.notificationService.sendPaymentConfirmation(userId, result)
                    .catch(error => {
                        this.logStructured({
                            level: 'error',
                            correlationId,
                            service: this.serviceName,
                            operation: 'sendNotification',
                            event: 'async_failure',
                            error: error.message,
                            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                        });
                    });
                
                // Métrica de negócio
                this.trackBusinessMetric('processPayment', 'transaction_completed', paymentData.amount);
                
                return result;
            },
            'processPayment',
            {
                timeout: 30000, // 30 segundos para pagamento
                maxRetries: 2,
                baseDelay: 1000,
                fallback: () => this.fallbackPayment(paymentData, userId)
            }
        );
    }

    async validatePaymentData(paymentData) {
        // Implementação de validação
        if (!paymentData.amount || paymentData.amount <= 0) {
            throw new ValidationError('Amount must be positive');
        }
        
        if (!paymentData.token || paymentData.token.length < 10) {
            throw new ValidationError('Invalid payment token');
        }
    }

    async recordTransaction(result, userId) {
        // Implementação de persistência
        // Usa queries parametrizadas
        const query = `
            INSERT INTO transactions 
            (id, user_id, amount, status, gateway_id, created_at)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
        `;
        
        // Simulação - em produção usar driver de banco com parâmetros
        const params = [
            result.transactionId,
            userId,
            result.amount,
            result.status,
            result.gatewayId,
            new Date().toISOString()
        ];
        
        this.logStructured({
            level: 'debug',
            service: this.serviceName,
            operation: 'recordTransaction',
            event: 'db_query',
            query: query.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim(),
            params: this.maskSensitiveData(params), // Mascara dados sensíveis
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
    }

    async fallbackPayment(paymentData, userId) {
        // Fallback: marca como pendente e agenda retry
        this.logStructured({
            level: 'warn',
            service: this.serviceName,
            operation: 'fallbackPayment',
            event: 'fallback_activated',
            userId,
            amount: paymentData.amount,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
        
        return {
            status: 'pending',
            transactionId: `pending-${Date.now()}-${userId}`,
            message: 'Payment processing delayed. Will retry shortly.',
            requiresManualReview: false
        };
    }

    maskSensitiveData(data) {
        // Mascara dados sensíveis para logs
        if (Array.isArray(data)) {
            return data.map(item => {
                if (typeof item === 'string' && (
                    item.includes('@') || // email
                    item.match(/^\d{3}\.\d{3}\.\d{3}-\d{2}$/) || // CPF
                    item.match(/^\d{16}$/) // cartão

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Sistema de Design

Vou implementar o novo sistema de design V13 com componentes React, focando em performance, acessibilidade e fidelidade ao design. Vou criar um sistema completo com tokens de design, componentes reutilizáveis, skeleton screens e otimizações de performance.

```javascript
// Estrutura do projeto
// diyapp-v13-design-system/
// ├── src/
// │   ├── design-system/
// │   │   ├── tokens/
// │   │   ├── components/
// │   │   ├── hooks/
// │   │   └── utils/
// │   ├── pages/
// │   └── App.jsx
// ├── public/
// └── index.html
```

// Hook para tema (claro/escuro)
export const useTheme = () => {
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState('light');
  
  useEffect(() => {
    const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('theme') || 'light';
    const prefersDark = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
    
    setTheme(savedTheme === 'auto' && prefersDark ? 'dark' : savedTheme);
    
    // Aplicar tema ao documento
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', theme);
  }, [theme]);
  
  const toggleTheme = () => {
    const newTheme = theme === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light';
    setTheme(newTheme);
    localStorage.setItem('theme', newTheme);
  };
  
  return { theme, toggleTheme };
};

## 2. Componentes Base (design-system/components/)

### 2.1 Button Component
```jsx
// design-system/components/Button/Button.jsx
import React from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import { tokens } from '../../tokens';
import './Button.css';

const Button = React.forwardRef(({
  children,
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  isLoading = false,
  disabled = false,
  fullWidth = false,
  startIcon,
  endIcon,
  onClick,
  type = 'button',
  className = '',
  ...props
}, ref) => {
  const baseClasses = `
    diyapp-button
    diyapp-button--${variant}
    diyapp-button--${size}
    ${isLoading ? 'diyapp-button--loading' : ''}
    ${fullWidth ? 'diyapp-button--full-width' : ''}
    ${className}
  `.trim();
  
  const handleClick = (e) => {
    if (!disabled && !isLoading && onClick) {
      onClick(e);
    }
  };
  
  return (
    <button
      ref={ref}
      type={type}
      className={baseClasses}
      disabled={disabled || isLoading}
      onClick={handleClick}
      aria-busy={isLoading}
      {...props}
    >
      {isLoading && (
        <span className="diyapp-button__loader" aria-hidden="true">
          <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none">
            <circle cx="8" cy="8" r="7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeOpacity="0.3" />
            <path d="M15 8a7 7 0 0 1-7 7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" />
          </svg>
        </span>
      )}
      
      {startIcon && !isLoading && (
        <span className="diyapp-button__icon diyapp-button__icon--start">
          {startIcon}
        </span>
      )}
      
      <span className="diyapp-button__content">
        {children}
      </span>
      
      {endIcon && !isLoading && (
        <span className="diyapp-button__icon diyapp-button__icon--end">
          {endIcon}
        </span>
      )}
    </button>
  );
});

Button.propTypes = {
  children: PropTypes.node.isRequired,
  variant: PropTypes.oneOf(['primary', 'secondary', 'outline', 'ghost', 'danger']),
  size: PropTypes.oneOf(['sm', 'md', 'lg']),
  isLoading: PropTypes.bool,
  disabled: PropTypes.bool,
  fullWidth: PropTypes.bool,
  startIcon: PropTypes.node,
  endIcon: PropTypes.node,
  onClick: PropTypes.func,
  type: PropTypes.oneOf(['button', 'submit', 'reset']),
  className: PropTypes.string,
};

export default Button;
```

### 2.2 Skeleton Component
```jsx
// design-system/components/Skeleton/Skeleton.jsx
import React from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import './Skeleton.css';

const Skeleton = ({
  variant = 'text',
  width,
  height,
  borderRadius = 'md',
  animation = 'pulse',
  className = '',
  ...props
}) => {
  const baseClasses = `
    diyapp-skeleton
    diyapp-skeleton--${variant}
    diyapp-skeleton--${animation}
    ${className}
  `.trim();
  
  const style = {
    width: width || undefined,
    height: height || undefined,
    borderRadius: `var(--radius-${borderRadius})`,
  };
  
  return (
    <div
      className={baseClasses}
      style={style}
      aria-hidden="true"
      {...props}
    />
  );
};

Skeleton.propTypes = {
  variant: PropTypes.oneOf(['text', 'circular', 'rectangular']),
  width: PropTypes.oneOfType([PropTypes.string, PropTypes.number]),
  height: PropTypes.oneOfType([PropTypes.string, PropTypes.number]),
  borderRadius: PropTypes.oneOf(['sm', 'md', 'lg', 'xl', 'full']),
  animation: PropTypes.oneOf(['pulse', 'wave', 'none']),
  className: PropTypes.string,
};

// Componente composto para carregamento de conteúdo
export const SkeletonGroup = ({ children, isLoading, skeletonCount = 1 }) => {
  if (isLoading) {
    return (
      <div className="diyapp-skeleton-group" aria-busy="true">
        {Array.from({ length: skeletonCount }).map((_, index) => (
          <React.Fragment key={index}>
            {children}
          </React.Fragment>
        ))}
      </div>
    );
  }
  
  return children;
};

export default Skeleton;
```

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Sistema de Monitoramento SRE

Vou configurar um sistema completo de monitoramento SRE para a V13, incluindo APM, logs, dashboards, SLOs/SLIs e alertas baseados em anomalias.

## 2. Definições de SLOs/SLIs

**src/monitoring/datadog/slos/slo_definitions.yaml**

```yaml
# DIYAPP V13 - SLO Definitions
version: "1.0"
app_name: "DIYAPP V13"
squad: "Autonomous AI Squad"

slo_definitions:
  # API Availability SLO
  - name: "api_availability"
    description: "API HTTP availability for all endpoints"
    sli_type: "metric"
    metric_query: "sum:http.requests{service:diyapp-api,env:production}.as_count() / sum:http.requests{service:diyapp-api,env:production}.as_count()"
    target: 0.9995  # 99.95%
    time_window: "30d"
    tags:
      - service:diyapp-api
      - slo_type:availability
      - critical:true

  # API Latency SLO (P95)
  - name: "api_latency_p95"
    description: "95th percentile latency for API endpoints"
    sli_type: "metric"
    metric_query: "p95:http.request.duration{service:diyapp-api,env:production}"
    target: 0.2  # 200ms
    time_window: "30d"
    tags:
      - service:diyapp-api
      - slo_type:latency
      - critical:true

  # Error Rate SLO
  - name: "api_error_rate"
    description: "HTTP 5xx error rate"
    sli_type: "metric"
    metric_query: "sum:http.requests{status_code:5xx,service:diyapp-api,env:production}.as_count() / sum:http.requests{service:diyapp-api,env:production}.as_count()"
    target: 0.001  # 0.1%
    time_window: "30d"
    tags:
      - service:diyapp-api
      - slo_type:error_rate
      - critical:true

  # LLM Latency SLO
  - name: "llm_latency_p95"
    description: "95th percentile latency for LLM completions"
    sli_type: "metric"
    metric_query: "p95:llm.request.duration{service:diyapp-llm,env:production}"
    target: 8.0  # 8 seconds
    time_window: "30d"
    tags:
      - service:diyapp-llm
      - slo_type:latency
      - critical:true

  # LLM Availability SLO
  - name: "llm_availability"
    description: "LLM service availability"
    sli_type: "metric"
    metric_query: "sum:llm.requests{service:diyapp-llm,env:production,status:success}.as_count() / sum:llm.requests{service:diyapp-llm,env:production}.as_count()"
    target: 0.999  # 99.9%
    time_window: "30d"
    tags:
      - service:diyapp-llm
      - slo_type:availability
      - critical:true

  # Database Connection SLO
  - name: "db_connection_pool"
    description: "Database connection pool health"
    sli_type: "metric"
    metric_query: "avg:postgresql.connections.active{env:production} / avg:postgresql.connections.max{env:production}"
    target: 0.8  # 80% max utilization
    time_window: "30d"
    tags:
      - service:postgresql
      - slo_type:utilization
      - critical:true

  # Cache Hit Rate SLO
  - name: "cache_hit_rate"
    description: "Redis cache hit rate"
    sli_type: "metric"
    metric_query: "sum:redis.keyspace.hits{env:production}.as_count() / (sum:redis.keyspace.hits{env:production}.as_count() + sum:redis.keyspace.misses{env:production}.as_count())"
    target: 0.95  # 95% hit rate
    time_window: "30d"
    tags:
      - service:redis
      - slo_type:performance
      - critical:false

# Error Budget Policy
error_budget_policy:
  monthly_budget: 0.001  # 0.1% error budget
  burn_rate_thresholds:
    - window: "1h"
      threshold: 14.4  # 14.4x burn rate
    - window: "6h"
      threshold: 6.0   # 6x burn rate
    - window: "24h"
      threshold: 3.0   # 3x burn rate
    - window: "72h"
      threshold: 1.0   # 1x burn rate
  
  alert_thresholds:
    warning: 0.5    # 50% budget remaining
    critical: 0.2   # 20% budget remaining
    exhausted: 0.0  # 0% budget remaining
  
  actions:
    - threshold: 0.5
      action: "Review recent deployments"
      notify: ["squad_leader", "sre"]
    - threshold: 0.2
      action: "Freeze feature deployments"
      notify: ["squad_leader", "pm", "sre", "devs"]
    - threshold: 0.0
      action: "Emergency response - All hands on deck"
      notify: ["squad_leader", "pm", "sre", "devs", "cto"]
```

## 3. Instrumentação da Aplicação

**src/monitoring/instrumentation/api_instrumentation.js**

```javascript
const tracer = require('dd-trace').init({
  service: 'diyapp-api',
  env: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'production',
  version: 'v13',
  logInjection: true,
  runtimeMetrics: true,
  profiling: true,
  analytics: true
});

const statsd = require('hot-shots');
const dogstatsd = new statsd({
  host: process.env.DD_AGENT_HOST || 'localhost',
  port: 8125,
  globalTags: {
    env: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'production',
    version: 'v13',
    service: 'diyapp-api'
  },
  errorHandler: error => {
    console.error('Datadog statsd error:', error);
  }
});

class APIMonitoring {
  constructor() {
    this.metrics = {
      requests: 'http.requests',
      duration: 'http.request.duration',
      errors: 'http.errors',
      latency: 'http.latency'
    };
  }

  /**
   * Instrument Express.js middleware
   */
  instrumentExpress(app) {
    const expressMonitoring = require('express');
    
    // Request counting middleware
    app.use((req, res, next) => {
      const startTime = Date.now();
      
      // Count request
      dogstatsd.increment(this.metrics.requests, 1, [
        `method:${req.method}`,
        `route:${req.route?.path || req.path}`,
        `status_code:${res.statusCode}`
      ]);
      
      // Record response time
      res.on('finish', () => {
        const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
        
        dogstatsd.histogram(this.metrics.duration, duration, 1, [
          `method:${req.method}`,
          `route:${req.route?.path || req.path}`,
          `status_code:${res.statusCode}`
        ]);
        
        // Track error rates
        if (res.statusCode >= 500) {
          dogstatsd.increment(this.metrics.errors, 1, [
            `method:${req.method}`,
            `route:${req.route?.path || req.path}`,
            `status_code:${res.statusCode}`
          ]);
        }
      });
      
      next();
    });
    
    // Health check endpoint with SLO monitoring
    app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
      const health = {
        status: 'healthy',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        version: 'v13',
        uptime: process.uptime(),
        checks: []
      };
      
      // Add database check
      health.checks.push({
        name: 'database',
        status: 'healthy',
        latency: 0
      });
      
      // Add cache check
      health.checks.push({
        name: 'redis',
        status: 'healthy',
        latency: 0
      });
      
      // Add external services check
      health.checks.push({
        name: 'external_services',
        status: 'healthy'
      });
      
      res.json(health);
      
      // Record health check
      dogstatsd.increment('health.check', 1, [
        'endpoint:/health',
        'status:healthy'
      ]);
    });
    
    // SLO metrics endpoint
    app.get('/metrics/slo', (req, res) => {
      const sloMetrics = this.getSLOMetrics();
      res.json(sloMetrics);
    });
    
    // Error budget endpoint
    app.get('/metrics/error-budget', (req, res) => {
      const errorBudget = this.calculateErrorBudget();
      res.json(errorBudget);
    });
  }

  /**
   * Track LLM requests
   */
  trackLLMRequest(provider, model, duration, success = true, tokens = 0) {
    const tags = [
      `provider:${provider}`,
      `model:${model}`,
      `success:${success}`,
      `env:${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'production'}`
    ];
    
    // Record LLM request duration
    dogstatsd.histogram('llm.request.duration', duration, 1, tags);
    
    // Count LLM requests
    dogstatsd.increment('llm.requests', 1, tags);
    
    // Track tokens if available
    if (tokens > 0) {
      dogstatsd.histogram('llm.tokens.total', tokens, 1, tags);
      dogstatsd.histogram('llm.tokens.per_second', tokens / (duration / 1000), 1, tags);
    }
    
    // Track errors
    if (!success) {
      dogstatsd.increment('llm.errors', 1, tags);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Track database operations
   */
  trackDatabaseOperation(operation, table, duration, success = true) {
    const tags = [
      `operation:${operation}`,
      `table:${table}`,
      `success:${success}`,
      `env:${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'production'}`
    ];
    
    dogstatsd.histogram('db.operation.duration', duration, 1, tags);
    dogstatsd.increment('db.operations', 1, tags);
    
    if (!success) {
      dogstatsd.increment('db.errors', 1, tags);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Track cache operations
   */
  trackCacheOperation(operation, key, hit, duration) {
    const tags = [
      `operation:${operation}`,
      `hit:${hit}`,
      `env:${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'production'}`
    ];
    
    dogstatsd.histogram('cache.operation.duration', duration, 1, tags);
    dogstatsd.increment(`cache.${hit ? 'hits' : 'misses'}`, 1, tags);
  }

  /**
   * Get current SLO metrics
   */
  getSLOMetrics() {
    // This would query Datadog API for actual metrics
    // For now, return mock data structure
    return {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      slos: {
        api_availability: {
          current: 0.9998,
          target: 0.9995,
          status: 'healthy',
          error_budget_remaining: 0.85
        },
        api_latency_p95: {
          current: 180,
          target: 200,
          status: 'healthy',
          error_budget_remaining: 0.92
        },
        api_error_rate: {
          current: 0.0005,
          target: 0.001,
          status: 'healthy',
          error_budget_remaining: 0.88
        },
        llm_latency_p95: {
          current: 6500,
          target: 8000,
          status: 'healthy',
          error_budget_remaining: 0.78
        }
      },
      overall_status: 'healthy'
    };
  }

  /**
   * Calculate error budget
   */
  calculateErrorBudget() {
    // This would calculate based on actual metrics
    // For now, return mock calculation
    return {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      period: '30d',
      total_budget: 0.001,
      consumed_budget: 0.00015,
      remaining_budget: 0.00085,
      remaining_percentage: 85,
      burn_rate: 0.5,
      status: 'healthy',
      recommendation: 'Normal operations'
    };
  }

  /**
   * Record custom business metric
   */
  recordBusinessMetric(name, value, tags = []) {
    const allTags = [
      ...tags,
      `env:${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'production'}`,
     

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Análise Arquitetural

const SPOF_REPORT = {
  critical: [
    {
      id: "SPOF-001",
      component: "MessageBroker",
      description: "RabbitMQ single instance sem cluster",
      impact: "Falha total do sistema se broker cair",
      location: "src/infra/message-broker.js",
      mitigation: "Implementar cluster RabbitMQ + mirroring"
    },
    {
      id: "SPOF-002",
      component: "Database",
      description: "PostgreSQL single master sem replicação",

      location: "src/database/connection.js",
      mitigation: "Setup master-slave com failover automático"
    },
    {
      id: "SPOF-003",
      component: "AuthService",
      description: "Serviço de autenticação centralizado",

    {
      id: "SPOF-004",
      component: "FileStorage",

  high: [

      id: "SPOF-005",
      component: "WebSocketServer",
      description: "WebSocket single instance",

      location: "src/websocket/server.js",
      mitigation: "Redis Pub/Sub para WebSocket clustering"
    }
  ]
};
