## 2. ADR: PADRÕES DE RESILIÊNCIA V13

```markdown
# ADR-013: Padrões de Resiliência para V13

Data: 2024-01-15
Status: Aceita
Autores: Tech Lead, Especialista Infra

## CONTEXTO:
A V12 apresenta múltiplos SPOFs e falta de padrões consistentes de resiliência.
Incidentes recentes mostraram:
1. Cascading failures quando serviços dependentes falham
2. Timeouts não tratados causando thread exhaustion
3. Retries infinitos criando DDoS interno
4. Ausência de fallback mechanisms

## DECISÃO:
Implementar padrão de resiliência baseado em:
1. Circuit Breaker para todas chamadas externas
2. Retry com backoff exponencial e jitter
3. Fallback strategies definidas por serviço
4. Bulkhead isolation por domínio de negócio
5. Health checks distribuídos

## OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:

### Opção A: Biblioteca única (resilience4j)
- Prós: Completa, bem testada, integração Spring
- Contras: Java-centric, overhead para Node.js
- Custo: Alto (learning curve)

### Opção B: Polly.js + custom implementation
- Prós: Específico para Node.js, flexível
- Contras: Manutenção customizada necessária
- Custo: Médio

### Opção C: Istio Service Mesh + circuit breaking nativo
- Prós: Infra-level, transparente para aplicação
- Contras: Complexidade operacional, custo cloud
- Custo: Alto

### Opção escolhida: B (Polly.js + custom)
Justificativa: 
- Melhor fit para stack Node.js atual
- Controle fino sobre políticas por serviço
- Custo operacional mais baixo que service mesh
- Pode evoluir para Opção C no futuro

## CONSEQUÊNCIAS:

### Positivas:
1. Isolamento de falhas entre serviços
2. Prevenção de cascading failures
3. Melhor UX com fallbacks elegantes
4. Métricas de resiliência observáveis

### Negativas:
1. Complexity increase no código
2. Latência adicional em circuitos abertos
3. Testing overhead para estados do circuit breaker

### Riscos:
1. Configuração incorreta pode mascarar problemas
2. Circuit breaker pode abrir desnecessariamente
   - Mitigação: Tuning baseado em métricas reais
3. Fallback logic pode se tornar complexa
   - Mitigação: Fallbacks simples (cache/static response)

## REVISÃO: 2024-04-15 (3 meses após implementação)
```

## 3. IMPLEMENTAÇÃO: CORE DE RESILIÊNCIA

```javascript
// Arquivo: src/core/resilience/ResilienceCore.js
/**
 * Core de Resiliência V13
 * Implementa circuit breaker, retry, fallback, bulkhead
 */

const Polly = require('@pollyjs/core').Polly;
const { CircuitBreaker, ConsecutiveBreaker } = require('@pollyjs/core').CircuitBreaker;
const { retry, handleWhen, exponentialBackoff } = require('@pollyjs/utils').retry;
const EventEmitter = require('events');
const metrics = require('../monitoring/metrics-collector');

class ResilienceCore extends EventEmitter {
  constructor(config = {}) {
    super();
    this.config = {
      circuitBreaker: {
        failureThreshold: 5,
        resetTimeout: 30000,
        halfOpenMaxCalls: 3,
        ...config.circuitBreaker
      },
      retry: {
        maxAttempts: 3,
        backoff: 'exponential',
        jitter: true,
        ...config.retry
      },
      bulkhead: {
        maxConcurrent: 10,
        maxQueue: 100,
        ...config.bulkhead
      }
    };
    
    this.circuits = new Map();
    this.bulkheads = new Map();
    this.healthChecks = new Map();
    
    this.initMetrics();
  }

  initMetrics() {
    metrics.registerGauge('circuit_state', 'Current state of circuit breaker', ['service']);
    metrics.registerCounter('circuit_transitions', 'Circuit state transitions', ['service', 'from', 'to']);
    metrics.registerHistogram('retry_attempts', 'Number of retry attempts per call', ['service']);
  }

  // Circuit Breaker Implementation
  createCircuit(serviceName, options = {}) {
    const circuitConfig = {
      ...this.config.circuitBreaker,
      ...options
    };

    const circuit = {
      state: 'CLOSED',
      failureCount: 0,
      successCount: 0,
      lastFailure: null,
      halfOpenCalls: 0,
      breaker: new CircuitBreaker(
        new ConsecutiveBreaker(circuitConfig.failureThreshold),
        circuitConfig.resetTimeout
      )
    };

    this.circuits.set(serviceName, circuit);
    
    // Estado inicial das métricas
    metrics.setGauge('circuit_state', 0, { service: serviceName });
    
    return {
      execute: async (fn) => {
        return await this.executeWithCircuit(serviceName, fn);
      },
      getState: () => circuit.state
    };
  }

  async executeWithCircuit(serviceName, fn) {
    const circuit = this.circuits.get(serviceName);
    
    if (!circuit) {
      throw new Error(`Circuit not found for service: ${serviceName}`);
    }

    // Verificar estado do circuito
    if (circuit.state === 'OPEN') {
      const now = Date.now();
      if (now - circuit.lastFailure > circuit.breaker.resetTimeout) {
        circuit.state = 'HALF_OPEN';
        circuit.halfOpenCalls = 0;
        metrics.incCounter('circuit_transitions', { 
          service: serviceName, 
          from: 'OPEN', 
          to: 'HALF_OPEN' 
        });
        metrics.setGauge('circuit_state', 1, { service: serviceName });
      } else {
        this.emit('circuitOpen', { service: serviceName });
        throw new Error(`Circuit OPEN for service: ${serviceName}`);
      }
    }

    try {
      // Executar com bulkhead se configurado
      const result = await this.executeWithBulkhead(serviceName, fn);
      
      // Registrar sucesso
      if (circuit.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
        circuit.halfOpenCalls++;
        if (circuit.halfOpenCalls >= this.config.circuitBreaker.halfOpenMaxCalls) {
          circuit.state = 'CLOSED';
          circuit.failureCount = 0;
          metrics.incCounter('circuit_transitions', { 
            service: serviceName, 
            from: 'HALF_OPEN', 
            to: 'CLOSED' 
          });
          metrics.setGauge('circuit_state', 0, { service: serviceName });
        }
      } else {
        circuit.successCount++;
        if (circuit.successCount > 10) {
          circuit.failureCount = Math.max(0, circuit.failureCount - 1);
        }
      }
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      // Registrar falha
      circuit.failureCount++;
      circuit.lastFailure = Date.now();
      
      if (circuit.state === 'HALF_OPEN' || 
          circuit.failureCount >= circuit.breaker.threshold) {
        circuit.state = 'OPEN';
        metrics.incCounter('circuit_transitions', { 
          service: serviceName, 
          from: circuit.state, 
          to: 'OPEN' 
        });
        metrics.setGauge('circuit_state', 2, { service: serviceName });
      }
      
      throw error;
    }
  }

  // Bulkhead Implementation
  async executeWithBulkhead(serviceName, fn) {
    const bulkhead = this.bulkheads.get(serviceName) || {
      concurrent: 0,
      queue: [],
      maxConcurrent: this.config.bulkhead.maxConcurrent,
      maxQueue: this.config.bulkhead.maxQueue
    };

    if (bulkhead.concurrent >= bulkhead.maxConcurrent) {
      if (bulkhead.queue.length >= bulkhead.maxQueue) {
        throw new Error(`Bulkhead queue full for service: ${serviceName}`);
      }
      
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        bulkhead.queue.push({ fn, resolve, reject });
      });
    }

    bulkhead.concurrent++;
    this.bulkheads.set(serviceName, bulkhead);

    try {
      const result = await fn();
      return result;
    } finally {
      bulkhead.concurrent--;
      
      // Processar próximo da fila
      if (bulkhead.queue.length > 0) {
        const next = bulkhead.queue.shift();
        setTimeout(() => {
          this.executeWithBulkhead(serviceName, next.fn)
            .then(next.resolve)
            .catch(next.reject);
        }, 0);
      }
    }
  }

  // Retry with Exponential Backoff
  async withRetry(serviceName, fn, context = {}) {
    const retryConfig = {
      ...this.config.retry,
      ...context.retryConfig
    };

    let lastError;
    let attempt = 0;

    while (attempt < retryConfig.maxAttempts) {
      attempt++;
      
      try {
        const result = await fn();
        metrics.observeHistogram('retry_attempts', attempt, { service: serviceName });
        return result;
      } catch (error) {
        lastError = error;
        
        // Verificar se erro é retryable
        if (!this.isRetryableError(error)) {
          break;
        }

        if (attempt < retryConfig.maxAttempts) {
          const delay = this.calculateBackoff(attempt, retryConfig);
          await this.delay(delay);
        }
      }
    }

    throw lastError;
  }

  isRetryableError(error) {
    const retryableStatusCodes = [408, 429, 500, 502, 503, 504];
    const retryableMessages = ['timeout', 'busy', 'unavailable', 'overload'];
    
    if (error.statusCode && retryableStatusCodes.includes(error.statusCode)) {
      return true;
    }
    
    if (error.message) {
      const lowerMessage = error.message.toLowerCase();
      return retryableMessages.some(msg => lowerMessage.includes(msg));
    }
    
    return false;
  }

  calculateBackoff(attempt, config) {
    let delay;
    
    switch (config.backoff) {
      case 'exponential':
        delay = Math.min(1000 * Math.pow(2, attempt), 30000);
        break;
      case 'linear':
        delay = 1000 * attempt;
        break;
      case 'fixed':
        delay = 2000;
        break;
      default:
        delay = 1000 * Math.pow(2, attempt);
    }
    
    if (config.jitter) {
      delay = delay * (0.8 + Math.random() * 0.4); // 0.8-1.2x
    }
    
    return delay;
  }

  delay(ms) {
    return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
  }

  // Fallback Strategies
  createFallbackStrategy(serviceName, strategies) {
    return {
      execute: async (primaryFn, context) => {
        try {
          return await primaryFn();
        } catch (error) {
          console.warn(`Primary function failed for ${serviceName}:`, error.message);
          
          // Tentar estratégias de fallback em ordem
          for (const strategy of strategies) {
            try {
              console.log(`Attempting fallback strategy: ${strategy.name}`);
              const result = await strategy.fn(context);
              
              this.emit('fallbackUsed', {
                service: serviceName,
                strategy: strategy.name,
                error: error.message
              });
              
              return result;
            } catch (fallbackError) {
              console.warn(`Fallback strategy ${strategy.name} failed:`, fallbackError.message);
              continue;
            }
          }
          
          throw new Error(`All fallback strategies failed for ${serviceName}`);
        }
      }
    };
  }

  // Health Check System
  registerHealthCheck(serviceName, checkFn, interval = 30000) {
    const healthCheck = {
      lastCheck: null,
      status: 'UNKNOWN',
      details: {},
      interval
    };

    this.healthChecks.set(serviceName, healthCheck);

    // Executar check inicial
    this.runHealthCheck(serviceName, checkFn);

    // Agendar checks periódicos
    const timer = setInterval(() => {
      this.runHealthCheck(serviceName, checkFn);
    }, interval);

    return () => clearInterval(timer);
  }

  async runHealthCheck(serviceName, checkFn) {
    try {
      const result = await checkFn();
      
      const healthCheck = this.healthChecks.get(serviceName);
      healthCheck.lastCheck = new Date();
      healthCheck.status = 'HEALTHY';
      healthCheck.details = result;
      
      this.emit('healthCheck', {
        service: serviceName,
        status: 'HEALTHY',
        timestamp: healthCheck.lastCheck
      });
    } catch (error) {
      const healthCheck = this.healthChecks.get(serviceName);
      healthCheck.lastCheck = new Date();
      healthCheck.status = 'UNHEALTHY';
      healthCheck.details = { error: error.message };
      
      this.emit('healthCheck', {
        service: serviceName,
        status: 'UNHEALTHY',
        error: error.message,
        timestamp: healthCheck.lastCheck
      });
    }
  }

  getHealthStatus(serviceName = null) {
    if (serviceName) {
      return this.healthChecks.get(serviceName) || { status: 'UNREGISTERED' };
    }
    
    const allStatus = {};
    for (const [name, check] of this.healthChecks) {
      allStatus[name] = {
        status: check.status,
        lastCheck: check.lastCheck
      };
    }
    
    return allStatus;
  }
}

module.exports = ResilienceCore;
```

        <div class="audit-section recommendations">

            <div class="recommendation-item">
                <i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i>
                <div>
                    <strong>Implementar Design Tokens sistemáticos:</strong> Definir escala de cores com contraste WCAG AA garantido, escala de espaçamento baseada em 4px/8px, e tokens tipográficos.
                </div>

                </div>

                <i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i>
                <div>
                    <strong>Garantir acessibilidade por padrão:</strong> Todos os componentes devem seguir WCAG 2.1 AA, com foco visível, ARIA labels e áreas de toque adequadas.
                </div>

                <i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i>

                    <strong>Implementar sistema de feedback visual:</strong> Estados de loading, success, error e empty states com consistência em toda aplicação.
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    
    <script>
        // Simulação de cálculo de contraste WCAG
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Adicionar interatividade aos itens de auditoria
            const issueItems

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# src/services/__init__.py
"""
Serviços da aplicação com padrões de resiliência implementados
"""
import json
import time
import logging
import functools
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Callable, TypeVar, Union
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from contextlib import contextmanager
import asyncio
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
import uuid

# Circuit breaker
from circuitbreaker import circuit

# Metrics
from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram, Gauge, generate_latest

# Type variables
T = TypeVar('T')
R = TypeVar('R')

# Configure structured logging
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

# JSON formatter for structured logs
class JSONFormatter(logging.Formatter):
    def format(self, record: logging.LogRecord) -> str:
        log_object = {
            'timestamp': datetime.fromtimestamp(record.created).isoformat(),
            'level': record.levelname,
            'logger': record.name,
            'message': record.getMessage(),
            'correlation_id': getattr(record, 'correlation_id', None),
            'user_id': getattr(record, 'user_id', None),
            'endpoint': getattr(record, 'endpoint', None),
            'duration_ms': getattr(record, 'duration_ms', None),
            'status': getattr(record, 'status', None),
            'service': getattr(record, 'service', None),
            'operation': getattr(record, 'operation', None),
        }
        
        # Add extra fields if present
        if hasattr(record, 'extra'):
            log_object.update(record.extra)
            
        return json.dumps(log_object)

# Apply JSON formatter to root logger
for handler in logging.root.handlers:
    handler.setFormatter(JSONFormatter())

@dataclass
class ServiceMetrics:
    """Métricas de serviço"""
    service_name: str
    total_requests: int = 0
    successful_requests: int = 0
    failed_requests: int = 0
    average_latency_ms: float = 0.0
    p50_latency_ms: float = 0.0
    p95_latency_ms: float = 0.0
    p99_latency_ms: float = 0.0
    circuit_state: str = "CLOSED"
    last_error: Optional[str] = None
    last_error_time: Optional[datetime] = None

class ResilientService:
    """Classe base para serviços com resiliência implementada"""
    
    def __init__(self, service_name: str):
        self.service_name = service_name
        self.metrics = ServiceMetrics(service_name=service_name)
        
        # Prometheus metrics
        self.request_counter = Counter(
            f'{service_name}_requests_total',
            f'Total requests to {service_name}',
            ['method', 'status']
        )
        
        self.request_latency = Histogram(
            f'{service_name}_request_duration_seconds',
            f'Request latency for {service_name}',
            ['method'],
            buckets=[0.01, 0.05, 0.1, 0.3, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0, 5.0]
        )
        
        self.circuit_gauge = Gauge(
            f'{service_name}_circuit_state',
            f'Circuit breaker state for {service_name}',
            ['state']
        )
        
        self.error_counter = Counter(
            f'{service_name}_errors_total',
            f'Total errors in {service_name}',
            ['error_type']
        )
        
        # Business metrics
        self.transaction_counter = Counter(
            f'{service_name}_transactions_total',
            f'Business transactions completed in {service_name}',
            ['transaction_type', 'status']
        )
        
        # Thread pool for async operations
        self.executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=10)
        
    def log_structured(self, level: str, message: str, **extra):
        """Log estruturado em JSON"""
        log_record = logger.makeRecord(
            name=self.service_name,
            level=getattr(logging, level.upper()),
            fn='',
            lno=0,
            msg=message,
            args=(),
            exc_info=None,
            extra=extra
        )
        logger.handle(log_record)
    
    @contextmanager
    def timed_operation(self, operation_name: str, correlation_id: str = None, **extra_log_fields):
        """Context manager para operações temporizadas com logging"""
        start_time = time.time()
        operation_id = str(uuid.uuid4())[:8]
        
        try:
            self.log_structured(
                'INFO',
                f'Starting operation: {operation_name}',
                operation=operation_name,
                operation_id=operation_id,
                correlation_id=correlation_id,
                **extra_log_fields
            )
            
            yield operation_id
            
            duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
            self.log_structured(
                'INFO',
                f'Completed operation: {operation_name}',
                operation=operation_name,
                operation_id=operation_id,
                correlation_id=correlation_id,
                duration_ms=round(duration_ms, 2),
                status='success',
                **extra_log_fields
            )
            
            # Update metrics
            self.metrics.total_requests += 1
            self.metrics.successful_requests += 1
            
        except Exception as e:
            duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
            self.log_structured(
                'ERROR',
                f'Failed operation: {operation_name} - {str(e)}',
                operation=operation_name,
                operation_id=operation_id,
                correlation_id=correlation_id,
                duration_ms=round(duration_ms, 2),
                status='error',
                error=str(e),
                **extra_log_fields
            )
            
            # Update metrics
            self.metrics.total_requests += 1
            self.metrics.failed_requests += 1
            self.metrics.last_error = str(e)
            self.metrics.last_error_time = datetime.now()
            
            self.error_counter.labels(error_type=type(e).__name__).inc()
            raise
    
    def resilient_call(self, func: Callable[..., T], 
                      fallback: Optional[Callable[..., T]] = None,
                      timeout: float = 5.0,
                      max_retries: int = 3,
                      circuit_failure_threshold: int = 5,
                      circuit_recovery_timeout: int = 30) -> Callable[..., T]:
        """
        Decorator para chamadas resilientes com:
        - Timeout explícito
        - Retry com backoff exponencial
        - Circuit breaker
        - Fallback gracioso
        """
        
        @circuit(failure_threshold=circuit_failure_threshold, 
                recovery_timeout=circuit_recovery_timeout,
                expected_exception=Exception)
        def execute_with_resilience(*args, **kwargs) -> T:
            last_exception = None
            
            for attempt in range(max_retries + 1):
                try:
                    # Set timeout for this attempt
                    if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(func):
                        # Async function
                        return asyncio.wait_for(
                            func(*args, **kwargs), 
                            timeout=timeout
                        )
                    else:
                        # Sync function - run in thread pool
                        future = self.executor.submit(func, *args, **kwargs)
                        return future.result(timeout=timeout)
                        
                except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                    last_exception = TimeoutError(f"Timeout after {timeout}s on attempt {attempt + 1}")
                    self.log_structured(
                        'WARNING',
                        f'Timeout in attempt {attempt + 1}',
                        service=self.service_name,
                        timeout=timeout,
                        attempt=attempt + 1
                    )
                    
                except Exception as e:
                    last_exception = e
                    self.log_structured(
                        'WARNING',
                        f'Error in attempt {attempt + 1}: {str(e)}',
                        service=self.service_name,
                        error_type=type(e).__name__,
                        attempt=attempt + 1
                    )
                
                # If not last attempt, wait with exponential backoff + jitter
                if attempt < max_retries:
                    wait_time = (2 ** attempt) + (0.1 * attempt)  # Exponential backoff
                    time.sleep(wait_time)
            
            # All retries failed, try fallback
            if fallback:
                self.log_structured(
                    'WARNING',
                    'All retries failed, using fallback',
                    service=self.service_name,
                    max_retries=max_retries
                )
                try:
                    return fallback(*args, **kwargs)
                except Exception as fallback_error:
                    self.log_structured(
                        'ERROR',
                        f'Fallback also failed: {str(fallback_error)}',
                        service=self.service_name
                    )
                    raise last_exception from fallback_error
            
            # No fallback, raise last exception
            raise last_exception
        
        return execute_with_resilience
    
    def get_health_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Retorna status de saúde detalhado do serviço"""
        return {
            'service': self.service_name,
            'status': 'healthy' if self.metrics.failed_requests == 0 else 'degraded',
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'metrics': asdict(self.metrics),
            'circuit_breaker': {
                'state': self.metrics.circuit_state,
                'failure_rate': (
                    self.metrics.failed_requests / self.metrics.total_requests * 100
                    if self.metrics.total_requests > 0 else 0
                )
            },
            'dependencies': self._check_dependencies()
        }
    
    def _check_dependencies(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Verifica dependências do serviço (sobrescrever nas classes filhas)"""
        return {'status': 'ok', 'details': 'No external dependencies'}
    
    def record_transaction(self, transaction_type: str, status: str = 'completed'):
        """Registra métrica de transação de negócio"""
        self.transaction_counter.labels(
            transaction_type=transaction_type,
            status=status
        ).inc()
        
        self.log_structured(
            'INFO',
            f'Business transaction recorded: {transaction_type} - {status}',
            transaction_type=transaction_type,
            transaction_status=status,
            service=self.service_name
        )

# Serviços específicos da aplicação
class DatabaseService(ResilientService):
    """Serviço de banco de dados com resiliência"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__('database_service')
        self.connection_pool = None
        self.metrics.circuit_state = "CLOSED"
    
    def _check_dependencies(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Verifica conexão com banco de dados"""
        try:
            # Simulação de verificação de conexão
            # Em produção, testaria conexão real
            return {
                'status': 'healthy',
                'connection_pool_size': 10,
                'active_connections': 3,
                'database': 'postgresql'
            }
        except Exception as e:
            return {
                'status': 'unhealthy',
                'error': str(e)
            }
    
    @ResilientService.resilient_call
    def execute_query(self, query: str, params: tuple = None) -> List[Dict]:
        """
        Executa query com parâmetros preparados (SQL injection safe)
        """
        if params is None:
            params = ()
        
        # Log da query (sem parâmetros sensíveis)
        self.log_structured(
            'DEBUG',
            'Executing database query',
            query_hash=hash(query),
            params_count=len(params),
            service=self.service_name
        )
        
        # Simulação de execução de query
        # Em produção, usaria psycopg2 ou similar com connection pool
        time.sleep(0.05)  # Simula latência de banco
        
        # Simulação de resultado
        return [{'id': 1, 'data': 'sample'}]
    
    def get_user_data(self, user_id: str, correlation_id: str = None) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """Exemplo de método que usa todos os padrões de resiliência"""
        with self.timed_operation('get_user_data', correlation_id=correlation_id, user_id=user_id):
            # Query parametrizada (SQL injection safe)
            query = "SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = %s"
            params = (user_id,)
            
            results = self.execute_query(query, params)
            
            if results:
                # Mascarar dados sensíveis nos logs
                user_data = results[0]
                masked_data = {
                    'id': user_data['id'],
                    'email': self._mask_email(user_data.get('email', '')),
                    'name': user_data.get('name', '')
                }
                
                self.log_structured(
                    'INFO',
                    'User data retrieved',
                    user_id=user_id,
                    data_masked=True,
                    service=self.service_name
                )
                
                return user_data
            
            return None
    
    def _mask_email(self, email: str) -> str:
        """Mascara email para logs"""
        if '@' in email:
            local, domain = email.split('@')
            if len(local) > 2:
                return local[:2] + '***' + '@' + domain
        return '***@***'

class ExternalAPIService(ResilientService):
    """Serviço para integração com APIs externas"""
    
    def __init__(self, base_url: str):
        super().__init__('external_api_service')
        self.base_url = base_url
        self.session = None  # Em produção, seria uma session HTTP reutilizável
        self.cache = {}
    
    def _check_dependencies(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Verifica conectividade com API externa"""
        try:
            # Simulação de health check
            return {
                'status': 'healthy',
                'base_url': self.base_url,
                'response_time_ms': 45.2
            }
        except Exception as e:
            return {
                'status': 'unhealthy',
                'error': str(e),
                'base_url': self.base_url
            }
    
    @ResilientService.resilient_call
    def call_external_api(self, endpoint: str, method: str = 'GET', 
                         data: Dict = None, timeout: float = 3.0) -> Dict:
        """
        Chama API externa com resiliência
        """
        # Em produção, usaria requests ou aiohttp
        # Simulação de chamada HTTP
        time.sleep(0.1)  # Simula latência de rede
        
        if endpoint == '/health':
            return {'status': 'ok', 'service': 'external'}
        elif endpoint == '/data':
            return {'data': 'sample', 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()}
        else:
            raise ConnectionError(f"Endpoint {endpoint} not reachable")
    
    def get_cached_data(self, key: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """Fallback para dados em cache"""
        return self.cache.get(key)
    
    def fetch_data_with_fallback(self, endpoint: str, cache_key: str = None) -> Dict:
        """
        Busca dados com fallback para cache
        """
        if cache_key and cache_key in self.cache:
            # Tenta primeiro do cache se disponível
            cached_data = self.cache[cache_key]
            if time.time() - cached_data.get('_cached_at', 0) < 300:  # 5 minutos
                self.log_structured(
                    'INFO',
                    'Using cached data',
                    endpoint=endpoint,
                    cache_key=cache_key,
                    service=self.service_name
                )
                return cached_data
        
        try:
            # Tenta API externa com resiliência
            data = self.call_external_api(endpoint)
            
            # Atualiza cache
            if cache_key:
                data['_cached_at'] = time.time()
                self.cache[cache_key] = data
            
            return data
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.log_structured(
                'ERROR',
                f'Failed to fetch from API, trying cache: {str(e)}',
                endpoint=endpoint,
                service=self.service_name
            )
            
            # Fallback para cache mesmo se expirado
            if cache_key and cache_key in self.cache:
                self.log_structured(
                    'WARNING',
                    'Using expired cache as fallback',
                    endpoint=endpoint,
                    cache_key=cache_key,
                    service=self.service_name
                )
                return self.cache[cache_key]
            
            # Fallback padrão se não houver cache
            return {
                'status': 'degraded',
                'message': 'Service temporarily unavailable',
                'data': None,
                'from_cache': False
            }

class LLMService(ResilientService):
    """Serviço para integração com LLMs"""
    
    def __init__(self, model_name: str = 'gpt-4'):

            # Simulação de health check para LLM

                'status': 'healthy',
                'model': self.model_name,
                'max_tokens': self.max_tokens,
                'timeout_seconds': self.timeout
            }
        except Exception as e:
            return {
                'status': 'unhealthy',
                'error': str(e),
                'model': self.model_name
            }

        """

        # Simulação de chamada ao LLM
        # Em produção, usaria OpenAI SDK ou similar
        time.sleep(2.5)  # Simula latência do modelo

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Sistema de Design

Vou implementar um sistema de design moderno para a V13 com foco em performance, acessibilidade e experiência do usuário. Vou criar componentes React com TypeScript, tokens de design, skeleton screens, transições suaves e tratamento de erros granular.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
src/
├── design-system/
│   ├── tokens/
│   │   ├── colors.ts
│   │   ├── spacing.ts
│   │   ├── typography.ts
│   │   ├── shadows.ts
│   │   └── index.ts
│   ├── components/
│   │   ├── Button/
│   │   ├── Card/
│   │   ├── Input/

│   ├── hooks/

│   │   ├── usePerformance.ts
│   │   └── useErrorBoundary.ts
│   └── utils/

│       ├── performance.ts
│       └── a11y.ts
├── pages/

## 2. Componentes Base

**src/design-system/components/Button/Button.tsx**
```typescript
import React, { forwardRef, ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { colors, spacing, typography, shadows } from '../../tokens';
import { cva, type VariantProps } from 'class-variance-authority';
import { cn } from '../../../utils/classNames';

const buttonVariants = cva(
  'inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-lg font-medium transition-all duration-200 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50',
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        primary: 'bg-primary-500 text-white hover:bg-primary-600 active:bg-primary-700 focus-visible:ring-primary-500',
        secondary: 'bg-neutral-100 text-neutral-900 hover:bg-neutral-200 active:bg-neutral-300 focus-visible:ring-neutral-500',
        outline: 'border border-neutral-300 bg-transparent text-neutral-700 hover:bg-neutral-50 active:bg-neutral-100 focus-visible:ring-neutral-500',
        ghost: 'bg-transparent text-neutral-700 hover:bg-neutral-100 active:bg-neutral-200 focus-visible:ring-neutral-500',
        danger: 'bg-error-500 text-white hover:bg-error-600 active:bg-error-700 focus-visible:ring-error-500',
        success: 'bg-success-500 text-white hover:bg-success-600 active:bg-success-700 focus-visible:ring-success-500',
      },
      size: {
        xs: 'h-7 px-2 text-xs',
        sm: 'h-8 px-3 text-sm',
        md: 'h-10 px-4 text-base',
        lg: 'h-12 px-6 text-lg',
        xl: 'h-14 px-8 text-xl',
      },
      fullWidth: {
        true: 'w-full',
      },
      loading: {
        true: 'relative text-transparent',
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: 'primary',
      size: 'md',
    },
  }
);

export interface ButtonProps
  extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement>,
    VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> {
  loading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
}

const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  ({ className, variant, size, fullWidth, loading, leftIcon, rightIcon, children, disabled, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <button
        className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, fullWidth, loading, className }))}
        ref={ref}
        disabled={disabled || loading}
        aria-busy={loading}
        {...props}
      >
        {loading && (
          <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin rounded-full border-2 border-current border-t-transparent" />
          </div>
        )}
        {leftIcon && !loading && <span className="mr-2">{leftIcon}</span>}
        <span className={loading ? 'opacity-0' : 'opacity-100'}>{children}</span>
        {rightIcon && !loading && <span className="ml-2">{rightIcon}</span>}
      </button>
    );
  }
);

Button.displayName = 'Button';

export { Button, buttonVariants };
```

**src/design-system/components/Button/Button.test.tsx**
```typescript
import React from 'react';
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import { Button } from './Button';
import { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest';

describe('Button', () => {
  it('renders with default props', () => {
    render(<Button>Click me</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i });
    expect(button).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(button).toHaveClass('bg-primary-500');
  });

  it('handles click events', () => {
    const handleClick = vi.fn();
    render(<Button onClick={handleClick}>Click me</Button>);
    fireEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button'));
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
  });

  it('shows loading state', () => {
    render(<Button loading>Loading</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toBeDisabled();
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('aria-busy', 'true');
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toContainElement(screen.getByRole('status'));
  });

  it('is accessible via keyboard', () => {
    render(<Button>Accessible</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    button.focus();
    expect(button).toHaveFocus();
    fireEvent.keyDown(button, { key: 'Enter' });
    fireEvent.keyDown(button, { key: ' ' });
  });
});
```

**src/design-system/components/Skeleton/Skeleton.tsx**
```typescript
import React from 'react';
import { cn } from '../../../utils/classNames';

export interface SkeletonProps extends React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
  variant?: 'text' | 'circular' | 'rectangular' | 'rounded';
  width?: string | number;
  height?: string | number;
  animation?: 'pulse' | 'wave' | 'none';
  count?: number;
}

const Skeleton: React.FC<SkeletonProps> = ({
  className,
  variant = 'text',
  width,
  height,
  animation = 'pulse',
  count = 1,
  style,
  ...props
}) => {
  const baseStyles = {
    width: width || (variant === 'circular' ? '40px' : '100%'),
    height: height || (variant === 'text' ? '1em' : variant === 'circular' ? '40px' : '100px'),
  };

  const variantClasses = {
    text: 'rounded',
    circular: 'rounded-full',
    rectangular: 'rounded-none',
    rounded: 'rounded-lg',
  };

  const animationClasses = {
    pulse: 'animate-pulse',
    wave: 'animate-wave',
    none: '',
  };

  const skeletons = Array.from({ length: count }, (_, index) => (
    <div
      key={index}
      className={cn(
        'bg-neutral-200 dark:bg-neutral-700',
        variantClasses[variant],
        animationClasses[animation],
        className
      )}
      style={{
        ...baseStyles,
        ...style,
        ...(count > 1 && index > 0 ? { marginTop: '0.5rem' } : {}),
      }}
      aria-busy="true"
      aria-label="Loading content"
      {...props}
    />
  ));

  return <>{skeletons}</>;
};

// Skeleton screen para páginas
export const SkeletonScreen: React.FC<{
  header?: boolean;
  sidebar?: boolean;
  contentLines?: number;
  footer?: boolean;
}> = ({ header = true, sidebar = true, contentLines = 5, footer = true }) => {
  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background-primary p-6" role="status" aria-label="Page loading">
      <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl">
        {header && (
          <div className="mb-8">
            <Skeleton variant="rounded" height="64px" className="mb-4" />
            <Skeleton variant="text" width="60%" height="32px" />
          </div>
        )}
        
        <div className="flex gap-6">
          {sidebar && (
            <div className="hidden w-64 flex-col gap-4 md:flex">
              <Skeleton variant="rounded" height="48px" count={4} />
            </div>
          )}
          
          <div className="flex-1">
            <div className="mb-6">
              <Skeleton variant="text" width="40%" height="28px" className="mb-2" />
              <Skeleton variant="text" width="80%" />
            </div>
            
            <div className="space-y-4">
              {Array.from({ length: contentLines }).map((_, i) => (
                <div key={i} className="rounded-lg border border-neutral-200 p-4">
                  <Skeleton variant="text" width={`${70 + (i % 3) * 10}%`} className="mb-2" />
                  <Skeleton variant="text" width={`${40 + (i % 4) * 15}%`} />
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
            
            {footer && (
              <div className="mt-8">
                <Skeleton variant="rounded" height="48px" />
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Skeleton;
```

## 1. Configuração Datadog Agent

**docker/Dockerfile.datadog-agent:**
```dockerfile
FROM datadog/agent:latest

# Configuração específica para DIYAPP V13
ENV DD_API_KEY=${DATADOG_API_KEY}
ENV DD_SITE="datadoghq.com"
ENV DD_APM_ENABLED=true
ENV DD_LOGS_ENABLED=true
ENV DD_PROCESS_AGENT_ENABLED=true
ENV DD_DOGSTATSD_NON_LOCAL_TRAFFIC=true
ENV DD_APM_NON_LOCAL_TRAFFIC=true

# Configurações de recursos
ENV DD_APM_MAX_MEMORY=512
ENV DD_APM_MAX_CPU=50

# Copiar configurações customizadas
COPY ./src/monitoring/datadog/config/datadog.yaml /etc/datadog-agent/datadog.yaml
COPY ./src/monitoring/datadog/config/apm-config.yaml /etc/datadog-agent/conf.d/apm.d/

EXPOSE 8125/udp 8126/tcp

CMD ["/init"]
```

## 2. Instrumentação da Aplicação

**src/monitoring/instrumentation/api-metrics.js:**
```javascript
const StatsD = require('hot-shots');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');

class APIMetrics {
  constructor() {
    this.statsd = new StatsD({
      host: process.env.DD_AGENT_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: 8125,
      prefix: 'diyapp.api.',
      errorHandler: (error) => {
        logger.error('StatsD error:', error);
      }
    });

    this.sloConfig = {
      availability: 99.95,
      latencyP95: 200,
      errorRate: 0.05,
      llmLatencyP95: 8000
    };
  }

  /**
   * Medir latência de requisição API
   */
  measureRequestLatency(method, route, statusCode, duration) {
    const tags = [
      `method:${method}`,
      `route:${route}`,
      `status:${statusCode}`,
      `status_class:${Math.floor(statusCode / 100)}xx`
    ];

    // Histogram para percentis
    this.statsd.histogram('request.duration', duration, tags);
    
    // Verificar violação de SLO
    if (duration > this.sloConfig.latencyP95) {
      this.statsd.increment('slo.violation.latency', 1, tags);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Medir disponibilidade do serviço
   */
  recordAvailability(isAvailable, serviceName) {
    const value = isAvailable ? 1 : 0;
    const tags = [`service:${serviceName}`];
    
    this.statsd.gauge('availability', value, tags);
    
    if (!isAvailable) {
      this.statsd.increment('slo.violation.availability', 1, tags);
      logger.warn(`Availability SLO violation for ${serviceName}`);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Medir taxa de erro
   */
  recordError(errorType, serviceName, isSLOViolation = false) {
    const tags = [
      `error_type:${errorType}`,
      `service:${serviceName}`
    ];

    this.statsd.increment('errors.count', 1, tags);
    
    if (isSLOViolation) {
      this.statsd.increment('slo.violation.errors', 1, tags);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Medir métricas de LLM
   */
  recordLLMMetrics(provider, model, duration, tokens, success) {
    const tags = [
      `provider:${provider}`,
      `model:${model}`,
      `success:${success}`
    ];

    // Latência
    this.statsd.histogram('llm.request.duration', duration, tags);
    
    // Tokens por segundo
    if (duration > 0 && tokens > 0) {
      const tokensPerSecond = tokens / (duration / 1000);
      this.statsd.gauge('llm.tokens_per_second', tokensPerSecond, tags);
    }
    
    // Verificar SLO de latência LLM
    if (duration > this.sloConfig.llmLatencyP95) {
      this.statsd.increment('slo.violation.llm_latency', 1, tags);
      logger.warn(`LLM latency SLO violation: ${provider}/${model} - ${duration}ms`);
    }
    
    // Disponibilidade do provedor
    this.statsd.gauge(`llm.provider.availability.${provider}`, success ? 1 : 0);
  }

  /**
   * Métricas de negócio
   */
  recordBusinessMetric(metricName, value, userId = null) {
    const tags = [];
    if (userId) {
      tags.push(`user_id:${userId}`);
    }
    
    this.statsd.gauge(`business.${metricName}`, value, tags);
  }

  /**
   * Calcular error budget em tempo real
   */
  calculateErrorBudget(serviceName, windowMinutes = 60) {
    // Em produção, isso consultaria o Datadog API
    // Esta é uma implementação simplificada
    return {
      service: serviceName,
      window_minutes: windowMinutes,
      error_budget_remaining: 0.95, // Exemplo: 95% restante
      slo_violations_last_hour: 2,
      estimated_time_to_burnout: '48h'
    };
  }
}

module.exports = new APIMetrics();
```

**src/monitoring/instrumentation/llm-tracing.js:**
```javascript
const { tracer } = require('dd-trace').init({
  service: 'diyapp-llm-gateway',
  env: process.env.NODE_ENV,
  version: 'v13'
});

class LLMTracing {
  /**
   * Rastrear requisição LLM
   */
  async traceLLMRequest(provider, model, operation, fn) {
    return tracer.trace('llm.request', {
      resource: `${provider}.${model}.${operation}`,
      type: 'llm',
      tags: {
        'llm.provider': provider,
        'llm.model': model,
        'llm.operation': operation,
        'service.version': 'v13'
      }
    }, async (span) => {
      const startTime = Date.now();
      
      try {
        const result = await fn();
        const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
        
        span.setTag('duration', duration);
        span.setTag('success', true);
        
        return result;
      } catch (error) {
        const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
        
        span.setTag('duration', duration);
        span.setTag('success', false);
        span.setTag('error.type', error.constructor.name);
        span.setTag('error.message', error.message);
        
        throw error;
      }
    });
  }

  /**
   * Rastrear cadeia de LLMs (rag, chain, etc)
   */
  async traceLLMChain(chainName, steps) {
    return tracer.trace('llm.chain', {
      resource: chainName,
      type: 'llm-chain',
      tags: {
        'llm.chain.name': chainName,
        'llm.steps.count': steps.length
      }
    }, async (span) => {
      const results = [];
      
      for (let i = 0; i < steps.length; i++) {
        const step = steps[i];
        
        await tracer.trace(`llm.chain.step.${i}`, {
          resource: step.name,
          tags: {
            'llm.step.index': i,
            'llm.step.name': step.name,
            'llm.step.type': step.type
          }
        }, async (stepSpan) => {
          const result = await step.execute();
          results.push(result);
          
          stepSpan.setTag('success', true);
          return result;
        });
      }
      
      span.setTag('success', true);
      return results;
    });
  }
}

module.exports = new LLMTracing();
```

## 3. Definição de SLOs e SLIs

**src/monitoring/slo/slo-definitions.js:**
```javascript
class SLODefinitions {
  constructor() {
    this.slos = {
      // SLOs de API
      api_availability: {
        name: 'API Availability',
        description: 'Disponibilidade do serviço API principal',
        sli: 'availability_sli',
        target: 99.95, // 99.95%
        period: '30d',
        tags: ['service:api-gateway', 'tier:critical']
      },
      
      api_latency_p95: {
        name: 'API Latency P95',
        description: '95º percentil de latência das requisições API',
        sli: 'latency_p95_sli',
        target: 200, // 200ms
        period: '30d',
        tags: ['service:api-gateway', 'tier:critical']
      },
      
      api_error_rate: {
        name: 'API Error Rate',
        description: 'Taxa de erros 5xx nas requisições API',
        sli: 'error_rate_sli',
        target: 0.05, // 0.05%
        period: '30d',
        tags: ['service:api-gateway', 'tier:critical']
      },
      
      // SLOs de LLM
      llm_latency_p95: {
        name: 'LLM Response Latency P95',
        description: '95º percentil de latência das respostas LLM',
        sli: 'llm_latency_p95_sli',
        target: 8000, // 8 segundos
        period: '30d',
        tags: ['service:llm-gateway', 'tier:critical']
      },
      
      llm_availability: {
        name: 'LLM Provider Availability',
        description: 'Disponibilidade dos provedores de LLM',
        sli: 'llm_availability_sli',
        target: 99.9, // 99.9%
        period: '30d',
        tags: ['service:llm-gateway', 'tier:critical']
      },
      
      // SLOs de negócio
      user_session_success: {
        name: 'User Session Success Rate',
        description: 'Taxa de sucesso de sessões de usuário',
        sli: 'user_session_sli',
        target: 99.8, // 99.8%
        period: '7d',
        tags: ['tier:business']
      }
    };

    this.errorBudgetPolicies = {
      healthy: { threshold: 50, action: 'normal_operations' },
      warning: { threshold: 20, action: 'increased_caution' },
      critical: { threshold: 5, action: 'feature_freeze' },
      exhausted: { threshold: 0, action: 'stabilization_only' }
    };
  }

  /**
   * Calcular SLI baseado em métricas
   */
  calculateSLI(metricName, goodEvents, totalEvents) {
    if (totalEvents === 0) return 100; // Sem eventos, considerado 100%
    
    const sliValue = (goodEvents / totalEvents) * 100;
    
    // Log para debugging
    console.log(`SLI Calculation: ${metricName} = ${goodEvents}/${totalEvents} = ${sliValue.toFixed(2)}%`);
    
    return sliValue;
  }

  /**
   * Calcular error budget restante
   */
  calculateErrorBudget(slo, sliValue, timeWindowDays = 30) {
    const target = slo.target;
    const errorBudget = 100 - target; // Budget de erro em porcentagem
    
    const consumedBudget = Math.max(0, target - sliValue);
    const remainingBudget = Math.max(0, errorBudget - consumedBudget);
    
    const remainingPercentage = (remainingBudget / errorBudget) * 100;
    
    return {
      slo_name: slo.name,
      sli_value: sliValue,
      target: target,
      error_budget_total: errorBudget,
      error_budget_consumed: consumedBudget,
      error_budget_remaining: remainingBudget,
      error_budget_remaining_percentage: remainingPercentage,
      status: this.getBudgetStatus(remainingPercentage)
    };
  }

  /**
   * Determinar status do error budget
   */
  getBudgetStatus(remainingPercentage) {
    if (remainingPercentage >= this.errorBudgetPolicies.healthy.threshold) {
      return 'healthy';
    } else if (remainingPercentage >= this.errorBudgetPolicies.warning.threshold) {
      return 'warning';
    } else if (remainingPercentage >= this.errorBudgetPolicies.critical.threshold) {
      return 'critical';
    } else {
      return 'exhausted';
    }
  }

  /**
   * Gerar recomendações baseadas no error budget
   */
  getBudgetRecommendations(status) {
    const policies = {
      healthy: {
        message: 'Error budget saudável (>50%)',
        actions: [
          'Deploys frequentes permitidos',
          'Experimentação com novas features',
          'Mudanças de maior risco podem ser consideradas'
        ],
        deploy_policy: 'normal'
      },
      warning: {
        message: 'Error budget em alerta (20-50%)',
        actions: [
          'Deploys continuam com cautela aumentada',
          'Revisar alertas e runbooks',
          'Priorizar estabilidade sobre features novas',
          'Investigar causas de consumo de budget'
        ],
        deploy_policy: 'cautious'
      },
      critical: {
        message: 'Error budget crítico (5-20%)',
        actions: [
          'Notificar Squad Leader e Product Manager',
          'Freeze de features novas',
          'Foco total em confiabilidade',
          'Postmortem obrigatório para novos incidentes'
        ],
        deploy_policy: 'restricted'
      },
      exhausted: {
        message: 'Error budget esgotado (0%)',
        actions: [
          'FREEZE DE DEPLOYS IMEDIATO',
          'Toda capacidade da squad para estabilização',
          'Revisão completa de todos os SLOs',
          'Game Day obrigatório após recuperação'
        ],
        deploy_policy: 'frozen'
      }
    };

    return policies[status] || policies.healthy;
  }
}

module.exports = new SLODefinitions();
```

## 4. Dashboard SLO Overview (Datadog

### [Sessão Paralela: QA]
```javascript
// k6-load-tests/src/scenarios/diyapp-load.js
import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep, group } from 'k6';
import { Rate, Trend, Counter } from 'k6/metrics';

// Custom metrics
const errorRate = new Rate('errors');
const requestDuration = new Trend('request_duration');
const successfulRequests = new Counter('successful_requests');
const failedRequests = new Counter('failed_requests');

// SLO thresholds
const SLO_P95 = 500; // 95th percentile response time < 500ms
const SLO_ERROR_RATE = 0.01; // Error rate < 1%
const SLO_AVAILABILITY = 0.999; // 99.9% availability

// Configuration
export const options = {
  stages: [
    { duration: '2m', target: 50 }, // Ramp up
    { duration: '5m', target: 100 }, // Normal load
    { duration: '3m', target: 250 }, // Stress test
    { duration: '2m', target: 500 }, // Peak load
    { duration: '2m', target: 100 }, // Ramp down
    { duration: '1m', target: 0 }, // Recovery
  ],
  thresholds: {
    'errors': ['rate<0.01'], // SLO: Error rate < 1%
    'http_req_duration{type:api}': ['p(95)<500'], // SLO: P95 < 500ms
    'http_req_duration{type:ui}': ['p(95)<1000'], // SLO: UI P95 < 1s
    'http_req_failed': ['rate<0.01'], // SLO: Failed requests < 1%
  },
  ext: {
    loadimpact: {
      projectID: 123456,
      name: 'DIYAPP Load Test - SLO Validation'
    }
  }
};

// Test data
const testUsers = JSON.parse(open('./test-data/users.json'));
const premiumFlows = JSON.parse(open('./test-data/premium-flows.json'));

// Helper functions
function generateSessionToken(userId) {
  return `session_${userId}_${Date.now()}`;
}

function simulateUserThinkTime() {
  sleep(Math.random() * 3 + 1); // 1-4 seconds
}

function validateSLO(response, endpoint) {
  const isSuccess = check(response, {
    [`${endpoint} status 2xx/3xx`]: (r) => r.status >= 200 && r.status < 400,
    [`${endpoint} response time < 1s`]: (r) => r.timings.duration < 1000,
  });
  
  if (!isSuccess) {
    failedRequests.add(1);
    errorRate.add(1);
    console.error(`SLO violation on ${endpoint}: ${response.status} - ${response.timings.duration}ms`);
  } else {
    successfulRequests.add(1);
    requestDuration.add(response.timings.duration, { endpoint: endpoint });
  }
  
  return isSuccess;
}

// Main test scenarios
export default function () {
  const user = testUsers[__VU % testUsers.length];
  const sessionToken = generateSessionToken(user.id);
  
  // Group 1: API Load Tests
  group('API Load Tests', function () {
    // Test 1: Health check endpoint
    const healthRes = http.get(`${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/health`, {
      tags: { type: 'api', endpoint: 'health' }
    });
    validateSLO(healthRes, 'health');
    
    // Test 2: Authentication load
    const authRes = http.post(
      `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/auth/login`,
      JSON.stringify({
        email: user.email,
        password: 'test_password'
      }),
      {
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${sessionToken}`
        },
        tags: { type: 'api', endpoint: 'auth' }
      }
    );
    validateSLO(authRes, 'auth');
    
    // Test 3: Premium feature API
    if (user.isPremium) {
      const premiumRes = http.get(
        `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/premium/features`,
        {
          headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${sessionToken}` },
          tags: { type: 'api', endpoint: 'premium' }
        }
      );
      validateSLO(premiumRes, 'premium');
    }
    
    // Test 4: Concurrent resource creation
    const batchRes = http.batch([
      ['POST', `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/projects`, null, { 
        headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${sessionToken}` } 
      }],
      ['POST', `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/templates`, null, { 
        headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${sessionToken}` } 
      }],
      ['GET', `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/user/profile`, null, { 
        headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${sessionToken}` } 
      }]
    ]);
    
    batchRes.forEach((res, index) => {
      validateSLO(res, `batch_${index}`);
    });
  });
  
  simulateUserThinkTime();
  
  // Group 2: UI Load Tests
  group('UI Load Tests', function () {
    // Test 5: Main dashboard
    const dashboardRes = http.get(`${__ENV.BASE_URL}/dashboard`, {
      tags: { type: 'ui', endpoint: 'dashboard' }
    });
    validateSLO(dashboardRes, 'dashboard');
    
    // Test 6: Premium UX flows
    if (user.isPremium) {
      premiumFlows.forEach((flow, index) => {
        const flowRes = http.get(
          `${__ENV.BASE_URL}${flow.path}`,
          {
            headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${sessionToken}` },
            tags: { type: 'ui', endpoint: `premium_flow_${index}` }
          }
        );
        validateSLO(flowRes, `premium_flow_${index}`);
        sleep(0.5);
      });
    }
    
    // Test 7: Asset loading (CSS, JS, images)
    const assets = [
      '/static/css/main.css',
      '/static/js/app.js',
      '/static/images/logo.png'
    ];
    
    assets.forEach((asset) => {
      const assetRes = http.get(`${__ENV.BASE_URL}${asset}`, {
        tags: { type: 'asset', endpoint: asset }
      });
      validateSLO(assetRes, asset);
    });
  });
  
  simulateUserThinkTime();
  
  // Group 3: Failure scenario simulations
  group('Failure Scenarios', function () {
    // Test 8: Service degradation simulation
    const degradedRes = http.get(`${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/degraded-endpoint`, {
      timeout: '10s', // Longer timeout for degraded service
      tags: { type: 'failure', scenario: 'degraded_service' }
    });
    
    // Expect failures for degraded endpoint
    const isDegraded = check(degradedRes, {
      'degraded endpoint timeout or 5xx': (r) => 
        r.status === 0 || (r.status >= 500 && r.status < 600)
    });
    
    if (!isDegraded) {
      console.warn('Degraded service test passed unexpectedly');
    }
    
    // Test 9: Database connection failure simulation
    const dbErrorRes = http.get(`${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/db-error`, {
      tags: { type: 'failure', scenario: 'db_failure' }
    });
    
    check(dbErrorRes, {
      'db error returns 503': (r) => r.status === 503,
      'db error has proper message': (r) => 
        JSON.parse(r.body).error === 'Database unavailable'
    });
    
    // Test 10: Rate limiting
    for (let i = 0; i < 15; i++) {
      const rateLimitRes = http.get(`${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/rate-limited`, {
        headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${sessionToken}` },
        tags: { type: 'failure', scenario: 'rate_limiting' }
      });
      
      if (i >= 10) {
        check(rateLimitRes, {
          'rate limited after 10 requests': (r) => r.status === 429
        });
      }
      
      sleep(0.1);
    }
  });
}

// Teardown function for reporting
export function teardown(data) {
  console.log('Test completed. Generating SLO report...');
  
  const sloReport = {
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    test_duration: data.state.testRunDuration,
    total_requests: successfulRequests.count + failedRequests.count,
    successful_requests: successfulRequests.count,
    failed_requests: failedRequests.count,
    error_rate: failedRequests.count / (successfulRequests.count + failedRequests.count),
    p95_response_time: requestDuration.percentiles[95],
    slo_violations: {
      p95_response_time: requestDuration.percentiles[95] > SLO_P95,
      error_rate: (failedRequests.count / (successfulRequests.count + failedRequests.count)) > SLO_ERROR_RATE
    },
    recommendations: []
  };
  
  // Generate recommendations
  if (sloReport.slo_violations.p95_response_time) {
    sloReport.recommendations.push('P95 response time exceeds SLO. Consider: 1) Database query optimization, 2) Adding caching layer, 3) Scaling horizontally');
  }
  
  if (sloReport.slo_violations.error_rate) {
    sloReport.recommendations.push('Error rate exceeds SLO. Investigate: 1) Database connection pool, 2) External service dependencies, 3) Memory leaks');
  }
  
  console.log(JSON.stringify(sloReport, null, 2));
  
  // Send report to monitoring system
  if (__ENV.MONITORING_URL) {
    http.post(__ENV.MONITORING_URL, JSON.stringify(sloReport), {
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
    });
  }
}

// cypress/e2e/premium-ux-flows.cy.js
describe('DIYAPP Premium UX Flows', () => {
  const premiumUser = {
    email: 'premium@example.com',
    password: 'PremiumPass123!',
    tier: 'premium_plus'
  };

  const failureScenarios = {
    serviceOutage: false,
    slowNetwork: false,
    paymentFailure: false
  };

  beforeEach(() => {
    // Mock service status
    cy.intercept('GET', '/api/health', (req) => {
      if (failureScenarios.serviceOutage) {
        req.reply({
          statusCode: 503,
          body: { status: 'unavailable', message: 'Service undergoing maintenance' }
        });
      } else {
        req.reply({
          statusCode: 200,
          body: { status: 'healthy', version: 'v13.0.0' }
        });
      }
    }).as('healthCheck');

    // Network condition simulation
    if (failureScenarios.slowNetwork) {
      cy.intercept('**', (req) => {
        req.on('response', (res) => {
          res.setDelay(3000); // 3 second delay
        });
      });
    }

    cy.visit('/');
    cy.login(premiumUser.email, premiumUser.password);
  });

  describe('Premium Feature: Advanced Analytics Dashboard', () => {
    it('should load complex analytics with real-time data', () => {
      // Mock analytics data
      cy.intercept('GET', '/api/analytics/dashboard', {
        fixture: 'analytics-dashboard.json'
      }).as('getAnalytics');

      cy.get('[data-testid="premium-nav"]').click();
      cy.get('[data-testid="analytics-tab"]').click();
      
      cy.wait('@getAnalytics');
      
      // Validate dashboard components
      cy.get('[data-testid="metrics-grid"]').should('be.visible');
      cy.get('[data-testid="real-time-chart"]').should('be.visible');
      cy.get('[data-testid="top-projects"]').should('have.length.at.least', 5);
      
      // Test interactive elements
      cy.get('[data-testid="date-range-picker"]').click();
      cy.get('[data-testid="last-30-days"]').click();
      cy.wait('@getAnalytics'); // Should refetch with new range
      
      // Export functionality
      cy.get('[data-testid="export-analytics"]').click();
      cy.get('[data-testid="export-format"]').select('CSV');
      cy.get('[data-testid="confirm-export"]').click();
      cy.get('[data-testid="export-success"]').should('be.visible');
    });

    it('should handle large dataset visualization', () => {
      // Mock large dataset (10,000 data points)
      cy.intercept('GET', '/api/analytics/historical*', {
        fixture: 'large-dataset.json'
      }).as('getHistoricalData');

      cy.visit('/premium/analytics/historical');
      
      cy.wait('@getHistoricalData', { timeout: 10000 });
      
      // Performance assertions
      cy.window().then((win) => {
        const perfEntries = win.performance.getEntriesByType('resource');
        const analyticsLoad = perfEntries.find(e => e.name.includes('analytics/historical'));
        
        expect(analyticsLoad.duration).to.be.lessThan(2000); // Load under 2 seconds
      });
      
      // Virtual scroll test
      cy.get('[data-testid="virtual-scroll-container"]').scrollTo('bottom');
      cy.get('[data-testid="data-point"]').should('have.length.gt', 50);
    });
  });

  describe('Premium Feature: AI Template Generator', () => {
    it('should generate templates with AI assistance', () => {
      cy.intercept('POST', '/api/ai/templates/generate', {
        fixture: 'ai-template-response.json'
      }).as('generateTemplate');

      cy.visit('/premium/ai-templates');
      
      // Fill AI prompt
      cy.get('[data-testid="ai-prompt-input"]').type('Create a project management template for agile teams');
      cy.get('[data-testid="tone-selector"]').select('Professional');
      cy.get('[data-testid="complexity-slider"]').invoke('val', 7).trigger('input');
      
      // Generate
      cy.get('[data-testid="generate-button"]').click();
      
      cy.wait('@generateTemplate');
      
      // Validate generated template
      cy.get('[data-testid="generated-template"]').should('be.visible');
      cy.get('[data-testid="template-sections"]').should('have.length.at.least', 3);
      
      // Save template
      cy.get('[data-testid="save-template"]').click();
      cy.get('[data-testid="save-success"]').should('be.visible');
    });

    it('should handle AI service degradation gracefully', () => {
      failureScenarios.serviceOutage = true;
      
      cy.intercept('POST', '/api/ai/templates/generate', {
        statusCode: 503,
        body: { error: 'AI service temporarily unavailable' }
      }).as('aiServiceDown');

      cy.visit('/premium/ai-templates');
      
      cy.get('[data-testid="ai-prompt-input"]').type('Test prompt');
      cy.get('[data-testid="generate-button"]').click();
      
      cy.wait('@aiServiceDown');
      
      // Should show fallback UI
      cy.get('[data-testid="fallback-templates"]').should('be.visible');
      cy.get('[data-testid="error-message"]').should('contain', 'unavailable');
      
      // Manual template selection should still work
      cy.get('[data-testid="manual-template-1"]').click();
      cy.get('[data-testid="template-editor"]').should('be.visible');
      
      failureScenarios.serviceOutage = false;
    });
  });

  describe('Failure Scenario: Payment Processing', () => {
    it('should handle payment failure during upgrade', () => {
      failureScenarios.paymentFailure = true;
      
      cy.intercept('POST', '/api/payments/process', {
        statusCode: 402,
        body: { error: 'Payment failed', code: 'INSUFFICIENT_FUNDS' }
      }).as('paymentFailed');

      cy.visit('/billing/upgrade');
      
      // Fill payment form
      cy.get('[data-testid="card-number"]').type('4111111111111111');
      cy.get('[data-testid="expiry-date"]').type('12/25');

# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Instrumentação de Eventos de Usuário

## Estrutura do Projeto

```

├── src/
│   ├── events/
│   │   ├── collector.js          # Coletor de eventos no frontend
│   │   ├── types.js              # Tipos de eventos e schemas
│   │   ├── api.js                # API para envio de eventos
│   │   └── utils.js              # Utilitários para eventos

│       └── events-dashboard.js   # Dashboard de visualização
