## 2. Schema do Banco de Dados (scripts/setup-events-db.sql)

```sql
-- Banco de dados de eventos raw (camada bronze)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_diyapp_events (
    event_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    session_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    user_id TEXT,
    event_type TEXT NOT NULL,
    event_name TEXT NOT NULL,
    element_path TEXT,
    element_type TEXT,
    element_id TEXT,
    element_class TEXT,
    element_text TEXT,
    page_url TEXT NOT NULL,
    page_title TEXT,
    viewport_width INTEGER,
    viewport_height INTEGER,
    user_agent TEXT,
    referrer TEXT,
    language TEXT,
    timestamp INTEGER NOT NULL,
    timezone_offset INTEGER,
    metadata JSON,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Índices para performance de queries
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_raw_events_timestamp ON raw_diyapp_events(timestamp);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_raw_events_session ON raw_diyapp_events(session_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_raw_events_user ON raw_diyapp_events(user_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_raw_events_type ON raw_diyapp_events(event_type);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_raw_events_name ON raw_diyapp_events(event_name);

-- Tabela para sessões de usuário
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS user_sessions (
    session_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id TEXT,
    started_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
    ended_at INTEGER,
    page_count INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    event_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    device_type TEXT,
    browser TEXT,
    os TEXT,
    country TEXT,
    city TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Tabela para métricas diárias (agregação)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS daily_metrics (
    date TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    total_users INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    active_sessions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_events INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    click_events INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    error_events INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_session_duration INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    bounce_rate REAL DEFAULT 0,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Tabela para erros de aplicação
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS application_errors (
    error_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    session_id TEXT,
    user_id TEXT,
    error_type TEXT NOT NULL,
    error_message TEXT,
    stack_trace TEXT,
    page_url TEXT,
    line_number INTEGER,
    column_number INTEGER,
    timestamp INTEGER NOT NULL,
    resolved BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
```

## 3. Coletor de Eventos Frontend (public/events.js)

```javascript
// DIYAPP V13 - Coletor de Eventos de Usuário
(function() {
    'use strict';

    const DIYAPP_EVENTS = {
        VERSION: '1.0.0',
        ENDPOINT: '/api/events',
        SESSION_TIMEOUT: 30 * 60 * 1000, // 30 minutos
        SAMPLE_RATE: 1.0, // 100% dos eventos (ajustável para produção)
        
        // Buffer de eventos para batch processing
        eventBuffer: [],
        maxBufferSize: 20,
        flushInterval: 10000, // 10 segundos
        
        // Estado da sessão
        sessionId: null,
        userId: null,
        sessionStartTime: null,
        lastActivityTime: null,
        
        // Inicialização
        init: function(config = {}) {
            if (config.endpoint) this.ENDPOINT = config.endpoint;
            if (config.sampleRate) this.SAMPLE_RATE = config.sampleRate;
            
            this.generateSessionId();
            this.setupEventListeners();
            this.setupActivityTracker();
            this.setupErrorHandling();
            this.startFlushInterval();
            
            // Captura evento de página carregada
            this.capturePageView();
            
            console.log('DIYAPP Events initialized with session:', this.sessionId);
        },
        
        // Gera ID único para sessão
        generateSessionId: function() {
            this.sessionId = 'ses_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);
            this.sessionStartTime = Date.now();
            this.lastActivityTime = Date.now();
            
            // Tenta recuperar user_id do localStorage ou cookies
            this.userId = localStorage.getItem('diyapp_user_id') || 
                          this.getCookie('diyapp_user_id') || 
                          null;
        },
        
        // Configura listeners para eventos de interação
        setupEventListeners: function() {
            // Captura de clicks
            document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                if (Math.random() > this.SAMPLE_RATE) return;
                
                const element = e.target;
                const eventData = {
                    event_type: 'interaction',
                    event_name: 'click',
                    element_path: this.getElementPath(element),
                    element_type: element.tagName.toLowerCase(),
                    element_id: element.id || null,
                    element_class: element.className || null,
                    element_text: this.getTruncatedText(element.textContent, 100),
                    coordinates: { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY }
                };
                
                this.captureEvent(eventData);
            }, { capture: true });
            
            // Captura de submits de formulário
            document.addEventListener('submit', (e) => {
                if (Math.random() > this.SAMPLE_RATE) return;
                
                const form = e.target;
                const eventData = {
                    event_type: 'form',
                    event_name: 'submit',
                    element_path: this.getElementPath(form),
                    element_id: form.id || null,
                    form_name: form.getAttribute('name') || null,
                    field_count: form.elements.length
                };
                
                this.captureEvent(eventData);
            });
            
            // Captura de mudanças em campos importantes
            document.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                if (Math.random() > this.SAMPLE_RATE) return;
                
                const element = e.target;
                if (['INPUT', 'SELECT', 'TEXTAREA'].includes(element.tagName)) {
                    const eventData = {
                        event_type: 'form',
                        event_name: 'change',
                        element_path: this.getElementPath(element),
                        element_type: element.tagName.toLowerCase(),
                        element_id: element.id || null,
                        field_name: element.name || element.id || null,
                        field_type: element.type || 'text',
                        field_value_length: element.value ? element.value.length : 0
                    };
                    
                    this.captureEvent(eventData);
                }
            });
            
            // Captura de navegação SPA (se aplicável)
            if (window.history && window.history.pushState) {
                const originalPushState = history.pushState;
                history.pushState = function(state, title, url) {
                    originalPushState.apply(history, arguments);
                    DIYAPP_EVENTS.capturePageView();
                };
                
                window.addEventListener('popstate', () => {
                    DIYAPP_EVENTS.capturePageView();
                });
            }
        },
        
        // Rastreia atividade do usuário para sessão
        setupActivityTracker: function() {
            const activityEvents = ['mousemove', 'keydown', 'scroll', 'click', 'touchstart'];
            
            activityEvents.forEach(eventName => {
                document.addEventListener(eventName, () => {
                    this.lastActivityTime = Date.now();
                }, { passive: true });
            });
            
            // Verifica timeout da sessão a cada minuto
            setInterval(() => {
                const inactiveTime = Date.now() - this.lastActivityTime;
                if (inactiveTime > this.SESSION_TIMEOUT) {
                    this.endSession();
                    this.generateSessionId();
                    this.capturePageView();
                }
            }, 60000);
        },
        
        // Captura erros do JavaScript
        setupErrorHandling: function() {
            // Erros globais
            window.addEventListener('error', (e) => {
                const errorData = {
                    event_type: 'error',
                    event_name: 'javascript_error',
                    error_message: e.message,
                    error_type: e.type,
                    filename: e.filename,
                    line_number: e.lineno,
                    column_number: e.colno,
                    stack_trace: e.error ? e.error.stack : null
                };
                
                this.captureEvent(errorData);
            });
            
            // Promise rejections não tratadas
            window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', (e) => {
                const errorData = {
                    event_type: 'error',
                    event_name: 'promise_rejection',
                    error_message: e.reason ? e.reason.toString() : 'Unknown promise rejection',
                    stack_trace: e.reason ? e.reason.stack : null
                };
                
                this.captureEvent(errorData);
            });
            
            // Monitora chamadas AJAX/fetch (opcional)
            if (window.XMLHttpRequest) {
                const originalOpen = XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open;
                const originalSend = XMLHttpRequest.prototype.send;
                
                XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open = function(method, url) {
                    this._diystartTime = Date.now();
                    this._diymethod = method;
                    this._diyurl = url;
                    return originalOpen.apply(this, arguments);
                };
                
                XMLHttpRequest.prototype.send = function(body) {
                    this.addEventListener('loadend', function() {
                        if (this.status >= 400) {
                            const duration = Date.now() - this._diystartTime;
                            DIYAPP_EVENTS.captureEvent({
                                event_type: 'api',
                                event_name: 'request_error',
                                api_method: this._diymethod,
                                api_url: this._diyurl,
                                status_code: this.status,
                                duration_ms: duration,
                                response_size: this.responseText ? this.responseText.length : 0
                            });
                        }
                    });
                    
                    return originalSend.apply(this, arguments);
                };
            }
        },
        
        // Captura visualização de página
        capturePageView: function() {
            const eventData = {
                event_type: 'navigation',
                event_name: 'page_view',
                page_title: document.title,
                referrer: document.referrer,
                performance: this.getPerformanceMetrics()
            };
            
            this.captureEvent(eventData);
        },
        
        // Método principal para capturar eventos
        captureEvent: function(eventData) {
            const event = {
                event_id: 'evt_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9),
                session_id: this.sessionId,
                user_id: this.userId,
                timestamp: Date.now(),
                page_url: window.location.href,
                page_title: document.title,
                viewport_width: window.innerWidth,
                viewport_height: window.innerHeight,
                user_agent: navigator.userAgent,
                language: navigator.language,
                timezone_offset: new Date().getTimezoneOffset(),
                ...eventData
            };
            
            // Adiciona ao buffer
            this.eventBuffer.push(event);
            
            // Flush se buffer cheio
            if (this.eventBuffer.length >= this.maxBufferSize) {
                this.flushEvents();
            }
            
            // Atualiza contador de eventos na sessão
            this.updateSessionEventCount();
            
            return event.event_id;
        },
        
        // Envia eventos em batch para o servidor
        flushEvents: function() {
            if (this.eventBuffer.length === 0 || navigator.sendBeacon) return;
            
            const eventsToSend = [...this.eventBuffer];
            this.eventBuffer = [];
            
            // Usa sendBeacon se disponível (não bloqueante)
            if (navigator.sendBeacon) {
                const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify({ events: eventsToSend })], 
                    { type: 'application/json' });
                navigator.sendBeacon(this.ENDPOINT, blob);
            } else {
                // Fallback para fetch
                fetch(this.ENDPOINT, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ events: eventsToSend }),
                    keepalive: true // Mantém a requisição mesmo após navegação
                }).catch(error => {
                    console.warn('Failed to send events:', error);
                    // Recoloca eventos no buffer para retry
                    this.eventBuffer = [...eventsToSend, ...this.eventBuffer];
                });
            }
        },
        
        // Inicia intervalo para flush periódico
        startFlushInterval: function() {
            setInterval(() => {
                if (this.eventBuffer.length > 0) {
                    this.flushEvents();
                }
            }, this.flushInterval);
        },
        
        // Finaliza sessão atual
        endSession: function() {
            const sessionDuration = Date.now() - this.sessionStartTime;
            
            this.captureEvent({
                event_type: 'session',
                event_name: 'session_end',
                session_duration_ms: sessionDuration
            });
            
            // Envia eventos pendentes
            this.flushEvents();
        },
        
        // Utilitários
        getElementPath: function(element) {
            const path = [];
            let current = element;
            
            while (current && current !== document.body) {
                let selector = current.tagName.toLowerCase();
                
                if (current.id) {
                    selector += '#' + current.id;
                } else if (current.className && typeof current.className === 'string') {
                    const classes = current.className.split(' ').filter(c => c).join('.');
                    if (classes) selector += '.' + classes;
                }
                
                path.unshift(selector);
                current = current.parentNode;
            }
            
            return path.join(' > ');
        },
        
        getTruncatedText: function(text, maxLength) {
            if (!text) return null;
            text = text.trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
            return text.length > maxLength ? text.substr(0, maxLength) + '...' : text;
        },
        
        getPerformanceMetrics: function() {
            if (!window.performance || !window.performance.timing) return null;
            
            const perf = window.performance.timing;
            const navStart = perf.navigationStart;
            
            return {
                dns_lookup: perf.domainLookupEnd - perf.domainLookupStart,
                tcp_connect: perf.connectEnd - perf.connectStart,
                request_response: perf.responseEnd - perf.requestStart,
                dom_interactive: perf.domInteractive - navStart,
                dom_complete: perf.domComplete - navStart,
                load_event: perf.loadEventEnd - navStart,
                first_paint: window.performance.getEntriesByName('first-paint')[0]?.startTime,
                first_contentful_paint: window.performance.getEntriesByName('first-contentful-paint')[0]?.startTime
            };
        },
        
        getCookie: function(name) {
            const value = `; ${document.cookie}`;
            const parts = value.split(`; ${name}=`);
            if (parts.length === 2) return parts.pop().split(';').shift();
            return null;
        },
        
        updateSessionEventCount: function() {
            // Implementação simplificada - em produção, enviaria para servidor
            const sessionData = localStorage.getItem('diyapp_session') || '{}';
            const session = JSON.parse(sessionData);
            session.eventCount = (session.eventCount || 0) + 1;
            localStorage.setItem('diyapp_session', JSON.stringify(session));
        },
        
        // API pública para outras partes da aplicação
        setUserId: function(userId) {
            this.userId = userId;
            localStorage.setItem

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Mecanismo de Auto-Healing

Vou implementar um sistema completo de auto-healing baseado em métricas SRE com reinicialização automática, escalonamento horizontal e rollback automático.

```yaml
# docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  app:
    build: .
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - AUTO_HEALING_ENABLED=true
      - METRICS_PORT=9090
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    deploy:
      replicas: 2
      update_config:
        parallelism: 1
        delay: 10s
        order: start-first
        failure_action: rollback
        monitor: 60s
      rollback_config:
        parallelism: 1
        delay: 10s
        order: stop-first
      restart_policy:
        condition: any
        delay: 5s
        max_attempts: 3
        window: 120s

```javascript
// autohealing/src/index.js
const express = require('express');
const Docker = require('dockerode');
const axios = require('axios');
const winston = require('winston');
const { PrometheusMetrics } = require('./metrics');
const { AutoHealingEngine } = require('./engine');
const { HealthCheckManager } = require('./healthcheck');

class AutoHealingSystem {
  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.docker = new Docker();
    this.metrics = new PrometheusMetrics();
    this.engine = new AutoHealingEngine(this.docker, this.metrics);
    this.healthManager = new HealthCheckManager(this.docker);
    
    this.setupMiddleware();
    this.setupRoutes();
    this.startMonitoring();
  }

  setupMiddleware() {
    this.app.use(express.json());
    this.app.use((req, res, next) => {
      winston.info(`${req.method} ${req.url}`);
      next();
    });
  }

  setupRoutes() {
    this.app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
      res.json({ status: 'healthy', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() });
    });

    this.app.get('/metrics', async (req, res) => {
      const metrics = await this.metrics.getMetrics();
      res.set('Content-Type', 'text/plain');
      res.send(metrics);
    });

    this.app.get('/status', async (req, res) => {
      const status = await this.engine.getStatus();
      res.json(status);
    });

    this.app.post('/webhook/alert', async (req, res) => {
      const alert = req.body;
      await this.engine.handleAlert(alert);
      res.json({ received: true });
    });

    this.app.post('/scale/:service', async (req, res) => {
      const { service } = req.params;
      const { replicas } = req.body;
      
      try {
        await this.engine.scaleService(service, replicas);
        res.json({ success: true, service, replicas });
      } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
      }
    });

    this.app.post('/restart/:containerId', async (req, res) => {
      const { containerId } = req.params;
      
      try {
        await this.engine.restartContainer(containerId);
        res.json({ success: true, containerId });
      } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
      }
    });

    this.app.post('/rollback/:service', async (req, res) => {
      const { service } = req.params;
      
      try {
        await this.engine.rollbackService(service);
        res.json({ success: true, service });
      } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
      }
    });
  }

  async startMonitoring() {
    // Monitor health checks
    setInterval(async () => {
      await this.healthManager.checkAllServices();
    }, 30000); // Every 30 seconds

    // Monitor metrics and auto-scale
    setInterval(async () => {
      await this.engine.autoScaleBasedOnMetrics();
    }, 60000); // Every minute

    // Clean up old containers
    setInterval(async () => {
      await this.engine.cleanupOldContainers();
    }, 3600000); // Every hour
  }

  start(port = 8080) {
    this.app.listen(port, () => {
      winston.info(`Auto-healing system started on port ${port}`);
    });
  }
}

// Initialize and start
const autoHealingSystem = new AutoHealingSystem();
autoHealingSystem.start(8080);
```

```javascript
// autohealing/src/engine.js
const winston = require('winston');
const axios = require('axios');

class AutoHealingEngine {
  constructor(docker, metrics) {
    this.docker = docker;
    this.metrics = metrics;
    this.services = new Map();
    this.alertHistory = [];
    this.scalingPolicies = new Map();
    
    this.initScalingPolicies();
  }

  initScalingPolicies() {
    // Define auto-scaling policies
    this.scalingPolicies.set('app', {
      minReplicas: 2,
      maxReplicas: 10,
      targetCpu: 70, // 70% CPU usage
      targetMemory: 80, // 80% memory usage
      targetLatency: 5000, // 5 seconds
      scaleUpThreshold: 85, // Scale up at 85% utilization
      scaleDownThreshold: 30, // Scale down at 30% utilization
      cooldownPeriod: 300000 // 5 minutes cooldown
    });
  }

  async handleAlert(alert) {
    const { status, labels, annotations } = alert;
    const alertName = labels.alertname;
    const service = labels.service || 'unknown';
    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();

    winston.info(`Received alert: ${alertName} for service: ${service}`, {
      status,
      labels,
      annotations
    });

    this.alertHistory.push({
      timestamp,
      alertName,
      service,
      status,
      labels,
      annotations
    });

    // Keep only last 100 alerts
    if (this.alertHistory.length > 100) {
      this.alertHistory.shift();
    }

    // Take action based on alert type
    switch (alertName) {
      case 'HighLatency':
        await this.handleHighLatency(service, labels, annotations);
        break;
      case 'HighErrorRate':
        await this.handleHighErrorRate(service, labels, annotations);
        break;
      case 'ContainerDown':
        await this.handleContainerDown(service, labels, annotations);
        break;
      case 'HighMemoryUsage':
        await this.handleHighMemoryUsage(service, labels, annotations);
        break;
      case 'HealthCheckFailed':
        await this.handleHealthCheckFailed(service, labels, annotations);
        break;
      default:
        winston.warn(`Unknown alert type: ${alertName}`);
    }
  }

  async handleHighLatency(service, labels, annotations) {
    const policy = this.scalingPolicies.get(service);
    if (!policy) return;

    // Check if we're in cooldown period
    if (this.isInCooldown(service)) {
      winston.info(`Service ${service} is in cooldown period, skipping scale-up`);
      return;
    }

    // Get current replicas
    const currentReplicas = await this.getServiceReplicas(service);
    
    if (currentReplicas < policy.maxReplicas) {
      const newReplicas = Math.min(currentReplicas + 1, policy.maxReplicas);
      winston.info(`Scaling up ${service} from ${currentReplicas} to ${newReplicas} due to high latency`);
      await this.scaleService(service, newReplicas);
      this.setCooldown(service);
    }
  }

  async handleContainerDown(service, labels, annotations) {
    const containerId = labels.container_id;
    if (containerId) {
      winston.info(`Restarting container ${containerId} for service ${service}`);
      await this.restartContainer(containerId);
    }
  }

  async handleHealthCheckFailed(service, labels, annotations) {
    // If health check fails multiple times, trigger rollback
    const failedCount = this.countRecentAlerts(service, 'HealthCheckFailed', 300000); // Last 5 minutes
    
    if (failedCount >= 3) {
      winston.warn(`Multiple health check failures for ${service}, triggering rollback`);
      await this.rollbackService(service);
    }
  }

  async autoScaleBasedOnMetrics() {
    for (const [service, policy] of this.scalingPolicies) {
      try {
        const metrics = await this.metrics.getServiceMetrics(service);
        
        if (!metrics) continue;

        const currentReplicas = await this.getServiceReplicas(service);
        let desiredReplicas = currentReplicas;

        // Scale up logic
        if (metrics.cpuUsage > policy.scaleUpThreshold ||
            metrics.memoryUsage > policy.scaleUpThreshold ||
            metrics.latencyP95 > policy.targetLatency) {
          
          if (!this.isInCooldown(service) && currentReplicas < policy.maxReplicas) {
            desiredReplicas = Math.min(currentReplicas + 1, policy.maxReplicas);
          }
        }
        // Scale down logic
        else if (metrics.cpuUsage < policy.scaleDownThreshold &&
                 metrics.memoryUsage < policy.scaleDownThreshold &&
                 currentReplicas > policy.minReplicas) {
          
          if (!this.isInCooldown(service)) {
            desiredReplicas = Math.max(currentReplicas - 1, policy.minReplicas);
          }
        }

        if (desiredReplicas !== currentReplicas) {
          winston.info(`Auto-scaling ${service} from ${currentReplicas} to ${desiredReplicas}`, {
            cpuUsage: metrics.cpuUsage,
            memoryUsage: metrics.memoryUsage,
            latency: metrics.latencyP95
          });
          
          await this.scaleService(service, desiredReplicas);
          this.setCooldown(service);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        winston.error(`Error auto-scaling ${service}:`, error);
      }
    }
  }

  async scaleService(service, replicas) {
    try {
      // In production, this would use Docker Swarm or Kubernetes API
      // For Docker Compose, we can use the Docker API
      const containers = await this.docker.listContainers({
        filters: { label: [`com.docker.compose.service=${service}`] }
      });

      const currentCount = containers.length;
      
      if (replicas > currentCount) {
        // Scale up - start new containers
        for (let i = currentCount; i < replicas; i++) {
          await this.startNewContainer(service);
        }
      } else if (replicas < currentCount) {
        // Scale down - stop excess containers
        const toRemove = currentCount - replicas;
        for (let i = 0; i < toRemove; i++) {
          if (containers[i]) {
            const container = this.docker.getContainer(containers[i].Id);
            await container.stop();
            await container.remove();
          }
        }
      }

      winston.info(`Scaled service ${service} to ${replicas} replicas`);
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      winston.error(`Error scaling service ${service}:`, error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async restartContainer(containerId) {
    try {
      const container = this.docker.getContainer(containerId);
      
      // Check if container exists
      const info = await container.inspect();
      
      if (info.State.Running) {
        await container.restart();
        winston.info(`Restarted container ${containerId}`);
      } else {
        await container.start();
        winston.info(`Started container ${containerId}`);
      }
      
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      winston.error(`Error restarting container ${containerId}:`, error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async rollbackService(service) {
    try {
      winston.warn(`Initiating rollback for service ${service}`);
      
      // In a real implementation, this would:
      // 1. Check for previous version tag/image
      // 2. Update service to use previous version
      // 3. Verify health checks pass
      // 4. Notify team about rollback
      
      // For now, we'll just restart all containers for the service
      const containers = await this.docker.listContainers({
        filters: { label: [`com.docker.compose.service=${service}`] }
      });

      for (const containerInfo of containers) {
        const container = this.docker.getContainer(containerInfo.Id);
        await container.restart();
      }

      winston.info(`Rollback completed for service ${service}`);
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      winston.error(`Error rolling back service ${service}:`, error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async startNewContainer(service) {
    // This is a simplified version
    // In production, you would use Docker Compose or Docker API to start services
    winston.info(`Starting new container for service ${service}`);
    // Implementation depends on your orchestration setup
  }

  async getServiceReplicas(service) {
    try {
      const containers = await this.docker.listContainers({
        filters: { label: [`com.docker.compose.service=${service}`] },
        all: true
      });
      
      const runningContainers = containers.filter(c => c.State === 'running');
      return runningContainers.length;
    } catch (error) {
      winston.error(`Error getting replicas for ${service}:`, error);
      return 0;
    }
  }

  isInCooldown(service) {
    const lastAction = this.services.get(`${service}_last_action`);
    if (!lastAction) return false;
    
    const policy = this.scalingPolicies.get(service);
    const cooldownEnd = lastAction + policy.cooldownPeriod;
    
    return Date.now() < cooldownEnd;
  }

  setCooldown(service) {
    this.services.set(`${service}_last_action`, Date.now());
  }

  countRecentAlerts(service, alertName, timeWindow) {
    const now = Date.now();
    const cutoff = now - timeWindow;
    
    return this.alertHistory.filter(alert => 
      alert.service === service &&
      alert.alertName === alertName &&
      new Date(alert.timestamp).getTime() > cutoff
    ).length;
  }

  async getStatus() {
    const status = {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      services: {},
      recentAlerts: this.alertHistory.slice(-10),
      scalingPolicies: Object.fromEntries(this.scalingPolicies)
    };

    // Get status for each service with scaling policy
    for (const [service] of this.scalingPolicies) {
      const replicas = await this.getServiceReplicas(service);
      const inCooldown = this.isInCooldown(service);
      
      status.services[service] = {
        replicas,
        inCooldown,
        cooldownEnd: inCooldown ? 
          this.services.get(`${service}_last_action`) + 
          this.scalingPolicies.get(service).cooldownPeriod : null
      };
    }

    return status;
  }

  async cleanupOldContainers() {
    try {
      const containers = await this.docker.listContainers({
        all: true,
        filters: { status: ['exited', 'dead'] }
      });

      for (const containerInfo of containers) {
        // Remove containers older than 24 hours
        const created = new Date(containerInfo.Created

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V13 Core - Pentest e Hardening de Segurança

## 1. Análise de Threat Modeling (STRIDE) da V13

### Ativos Críticos Identificados:
1. **API REST** - `/api/*` endpoints
2. **WebSocket** - Comunicação em tempo real
3. **Upload de arquivos** - `/upload` endpoint
4. **Autenticação** - JWT tokens, sessões
5. **Banco de dados** - SQLite/PostgreSQL
6. **LLM Integration** - OpenAI/Anthropic endpoints
7. **Webhooks** - Integrações externas

## 2. Implementação de Rate Limiting

```javascript
// src/security/rateLimiter.js
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const { RateLimiterRedis, RateLimiterMemory } = require('rate-limiter-flexible');

class SecurityRateLimiter {
    constructor() {
        this.redisClient = new Redis({
            host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
            port: process.env.REDIS_PORT || 6379,
            enableOfflineQueue: false
        });
        
        this.setupLimiters();
    }
    
    setupLimiters() {
        // Limiter global para API
        this.apiLimiter = rateLimit({
            windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
            max: 100, // limite por IP
            message: {
                error: 'Muitas requisições. Tente novamente em 15 minutos.',
                code: 'RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED'
            },
            standardHeaders: true,
            legacyHeaders: false,
            skipSuccessfulRequests: false,
            keyGenerator: (req) => {
                // Usa IP + user agent para melhor identificação
                return `${req.ip}-${req.headers['user-agent']}`;
            }
        });
        
        // Limiter específico para autenticação
        this.authLimiter = rateLimit({
            windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hora
            max: 5, // 5 tentativas por hora
            message: {
                error: 'Muitas tentativas de login. Tente novamente em 1 hora.',
                code: 'AUTH_RATE_LIMIT'
            },
            skipSuccessfulRequests: true
        });
        
        // Limiter para uploads
        this.uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
            windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hora
            max: 10, // 10 uploads por hora
            message: {
                error: 'Limite de uploads excedido. Tente novamente em 1 hora.',
                code: 'UPLOAD_LIMIT_EXCEEDED'
            }
        });
        
        // Rate limiter para WebSocket (usando Redis)
        this.wsRateLimiter = new RateLimiterRedis({
            storeClient: this.redisClient,
            keyPrefix: 'ws_ratelimit',
            points: 50, // 50 mensagens
            duration: 10, // por 10 segundos
            blockDuration: 60 // bloquear por 60 segundos se exceder
        });
        
        // Rate limiter para LLM API calls
        this.llmRateLimiter = new RateLimiterRedis({
            storeClient: this.redisClient,
            keyPrefix: 'llm_ratelimit',
            points: 30, // 30 requisições
            duration: 60, // por minuto
            blockDuration: 300 // 5 minutos de bloqueio
        });
    }
    
    // Middleware para WebSocket rate limiting
    async wsRateLimitMiddleware(socket, next) {
        try {
            const clientId = socket.handshake.address;
            await this.wsRateLimiter.consume(clientId, 1);
            next();
        } catch (rejRes) {
            socket.emit('error', {
                type: 'RATE_LIMIT',
                message: 'Limite de mensagens excedido',
                retryAfter: Math.ceil(rejRes.msBeforeNext / 1000)
            });
            socket.disconnect(true);
        }
    }
    
    // Middleware para LLM API rate limiting
    async llmRateLimitMiddleware(req, res, next) {
        try {
            const key = req.user?.id || req.ip;
            await this.llmRateLimiter.consume(key, 1);
            next();
        } catch (rejRes) {
            res.status(429).json({
                error: 'Limite de requisições para LLM excedido',
                retryAfter: Math.ceil(rejRes.msBeforeNext / 1000),
                code: 'LLM_RATE_LIMIT'
            });
        }
    }
    
    // Cleanup
    async cleanup() {
        await this.redisClient.quit();
    }
}

module.exports = SecurityRateLimiter;
```

## 3. Web Application Firewall (WAF) Rules

```javascript
// src/security/waf.js
const helmet = require('helmet');
const xss = require('xss-clean');
const hpp = require('hpp');
const mongoSanitize = require('express-mongo-sanitize');
const validator = require('validator');

class WebApplicationFirewall {
    constructor() {
        this.blockedIPs = new Set();
        this.suspiciousPatterns = [
            /<script\b[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/script>/gi,
            /javascript:/gi,
            /on\w+\s*=/gi,
            /union\s+select/gi,
            /select.*from/gi,
            /insert\s+into/gi,
            /update\s+\w+\s+set/gi,
            /delete\s+from/gi,
            /drop\s+table/gi,
            /exec(\s|\+)+(s|x)p\w+/gi,
            /\.\.\/\.\.\//gi,
            /\.\.\\\.\.\\/gi,
            /\/etc\/passwd/gi,
            /\/bin\/sh/gi,
            /<\?php/gi,
            /eval\s*\(/gi,
            /document\.cookie/gi,
            /alert\s*\(/gi,
            /console\.log/gi
        ];
        
        this.setupWAF();
    }
    
    setupWAF() {
        // Configuração do Helmet com políticas específicas
        this.helmetConfig = helmet({
            contentSecurityPolicy: {
                directives: {
                    defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
                    styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", "https:"],
                    scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", "'unsafe-eval'"],
                    imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
                    connectSrc: ["'self'", "https://api.openai.com", "https://api.anthropic.com"],
                    fontSrc: ["'self'", "https:", "data:"],
                    objectSrc: ["'none'"],
                    mediaSrc: ["'self'"],
                    frameSrc: ["'none'"]
                }
            },
            hsts: {
                maxAge: 31536000,
                includeSubDomains: true,
                preload: true
            },
            referrerPolicy: { policy: 'strict-origin-when-cross-origin' },
            frameguard: { action: 'deny' },
            noSniff: true,
            xssFilter: true
        });
        
        // Lista de user agents maliciosos conhecidos
        this.maliciousUserAgents = [
            'sqlmap', 'nikto', 'nmap', 'metasploit', 'hydra',
            'dirbuster', 'gobuster', 'wfuzz', 'ffuf', 'burpsuite',
            'zap', 'w3af', 'nessus', 'openvas', 'acunetix'
        ];
    }
    
    // Middleware principal do WAF
    wafMiddleware() {
        return [
            this.helmetConfig,
            xss(),
            hpp(),
            mongoSanitize(),
            this.requestScanner.bind(this),
            this.inputValidator.bind(this)
        ];
    }
    
    // Scanner de requisições
    async requestScanner(req, res, next) {
        const ip = req.ip;
        const userAgent = req.headers['user-agent'] || '';
        
        // Verifica IP bloqueado
        if (this.blockedIPs.has(ip)) {
            this.logSecurityEvent('BLOCKED_IP', { ip, path: req.path });
            return res.status(403).json({
                error: 'Acesso bloqueado por segurança',
                code: 'IP_BLOCKED'
            });
        }
        
        // Verifica user agent malicioso
        const isMaliciousUA = this.maliciousUserAgents.some(ua => 
            userAgent.toLowerCase().includes(ua.toLowerCase())
        );
        
        if (isMaliciousUA) {
            this.blockedIPs.add(ip);
            this.logSecurityEvent('MALICIOUS_UA', { ip, userAgent });
            return res.status(403).json({
                error: 'Acesso bloqueado por segurança',
                code: 'MALICIOUS_UA_DETECTED'
            });
        }
        
        // Scanner de payloads maliciosos
        const payload = JSON.stringify(req.body) + JSON.stringify(req.query) + JSON.stringify(req.params);
        
        for (const pattern of this.suspiciousPatterns) {
            if (pattern.test(payload)) {
                this.blockedIPs.add(ip);
                this.logSecurityEvent('MALICIOUS_PAYLOAD', {
                    ip,
                    pattern: pattern.toString(),
                    path: req.path
                });
                
                return res.status(403).json({
                    error: 'Payload malicioso detectado',
                    code: 'MALICIOUS_PAYLOAD'
                });
            }
        }
        
        next();
    }
    
    // Validador de input
    inputValidator(req, res, next) {
        // Sanitização de strings
        const sanitizeString = (str) => {
            if (typeof str !== 'string') return str;
            
            // Remove null bytes
            str = str.replace(/\0/g, '');
            
            // Remove caracteres de controle
            str = str.replace(/[\x00-\x1F\x7F-\x9F]/g, '');
            
            // Trim excessivo
            str = str.trim();
            
            return str;
        };
        
        // Validação de email
        if (req.body.email) {
            if (!validator.isEmail(req.body.email)) {
                return res.status(400).json({
                    error: 'Email inválido',
                    code: 'INVALID_EMAIL'
                });
            }
            req.body.email = validator.normalizeEmail(req.body.email);
        }
        
        // Validação de URL
        if (req.body.url) {
            if (!validator.isURL(req.body.url, {
                protocols: ['http', 'https'],
                require_protocol: true,
                require_valid_protocol: true
            })) {
                return res.status(400).json({
                    error: 'URL inválida',
                    code: 'INVALID_URL'
                });
            }
        }
        
        // Sanitização recursiva
        const sanitizeObject = (obj) => {
            if (typeof obj === 'string') {
                return sanitizeString(obj);
            }
            
            if (Array.isArray(obj)) {
                return obj.map(sanitizeObject);
            }
            
            if (obj && typeof obj === 'object') {
                const sanitized = {};
                for (const key in obj) {
                    sanitized[key] = sanitizeObject(obj[key]);
                }
                return sanitized;
            }
            
            return obj;
        };
        
        req.body = sanitizeObject(req.body);
        req.query = sanitizeObject(req.query);
        req.params = sanitizeObject(req.params);
        
        next();
    }
    
    // Log de eventos de segurança
    logSecurityEvent(event, data) {
        const logEntry = {
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            event,
            data,
            severity: this.getEventSeverity(event)
        };
        
        console.warn('[SECURITY EVENT]', JSON.stringify(logEntry));
        
        // Aqui você pode enviar para um SIEM, Elasticsearch, etc.
        // Exemplo: this.sendToSIEM(logEntry);
    }
    
    getEventSeverity(event) {
        const severityMap = {
            'BLOCKED_IP': 'MEDIUM',
            'MALICIOUS_UA': 'HIGH',
            'MALICIOUS_PAYLOAD': 'CRITICAL',
            'SQL_INJECTION_ATTEMPT': 'CRITICAL',
            'XSS_ATTEMPT': 'HIGH',
            'RATE_LIMIT_BYPASS': 'MEDIUM'
        };
        
        return severityMap[event] || 'LOW';
    }
    
    // Método para adicionar IP à whitelist (apenas para testes)
    addToWhitelist(ip) {
        this.blockedIPs.delete(ip);
    }
    
    // Método para limpar IPs bloqueados temporários
    cleanupBlockedIPs() {
        // Implementar lógica para limpar IPs após X tempo
        // Por enquanto, mantém em memória
    }
}

module.exports = WebApplicationFirewall;
```

## 4. Proteção contra OWASP Top 10

```javascript
// src/security/owaspProtection.js
const crypto = require('crypto');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');

class OWASPProtection {
    constructor() {
        this.saltRounds = 12;
        this.jwtSecret = process.env.JWT_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
        this.csrfTokens = new Map();
    }
    
    // A1:2021 - Broken Access Control
    setupAccessControl() {
        return {
            // Middleware para verificação de autorização
            authorize: (requiredRoles = []) => {
                return (req, res, next) => {
                    if (!req.user) {
                        return res.status(401).json({
                            error: 'Não autorizado',
                            code: 'UNAUTHORIZED'
                        });
                    }
                    
                    if (requiredRoles.length > 0) {
                        const hasRole = requiredRoles.some(role => 
                            req.user.roles.includes(role)
                        );
                        
                        if (!hasRole) {
                            return res.status(403).json({
                                error: 'Permissão insuficiente',
                                code: 'FORBIDDEN'
                            });
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Verificação de IDOR (Insecure Direct Object Reference)
                    if (req.params.userId && req.params.userId !== req.user.id) {
                        // Verifica se o usuário tem acesso ao recurso
                        if (!req.user.isAdmin && req.params.userId !== req.user.id) {
                            return res.status(403).json({
                                error: 'Acesso não autorizado ao recurso',
                                code: 'IDOR_PROTECTION'
                            });
                        }
                    }
                    
                    next();
                };
            },
            
            // RBAC (Role-Based Access Control)
            roles: {
                ADMIN: ['admin'],
                USER: ['user'],
                READONLY: ['readonly']
            }
        };
    }
    
    // A2:2021 - Cryptographic Failures
    setupCryptography() {
        return {
            // Hash de senha com bcrypt
            hashPassword: async (password) => {
                if (password.length < 8) {
                    throw new Error('Senha muito curta');
                }
                
                const salt = await bcrypt.genSalt(this.saltRounds);
                return await bcrypt.hash(password, salt);
            },
            
            // Verificação de senha
            verifyPassword: async (password, hash) => {
                return await bcrypt.compare(password, hash);
            },
            
            // Criptografia de dados sensíveis
            encryptData: (data, key = this.jwtSecret) => {
                const iv = crypto.randomBytes(16);
                const cipher = crypto.createCipheriv('aes-256-gcm', 
                    crypto.createHash('sha256').update(key).digest(), 
                    iv
                );
                
                let encrypted = cipher.update(data, 'utf8', 'hex');
                encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
                const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
                
                return {
                    iv: iv.toString('hex'),
                    encrypted,
                    authTag: authTag.toString('hex')
                };
            },
            
            // Decriptografia
            decryptData: (encryptedData, key = this.jwtSecret) => {
                const decipher = crypto.createDecipheriv('aes-256-gcm',
                    crypto.createHash('sha256').update(key).digest(),
                    Buffer.from(encryptedData.iv, 'hex')
                );
                
                decipher.setAuthTag(Buffer.from(encryptedData.authTag, 'hex'));
                
                let decrypted = decipher.update(encryptedData.encrypted, 'hex', 'utf8');
                decrypted += decipher.final('utf8');
                
                return decrypted;
            },
            
            // Geração de JWT seguro
            generateJWT: (payload, expiresIn = '15m') => {
                return jwt.sign(payload, this.jwtSecret, {
                    expiresIn,
                    algorithm: 'HS256',
                    issuer: 'diyapp-v13',
                    audience: 'diyapp-users'
                });
            },
            
            // Verificação de JWT
            verifyJWT: (token) => {
                try {
                    return jwt.verify(token, this.jwtSecret, {
                        algorithms: ['HS256'],
                        issuer: 'diyapp-v13',
                        audience: 'diyapp-users'
                    });
                } catch (error) {
                    throw new Error('Token inválido ou expirado');
                }
            }
        };
    }
    
    // A3:2021 - Injection
    setupInjectionProtection() {
        return {
            // Sanitização de SQL
            sanitizeSQL: (query, params) => {
                // Implementação usando prepared statements
                // Exemplo com PostgreSQL
                return {
                    text: query,
                    values: params
                };
            },
            
            // Validação de NoSQL injection
            sanitizeNoSQL: (input) => {
                const dangerousOperators = ['$where', '$regex', '$function', '$code'];

## 1. Sistema de Gestão de Consentimento e Base Legal

### `src/compliance/consent_manager.py`

```python
"""
Sistema de Gestão de Consentimento LGPD/GDPR
Gerencia bases legais, consentimentos e preferências de usuários
"""
import json
import hashlib
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from enum import Enum
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
import sqlite3
from contextlib import contextmanager
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class LegalBasis(Enum):
    """Bases legais conforme LGPD Art. 7 e GDPR Art. 6"""
    CONSENT = "consent"
    CONTRACT = "contract"
    LEGAL_OBLIGATION = "legal_obligation"
    VITAL_INTERESTS = "vital_interests"
    PUBLIC_INTEREST = "public_interest"
    LEGITIMATE_INTEREST = "legitimate_interest"

@dataclass
class ConsentRecord:
    """Registro de consentimento granular"""
    consent_id: str
    data_subject_id: str
    processing_activity: str
    legal_basis: LegalBasis
    purposes: List[str]
    data_categories: List[str]
    granted_at: datetime
    expires_at: Optional[datetime]
    version: str
    consent_text_hash: str
    withdrawal_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = None
    
    def is_valid(self) -> bool:
        """Verifica se o consentimento está válido"""
        now = datetime.utcnow()
        if self.withdrawal_at and self.withdrawal_at <= now:
            return False
        if self.expires_at and self.expires_at <= now:
            return False
        return True

class ConsentManager:
    """Gerencia consentimentos e bases legais"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_path: str = "database/compliance.db"):
        self.db_path = db_path
        self._init_database()
    
    def _init_database(self):
        """Inicializa tabelas do banco de dados"""
        with self._get_connection() as conn:
            conn.execute("""
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS consent_records (
                    consent_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    data_subject_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                    processing_activity TEXT NOT NULL,
                    legal_basis TEXT NOT NULL,
                    purposes TEXT NOT NULL,
                    data_categories TEXT NOT NULL,
                    granted_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
                    expires_at TIMESTAMP,
                    version TEXT NOT NULL,
                    consent_text_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
                    withdrawal_at TIMESTAMP,
                    metadata TEXT,
                    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
                    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                )
            """)
            
            conn.execute("""
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS legal_basis_mapping (
                    processing_activity TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    legal_basis TEXT NOT NULL,
                    legitimate_interest_assessment TEXT,
                    data_minimization_check BOOLEAN DEFAULT 1,
                    retention_period_days INTEGER,
                    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                )
            """)
            
            conn.execute("""
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS consent_audit_log (
                    log_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                    consent_id TEXT,
                    action TEXT NOT NULL,
                    action_by TEXT,
                    old_state TEXT,
                    new_state TEXT,
                    ip_address TEXT,
                    user_agent TEXT,
                    timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                )
            """)
    
    @contextmanager
    def _get_connection(self):
        """Context manager para conexão com banco de dados"""
        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)
        conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
        try:
            yield conn
            conn.commit()
        except Exception as e:
            conn.rollback()
            logger.error(f"Database error: {e}")
            raise
        finally:
            conn.close()
    
    def register_legal_basis(self, processing_activity: str, legal_basis: LegalBasis,
                           legitimate_interest_assessment: Optional[str] = None,
                           retention_period_days: Optional[int] = None) -> bool:
        """Registra base legal para uma atividade de processamento"""
        try:
            with self._get_connection() as conn:
                conn.execute("""
                    INSERT OR REPLACE INTO legal_basis_mapping 
                    (processing_activity, legal_basis, legitimate_interest_assessment, retention_period_days)
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
                """, (
                    processing_activity,
                    legal_basis.value,
                    legitimate_interest_assessment,
                    retention_period_days
                ))
            
            logger.info(f"Legal basis registered for {processing_activity}: {legal_basis.value}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to register legal basis: {e}")
            return False
    
    def obtain_consent(self, data_subject_id: str, processing_activity: str,
                      purposes: List[str], data_categories: List[str],
                      consent_text: str, expires_in_days: Optional[int] = 365) -> Optional[ConsentRecord]:
        """Obtém e registra consentimento granular"""
        try:
            # Verifica se há base legal válida
            legal_basis = self._get_legal_basis(processing_activity)
            if legal_basis != LegalBasis.CONSENT:
                logger.warning(f"Processing activity {processing_activity} doesn't require consent")
                return None
            
            # Gera hash do texto de consentimento
            consent_hash = hashlib.sha256(consent_text.encode()).hexdigest()
            
            # Cria registro de consentimento
            consent_id = f"CONS-{hashlib.md5(f'{data_subject_id}{processing_activity}{datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}'.encode()).hexdigest()[:12]}"
            
            expires_at = None
            if expires_in_days:
                expires_at = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=expires_in_days)
            
            consent_record = ConsentRecord(
                consent_id=consent_id,
                data_subject_id=data_subject_id,
                processing_activity=processing_activity,
                legal_basis=legal_basis,
                purposes=purposes,
                data_categories=data_categories,
                granted_at=datetime.utcnow(),
                expires_at=expires_at,
                version="1.0",
                consent_text_hash=consent_hash
            )
            
            # Salva no banco de dados
            with self._get_connection() as conn:
                conn.execute("""
                    INSERT INTO consent_records 
                    (consent_id, data_subject_id, processing_activity, legal_basis, 
                     purposes, data_categories, granted_at, expires_at, version, consent_text_hash)
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                """, (
                    consent_record.consent_id,
                    consent_record.data_subject_id,
                    consent_record.processing_activity,
                    consent_record.legal_basis.value,
                    json.dumps(consent_record.purposes),
                    json.dumps(consent_record.data_categories),
                    consent_record.granted_at.isoformat(),
                    consent_record.expires_at.isoformat() if consent_record.expires_at else None,
                    consent_record.version,
                    consent_record.consent_text_hash
                ))
                
                # Log de auditoria
                conn.execute("""
                    INSERT INTO consent_audit_log (consent_id, action, old_state, new_state)
                    VALUES (?, 'GRANTED', NULL, ?)
                """, (consent_id, json.dumps(asdict(consent_record))))
            
            logger.info(f"Consent obtained: {consent_id} for {data_subject_id}")
            return consent_record
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to obtain consent: {e}")
            return None
    
    def withdraw_consent(self, consent_id: str, data_subject_id: str) -> bool:
        """Revoga consentimento"""
        try:
            with self._get_connection() as conn:
                # Verifica se o consentimento existe e pertence ao titular
                cursor = conn.execute("""
                    SELECT * FROM consent_records 
                    WHERE consent_id = ? AND data_subject_id = ? AND withdrawal_at IS NULL
                """, (consent_id, data_subject_id))
                
                record = cursor.fetchone()
                if not record:
                    logger.warning(f"Consent not found or already withdrawn: {consent_id}")
                    return False
                
                # Atualiza registro
                withdrawal_time = datetime.utcnow()
                conn.execute("""
                    UPDATE consent_records 
                    SET withdrawal_at = ?, updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                    WHERE consent_id = ?
                """, (withdrawal_time.isoformat(), consent_id))
                
                # Log de auditoria
                conn.execute("""
                    INSERT INTO consent_audit_log (consent_id, action, old_state, new_state)
                    VALUES (?, 'WITHDRAWN', ?, ?)
                """, (consent_id, json.dumps(dict(record)), json.dumps({"withdrawal_at": withdrawal_time.isoformat()})))
            
            logger.info(f"Consent withdrawn: {consent_id}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to withdraw consent: {e}")
            return False
    
    def validate_processing(self, processing_activity: str, data_categories: List[str],
                          data_subject_id: Optional[str] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Valida se o processamento está em conformidade"""
        try:
            with self._get_connection() as conn:
                # Obtém base legal
                cursor = conn.execute("""
                    SELECT * FROM legal_basis_mapping 
                    WHERE processing_activity = ?
                """, (processing_activity,))
                
                basis_record = cursor.fetchone()
                if not basis_record:
                    return {
                        "valid": False,
                        "reason": f"No legal basis registered for {processing_activity}",
                        "legal_basis": None
                    }
                
                legal_basis = LegalBasis(basis_record["legal_basis"])
                
                # Validações específicas por base legal
                if legal_basis == LegalBasis.CONSENT:
                    if not data_subject_id:
                        return {
                            "valid": False,
                            "reason": "Data subject ID required for consent-based processing",
                            "legal_basis": legal_basis.value
                        }
                    
                    # Verifica consentimento válido
                    cursor = conn.execute("""
                        SELECT * FROM consent_records 
                        WHERE data_subject_id = ? 
                        AND processing_activity = ?
                        AND withdrawal_at IS NULL
                        AND (expires_at IS NULL OR expires_at > CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
                    """, (data_subject_id, processing_activity))
                    
                    consent_record = cursor.fetchone()
                    if not consent_record:
                        return {
                            "valid": False,
                            "reason": "No valid consent found",
                            "legal_basis": legal_basis.value
                        }
                
                elif legal_basis == LegalBasis.LEGITIMATE_INTEREST:
                    if not basis_record["legitimate_interest_assessment"]:
                        return {
                            "valid": False,
                            "reason": "Legitimate interest assessment required",
                            "legal_basis": legal_basis.value
                        }
                
                # Verifica minimização de dados
                if basis_record["data_minimization_check"]:
                    # Implementar lógica de verificação de minimização
                    pass
                
                return {
                    "valid": True,
                    "legal_basis": legal_basis.value,
                    "retention_period_days": basis_record["retention_period_days"],
                    "requires_consent": legal_basis == LegalBasis.CONSENT
                }
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Validation error: {e}")
            return {
                "valid": False,
                "reason": f"Validation error: {str(e)}",
                "legal_basis": None
            }
    
    def _get_legal_basis(self, processing_activity: str) -> Optional[LegalBasis]:
        """Obtém base legal para uma atividade"""
        try:
            with self._get_connection() as conn:
                cursor = conn.execute("""
                    SELECT legal_basis FROM legal_basis_mapping 
                    WHERE processing_activity = ?
                """, (processing_activity,))
                
                record = cursor.fetchone()
                if record:
                    return LegalBasis(record["legal_basis"])
                return None
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to get legal basis: {e}")
            return None
    
    def get_data_subject_consents(self, data_subject_id: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Obtém todos os consentimentos de um titular"""
        try:
            with self._get_connection() as conn:
                cursor = conn.execute("""
                    SELECT * FROM consent_records 
                    WHERE data_subject_id = ?
                    ORDER BY granted_at DESC
                """, (data_subject_id,))
                
                records = []
                for row in cursor.fetchall():
                    record = dict(row)
                    record["is_valid"] = self._is_consent_valid(row)
                    records.append(record)
                
                return records
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to get consents: {e}")
            return []
    
    def _is_consent_valid(self, consent_record) -> bool:
        """Verifica se um consentimento está válido"""
        try:
            withdrawal_at = consent_record["withdrawal_at"]
            expires_at = consent_record["expires_at"]
            now = datetime.utcnow()
            
            if withdrawal_at:
                withdrawal_time = datetime.fromisoformat(withdrawal_at)
                if withdrawal_time <= now:
                    return False
            
            if expires_at:
                expire_time = datetime.fromisoformat(expires_at)
                if expire_time <= now:
                    return False
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error checking consent validity: {e}")
            return False
```

## 2. Sistema de Captura de Dados em Conformidade

### `src/data_engineer/data_capture.py`

```python
"""
Sistema de captura de dados em conformidade com LGPD/GDPR
Implementa privacy by design e data minimization
"""
import json
import hashlib
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional, Tuple
import logging
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
import uuid
from enum import Enum

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class DataCategory(Enum):
    """Categorias de dados pessoais conforme LGPD"""
    IDENTIFICATION = "identification"
    CONTACT = "contact"
    FINANCIAL = "financial"
    LOCATION = "location"
    BEHAVIORAL = "behavioral"
    TECHNICAL = "technical"
    SENSITIVE = "sensitive"  # Dados sensíveis conforme LGPD Art. 5º II
    ANONYMIZED = "anonymized"

@dataclass
class DataCaptureConfig:
    """Configuração de captura de dados"""
    processing_activity: str
    legal_basis: str
    purposes: List[str]
    retention_days: int
    anonymize_after_days: Optional[int] = None
    encryption_required: bool = True
    access_logging: bool = True

class CompliantDataCapture:
    """Captura de dados com privacy by design"""
    
    def __init__(self, consent_manager, db_path: str = "database/compliance.db"):
        self.consent_manager = consent_manager
        self.db_path = db_path
        self._init_database()
    
    def _init_database(self):
        """Inicializa tabelas de captura de dados"""
        import sqlite3
        from contextlib import contextmanager
        
        @contextmanager
        def get_connection():
            conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)
            conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
            try:
                yield conn
                conn.commit()
            except Exception as e:
                conn.rollback()
                logger.error(f"Database error: {e}")
                raise
            finally:
                conn.close()
        
        with get_connection() as conn:
            # Tabela de dados pessoais
            conn.execute("""
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS personal_data (
                    data_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    data_subject_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                    data_category TEXT NOT NULL,
                    data_field TEXT NOT NULL,
                    data_value TEXT NOT NULL,
                    processing_activity TEXT

### [Sessão Paralela: QA]
```javascript
// k6-load-test.js - Testes de carga para validar SLOs sob estresse
import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep, group } from 'k6';
import { Rate, Trend, Counter } from 'k6/metrics';

// Configuração
export const options = {
  stages: [
    { duration: '1m', target: 50 },  // Ramp-up
    { duration: '3m', target: 100 }, // Carga normal
    { duration: '2m', target: 200 }, // Pico de carga
    { duration: '1m', target: 50 },  // Ramp-down
  ],
  thresholds: {
    'http_req_duration': ['p(95)<500'],  // 95% das requisições < 500ms
    'http_req_failed': ['rate<0.01'],    // Taxa de erro < 1%
    'checks': ['rate>0.99'],             // Checks > 99%
  },
};

// Métricas customizadas
const errorRate = new Rate('errors');
const requestDuration = new Trend('request_duration');
const successfulRequests = new Counter('successful_requests');

// Variáveis de ambiente
const BASE_URL = __ENV.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000';
const API_KEY = __ENV.API_KEY || 'test-key';

// Headers comuns
const headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'Authorization': `Bearer ${API_KEY}`,
  'X-Request-ID': 'k6-test-${__VU}-${__ITER}',
};

// Payloads de teste
const createUserPayload = {
  email: `testuser_${__VU}_${Date.now()}@test.com`,
  name: `Test User ${__VU}`,
  plan: 'premium',
};

const createProjectPayload = {
  name: `Project ${__VU}-${__ITER}`,
  description: 'Load test project',
  complexity: 'medium',
};

// Funções auxiliares
function logError(resource, error) {
  console.error(`[${__VU}:${__ITER}] ${resource} failed:`, error);
}

// Cenários de teste
export default function () {
  group('API - Fluxos Básicos', () => {
    // Teste: Health Check
    const healthRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/health`, { headers });
    check(healthRes, {
      'health check status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'health check response time < 100ms': (r) => r.timings.duration < 100,
    });
    
    // Teste: Autenticação
    const authRes = http.post(
      `${BASE_URL}/api/auth/login`,
      JSON.stringify({ email: 'loadtest@example.com', password: 'test123' }),
      { headers }
    );
    check(authRes, {
      'auth status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'auth returns token': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).token !== undefined,
    });
    
    let token = null;
    if (authRes.status === 200) {
      token = JSON.parse(authRes.body).token;
    }
    
    // Headers autenticados
    const authHeaders = { ...headers, 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` };
    
    // Teste: Listar projetos
    const listRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/projects`, { headers: authHeaders });
    check(listRes, {
      'list projects status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'list projects returns array': (r) => Array.isArray(JSON.parse(r.body)),
    });
    
    // Teste: Criar projeto
    const createRes = http.post(
      `${BASE_URL}/api/projects`,
      JSON.stringify(createProjectPayload),
      { headers: authHeaders }
    );
    check(createRes, {
      'create project status 201': (r) => r.status === 201,
      'create project returns id': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).id !== undefined,
    });
    
    let projectId = null;
    if (createRes.status === 201) {
      projectId = JSON.parse(createRes.body).id;
    }
    
    // Teste: Operações no projeto (se criado com sucesso)
    if (projectId) {
      // Ler projeto
      const readRes = http.get(
        `${BASE_URL}/api/projects/${projectId}`,
        { headers: authHeaders }
      );
      check(readRes, {
        'read project status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
        'read project returns correct id': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).id === projectId,
      });
      
      // Atualizar projeto
      const updateRes = http.put(
        `${BASE_URL}/api/projects/${projectId}`,
        JSON.stringify({ ...createProjectPayload, name: 'Updated Project' }),
        { headers: authHeaders }
      );
      check(updateRes, {
        'update project status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
      });
      
      // Deletar projeto
      const deleteRes = http.del(
        `${BASE_URL}/api/projects/${projectId}`,
        null,
        { headers: authHeaders }
      );
      check(deleteRes, {
        'delete project status 204': (r) => r.status === 204,
      });
    }
    
    // Atualizar métricas
    const allChecks = [healthRes, authRes, listRes, createRes];
    const allSuccessful = allChecks.every(res => res.status >= 200 && res.status < 300);
    
    if (allSuccessful) {
      successfulRequests.add(1);
    } else {
      errorRate.add(1);
    }
    
    requestDuration.add(healthRes.timings.duration);
  });
  
  group('API - Fluxos Premium (UX Avançado)', () => {
    // Teste: Upload de arquivo grande
    const fileData = 'A'.repeat(1024 * 1024); // 1MB
    const uploadRes = http.post(
      `${BASE_URL}/api/uploads`,
      fileData,
      { headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'application/octet-stream' } }
    );
    check(uploadRes, {
      'upload status 202': (r) => r.status === 202,
      'upload returns processing id': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).processingId !== undefined,
    });
    
    // Teste: Processamento assíncrono
    if (uploadRes.status === 202) {
      const processingId = JSON.parse(uploadRes.body).processingId;
      sleep(1); // Aguarda processamento
      
      const statusRes = http.get(
        `${BASE_URL}/api/uploads/${processingId}/status`,
        { headers }
      );
      check(statusRes, {
        'status check returns valid state': (r) => ['processing', 'completed', 'failed'].includes(JSON.parse(r.body).state),
      });
    }
    
    // Teste: WebSocket connection (simulado via HTTP)
    const wsRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/ws/connect`, { headers });
    check(wsRes, {
      'websocket endpoint available': (r) => r.status === 200 || r.status === 101,
    });
    
    // Teste: Analytics batch
    const analyticsPayload = {
      events: Array.from({ length: 100 }, (_, i) => ({
        type: 'click',
        timestamp: Date.now() + i,
        data: { element: `button-${i}` }
      }))
    };
    
    const analyticsRes = http.post(
      `${BASE_URL}/api/analytics/batch`,
      JSON.stringify(analyticsPayload),
      { headers }
    );
    check(analyticsRes, {
      'analytics batch status 202': (r) => r.status === 202,
    });
  });
  
  group('API - Cenários de Falha e Resiliência', () => {
    // Teste: Request com timeout curto
    const timeoutRes = http.get(
      `${BASE_URL}/api/slow-operation`,
      { headers, timeout: '1000' } // 1 segundo timeout
    );
    check(timeoutRes, {
      'timeout handled gracefully': (r) => r.status !== 0 || r.error_code === 'ETIMEDOUT',
    });
    
    // Teste: Payload malformado
    const malformedRes = http.post(
      `${BASE_URL}/api/projects`,
      '{ invalid json }',
      { headers }
    );
    check(malformedRes, {
      'malformed json returns 400': (r) => r.status === 400,
    });
    
    // Teste: Rate limiting
    for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
      const rateLimitRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/rate-test`, { headers });
      if (rateLimitRes.status === 429) {
        check(rateLimitRes, {
          'rate limit returns 429': (r) => r.status === 429,
          'rate limit includes retry-after': (r) => r.headers['Retry-After'] !== undefined,
        });
        break;
      }
      sleep(0.1);
    }
    
    // Teste: Serviço dependente offline
    const dependencyRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/external-service`, { headers });
    check(dependencyRes, {
      'dependency failure handled': (r) => r.status === 200 || r.status === 503,
    });
  });
  
  // Pausa entre iterações
  sleep(Math.random() * 2);
}

// Função de setup (executada uma vez antes dos testes)
export function setup() {
  console.log('Starting load test with base URL:', BASE_URL);
  
  // Verifica se o serviço está disponível
  const healthCheck = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/health`);
  if (healthCheck.status !== 200) {
    throw new Error(`Service not available at ${BASE_URL}`);
  }
  
  return { startTime: new Date().toISOString() };
}

// Função de teardown (executada após os testes)
export function teardown(data) {
  console.log('Load test completed at:', new Date().toISOString());
  console.log('Test started at:', data.startTime);
}
